 anādi ānanda kūṭa stha jñāna ananta sadātmane abhūta dvaita jālāya sākṣiṇe brahmaṇe namaḥ namaḥ śruti śiraḥ padma ṣaṇḍa mārtaṇḍa mūrtaye bādarāyaṇa saṃjñāya munaye śama veśmane namāmi abhogi parivāra sampadam nirasta bhūti manumārdha vigraham anugram unmṛdita kāla lāñchanam vinā vināyakam apūrva śaṅkaram yad vaktra mānasa saraḥ pratilabdha janma bhāṣya aravinda makaranda rasam pibanti pratyāśam unmukha vinīta vineya bhṛṅgāḥ tān bhāṣya vittaka gurūn praṇamāmi mūrdhnā pada ādi vṛnta bhāreṇa garimāṇam bibharti yad  bhāṣyam prasanna gambhīram tad vyākhyām śraddhayā ārabhe ayuṣmad asmad pratyaya gocarayoḥ ityādi ‘aham idam mama idam iti naisargikaḥ ayam loka vyavahāraḥ iti antam bhāṣyam ‘asya anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāya ātmā ekatva vidyā pratipattaye sarve vedāntā ārabhyante iti anena bhāṣyeṇa paryavasyat  śāstrasya viṣayaḥ prayojanam ca arthāt  prathama sūtreṇa sūtrite iti pratipādayati etad ca ‘tasmāt  brahma jijñāsitavyam ityādi bhāṣye spaṣṭataram pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ atra āha yadi evam etāvat eva astu bhāṣyam ‘asya anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāya ātmā ekatva vidyā pratipattaye sarve vedāntā ārabhyante iti tatra ‘anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāya iti prayojana nirdeśaḥ ‘a ātmā ekatva vidyā pratipattaye iti viṣaya pradarśanam kim anena ‘yuṣmad asmad ityādinā ‘aham manuṣyaḥ iti deha indriya ādiṣu aham mama idam iti abhimāna ātmakasya loka vyavahārasya avidyā nirmitatva pradarśana pareṇa bhāṣyeṇa ucyate brahma jñānam hi sūtritam anartha hetu nibarhaṇam anarthaḥ ca pramātṛ tā pramukham kartṛtva bhoktṛ tvam tad  yadi vastu kṛtam na jñānena nibarhaṇīyam yatas  jñānam ajñānasya eva nivartakam tad  yadi kartṛtva bhoktṛ tvam ajñāna hetukam syāt  tatas  brahma jñānam anartha hetu nibarhaṇam ucyamānam upapadyeta tena sūtrakāreṇa eva brahma jñānam anartha hetu nibarhaṇam sūcayatā avidyā hetukam kartṛtva bhoktṛ tvam pradarśitam bhavati atas  tad pradarśana dvāreṇa sūtra artha upapatti upayogi tayā sakala tantra upodghātaḥ prayojanam asya bhāṣyasya tathā ca asya śāstrasya aidamparyam sukha eka tāna sat ātmaka kūṭa stha caitanya eka rasa tā saṃsāritva abhimatasya ātmanaḥ pāramārthikam svarūpam iti vedāntāḥ paryavasyanti iti pratipāditam tad ca aham kartā sukhī duḥkhī iti pratyakṣa abhimatena abādhita kalpena avabhāsena virudhyate atas  tad virodha parihāra artham brahma svarūpa viparīta rūpam avidyā nirmitam ātmana iti yāvat  na pratipādyate tāvat  jarat gava ādi vākyavat anarthakam pratibhāti atas  tad nivṛtti artham avidyā vilasitam abrahma svarūpa tvam ātmana iti pratipādayitavyam vakṣyati ca etad  avirodha lakṣaṇe jīva prakriyāyām sūtra kāraḥ ‘tad guṇa sāra tvāt ityādinā yadi evam etad eva prathama m astu mā evam artha viśeṣa upapatteḥ artha viśeṣe hi samanvaye pradarśite tad viredha āśaṅkāyām tad nirākaraṇam upapadyate apradarśite punar  samanvaya viśeṣe tad virodha āśaṅkā tad nirākaraṇam ca nirviṣayam syāt  bhāṣya kāraḥ tu tad siddham eva ādi sūtreṇa sāmarthya balena sūcitam sukha pratipatti artham varṇayati iti na doṣaḥ nanu ca grantha karaṇa ādi kārya ārambhe kārya anurūpam iṣṭadevatā pūjā namaskāreṇa buddhi sannidhā pitātha vṛddhi ādi śabdaiḥ dadhi ādi darśanena vā kṛta maṅgalāḥ śiṣṭāḥ pravartante śiṣṭa ācāraḥ ca naḥ pramāṇam prasiddham ca maṅgala ācaraṇasya vighna upaśamanam prayojanam mahati ca niḥśreyasa prayojane grantham ārabhamāṇasya vighna bāhulyam sambhāvyate prasiddham ca `śreyāṃsi bahu vighnāni iti vijñāyate ca atasmāt eṣām tad na priyam yad etad manuṣyā vidyuḥ iti yeṣām ca yad na priyam te tad vighnanti iti prasiddham loke tad  katham ullaṅghya śiṣṭa ācāram akṛta maṅgala eva visrabdham bhāṣya kāraḥ pravavṛte atra ucyate ayuṣmad asmad ityādi `tad dharmāṇām api sutarām itaretara bhāva anupapattiḥ iti antam eva bhāṣyam asya ca ayam arthaḥ sarva upaplava rahitaḥ  vijñāna ghanaḥ pratyagarthaḥ iti tad  kathañcana paramārthataḥ evambhūte vastuni rūpa antaravat avabhāsaḥ mithyā iti kathayitum tad anya parāt eva bhāṣya vākyāt  nirasta samasta upaplavam caitanya eka tānam ātmānam pratipadyamānasya kutaḥ vighna upaplava sambhavaḥ tasmāt  agraṇīḥ śiṣṭa ācāra paripālane bhagavān bhāṣya kāraḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ tamaḥ prakāśavat viruddha svabhāvayoḥ itaretara bhāva anupapattau siddhāyām iti kaḥ ayam virodhaḥ kīdṛśaḥ  vā itaretara bhāvaḥ abhipretaḥ yasya anupapatteḥ atamaḥ prakāśavat iti nidarśanam yadi tāvat  saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ  virodhaḥ tatas  prakāśa bhāve tamasaḥ  bhāva anupapattiḥ tad asat  dṛśyate hi manda pradīpe veśmani aspaṣṭam rūpa darśanam itaratra ca spaṣṭam tena jñāyate manda pradīpe veśmani tamasaḥ api īṣat anuvṛttiḥ iti tathā chāyāyām api auṣṇyam tāratamyena upalabhyamānam ātapasya api tatra avasthānam sūcayati etena śīta uṣṇayoḥ api yugapad upalabdheḥ saha avasthānam uktam veditavyam ucyate parasparān ātma tā lakṣaṇaḥ  virodhaḥ na jāti vyaktyoḥ iva paramārthataḥ paraspara sambhedaḥ sambhavati iti arthaḥ tena itaretara bhāvasya itaretara sambheda ātmaka tvasya anupapattiḥ katham svatas tāvat  viṣayiṇaḥ cit eka rasa tvāt  na yuṣmad aṃśa sambhavaḥ apariṇāmi tvāt  nirañjana tvāt ca na paratas  viṣayasya api na svatas  cit sambhavaḥ sama tvāt  viṣayatva hāneḥ na paratas  citeḥ apratisaṅkrama tvāt  tad dharmāṇām api sutarām iti evam sthite sva āśrayam atiricya dharmāṇām anyatra bhāva anupapattiḥ su prasiddhā iti darśayati iti śabdaḥ  hetu arthaḥ yasmāt  evam uktena nyāyena itaretara bhāva asambhavaḥ atas  asmad pratyaya gocare viṣayiṇi cit ātmake iti asmad pratyaye yaḥ anidam aṃśaḥ cit eka rasaḥ tasmin tad bala nirbhāsita tayā lakṣaṇataḥ  yuṣmad arthasya manuṣya abhimānasya sambheda iva avabhāsaḥ sa eva adhyāsaḥ tad dharmāṇām ca iti yadi api viṣaya adhyāse tad dharmāṇām api artha siddhaḥ adhyāsaḥ tathā api vinā api viṣaya adhyāsena tad dharma adhyāsaḥ  bādhirya ādiṣu śrotra ādi dharmeṣu vidyate iti pṛthak  dharma grahaṇam tad viparyayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ tad dharmāṇām ca iti caitanyasya tad dharmāṇām ca iti arthaḥ nanu viṣayiṇaḥ cit eka rasasya kutaḥ dharmāḥ ye viṣaye adhyasyeran ucyate ānandaḥ  viṣaya anubhavaḥ  nitya tvam iti santi dharmāḥ apṛthaktve api caitanyāt  pṛthak iva avabhāsante iti na doṣaḥ adhyāsaḥ  nāma atad rūpe tad rūpa avabhāsaḥ saḥ mithyā iti bhavitum yuktam iti mithyā śabdaḥ  dvi arthaḥ apahnava vacanaḥ anirvacanīya tā vacanaḥ ca atra ayam apahnava vacanaḥ mithyā iti bhavitum yuktam abhāva eva adhyāsasya yuktaḥ iti arthaḥ yadi api evam tathā api naisargikaḥ pratyak caitanya sattā trāmā anubandhī ayam yuṣmad asmadoḥ itaretara adhyāsa ātmakaḥ aham idam mama ida m iti loka vyavahāraḥ tena yathā asmad arthasya sadbhāvaḥ  na upālambham arhati evam adhyāsasya api iti abhiprāyaḥ loka iti manuṣyaḥ aham iti abhimanyamānaḥ prāṇi nikāyaḥ ucyate vyavaharaṇam vyavahāraḥ loka iti vyavahāraḥ  loka vyavahāraḥ manuṣyaḥ aham iti abhimānaḥ iti arthaḥ satya anṛte mithunīkṛtya iti satyam anidam caitanyam anṛtam yuṣmad arthaḥ svarūpataḥ api adhyasta svarūpa tvāt ‘adhyasya ‘mithunīkṛtya iti ca ktvā apratyayaḥ na pūrva kāla tvam anya tvam ca loka vyavahārāt aṅgīkṛtya prayuktaḥ bhuktvā vrajati itivat  kriyā antara anupādānāt ‘adhyasya naisargikaḥ ayam loka vyavahāraḥ iti sva rūpa mātra paryavasānāt upasaṃhāre ca ‘evam ayam anādiḥ anantaḥ  naisargikaḥ adhyāsaḥ iti tāvat mātra upasaṃhārāt  atas  caitanyam puruṣasya svarūpam itivat  vyapadeśa mātram draṣṭavyam mithyājñāna nimittaḥ iti mithyā ca tad ajñānam ca mithyājñānam mithyā iti anirvacanīya tā ucyate ajñānam iti ca jaḍa ātmikā avidyā śaktiḥ jñāna paryudāsena ucyate tad nimittaḥ tad upādānaḥ iti arthaḥ katham punar  naimittaka vyavahārasya naisargika tvam atra ucyate avaśyam eṣā avidyā śaktiḥ bāhya ādhyātmikeṣu vastuṣu tad svarūpa sattā mātra anubandhinī abhyupagantavyā anyathā mithyā artha avabhāsa anupapatteḥ sā ca na jaḍeṣu vastuṣu tad svarūpa avabhāsam pratibadhnāti pramāṇa vaikalyāt eva tad agrahaṇa siddheḥ rajata pratibhāsāt  prāk  ūrdhvam ca satyām api tasyām svarūpa grahaṇa darśanāt  atas  tatra rūpa antara avabhāsa hetuḥ eva kevalam pratyagātmani tu citi svabhāva tvāt  svayam prakāśa māne brahma svarūpa anavabhāsasya ananya nimitta tvāt  tad gata nisarga siddha avidyā śakti pratibandhāt eva tasya anavabhāsaḥ atas  sā pratyakciti brahma svarūpa avabhāsam pratibadhnāti ahaṅkāra ādya tad rūpa pratibhāsa nimittam ca bhavati suṣupti ādau ca ahaṅkāra ādi vikṣepa saṃskāra mātra śeṣam sthitvā punar udbhavati iti atas  naisargikaḥ api ahaṅkāram amakāra ātmakaḥ  manuṣya ādi abhimānaḥ  loka vyavahāraḥ mithyājñāna nimittaḥ ucyate na punar  āgantuka tvena tena naisargika tvam naimittika tvena na virudhyate ‘anyonya dharmān  ca iti pṛthak  dharma grahaṇam dharma mātrasya api kasyacid adhyāsa iti darśayitum itaretarauvivekena iti eka tā āpattyā eva iti arthaḥ kasya dharmiṇaḥ katham kutra ca adhyāsaḥ dharma mātrasya vā kva adhyāsaḥ iti bhāṣya kāraḥ svayam eva vakṣyati ‘aham idam mama idam iti adhyāsasya svarūpam darśayati aham iti tāvat  prathamaḥ adhyāsaḥ nanu aham iti niraṃśam caitanya mātram pratibhāsate na aṃśa antaram adhyastam vā yathā adhyasta aṃśa antarbhāvaḥ tathā darśayiṣyāmaḥ nanu idam iti ahaṅkartuḥ bhoga sādhanam kārya karaṇa saṅghātaḥ avabhāsate mama idam iti ca ahaṅkartrā sva tvena tasya sambandhaḥ tatra na kiñcid  adhyastam iva dṛśyate ucyate yadā eva ahaṅkartā adhyāsa ātmakaḥ tadā eva tad upakaraṇasya api tad ātmakatva siddhiḥ na hi svapna avāpta rājya abhiṣekasya māhendra jāla nirmitasya vā rājñaḥ rājya upakaraṇam paramārtha sat  bhavati evam ahaṅkartṛtva pramukhaḥ kriyā kāraka phala ātmakaḥ  loka vyavahāraḥ adhyastaḥ nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāve ātmani atas  tādṛś brahma ātma anubhava paryantāt jñānāt  anartha hetoḥ adhyāsasya nivṛttiḥ upapadyate iti tad artha viṣaya vedāntamī māṃsa ārambhaḥ upapadyate āha kaḥ ayam adhyāsaḥ  nāma iti ādi ārabhya adhyāsa siddhi param bhāṣyam tatra api akatham punar avidyāvat viṣayāṇi iti atas  prāk  adhyāsa svarūpa tad sambhāvanāya tad ādi tad sadbhāva nirṇaya artham iti vibhāgaḥ yadi evam tad svarūpa tad sambhāvana upanyāsaḥ pṛthak  na kartavyaḥ na hi anirjñāta rūpam asambhāvyamānam ca nirṇīyate ca iti duḥsampādam viśeṣataḥ adhyakṣa anubhava nirṇaye ucyate na deha indriya ādiṣu ahaṃmama abhimānavata eva pramātṛtva pradarśana mātreṇa tasya adhyāsa ātmaka tā sidhyati tad  kasya hetoḥ loke śukti rajatadvi candra ādivat  adhyāsa anubhava abhāvāt bādhe hi sati sa bhavati na iha sa vidyate tasmāt  adhyāsasya lakṣaṇam abhidhāya tad lakṣaṇa vyāptasya sadbhāvaḥ kathanīyaḥ nanu evam api tad lakṣaṇasya vastunaḥ sadbhāva mātram iha kathanīyam na hi yatra yasya sadbhāvaḥ pramāṇataḥ pratipannaḥ tatra eva tasya asambhāvanā āśaṅkā yena tad vinivṛttaye tad sambhāvanā aparā kathyeta satyam evam viṣaya viśeṣaḥ tu prayatnena anvicchadbhiḥ api anupalabhyamāna kāraṇa doṣe vijñāne avabhāsamānaḥ api pūrva pravṛttena sakala loka vyāpinā niścitena pramāṇena asambhāvyamāna tayā apodyamānaḥ  dṛśyate tad yathā autpātikaḥ savitari suṣiḥ yathā vā māhendra jāla kuśalena prāsāda ādeḥ nigaraṇam evam aviṣaye asaṅge kenacid api guṇa ādinā adhyāsa hetunā rahite niṣkalaṅka caitanya tayā anya gatasya api adhyāsasya apanodana samarthe adhyāsa avagamaḥ avibhāvyamāna kāraṇa doṣaḥ vibhramaḥ iti āśaṅkyeta tad  mā śaṅki iti sadbhāva atirekeṇa sambhavaḥ api pṛthak  kathanīyaḥ tad ucyate  āha kaḥ ayam adhyāsaḥ  nāma  iti kiṃvṛttasya praśne ākṣepe ca prayoga darśanāt  ubhayasya ca iha sambhavāt  tantreṇa vākyam uccaritam tatra api prathamam praśnasya prativacanam svarūpam ākhyāya punar  tasya eva sambhavam ākṣipya pratividhatte tatra evaṃbhūte viṣaye śrotṝṇām sukha prabodha artham vyācakṣāṇāḥ prativādinam tatrastham iva samutthāpya tena ākṣiptam anena pṛṣṭam iti matvā pratyuktam punar asau sva abhiprāyam vivṛṇoti iti ākṣepam avatārya pratividhānam pratipadyante sarvatra evaṃvidhe grantha sanniveśe eṣa eva vyākhyā prakāraḥ ‘smṛti rūpaḥ paratra pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ iti praśna vākya sthitam adhyāsam uddiśya lakṣaṇam abhidhīyate tatra paratra iti ukte arthāt  parasya avabhāsamāna tā siddhā tasya viśeṣaṇam smṛti rūpa tvam smaryate iti smṛtiḥ asaṃjñāyām api akartari kārake ghañā ādīnām prayoga darśanāt  smaryamāṇa rūpam iva rūpam asya na punar  smaryate eva spaṣṭam puras avasthitatva avabhāsanāt  pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ iti upapattiḥ smṛti rūpa tve na hi pūrvam adṛṣṭa rajatasya śukti samprayoge rajatam avabhāsate yatas arthāt  tad viṣayasya avabhāsasya api idam eva lakṣaṇam uktam bhavati katham tad ucyate smṛteḥ rūpam iva rūpam asya na punar  smṛtiḥ eva pūrva pramāṇa viṣaya viśeṣasya tathā anavabhāsaka tvāt  katham punar  smṛti rūpa tvam pūrva pramāṇa dvāra samuttha tvāt na hi asamprayukta avabhāsinaḥ pūrva pravṛtta tad viṣaya pramāṇa dvāra samuttha tvam antareṇa samudbhavaḥ sambhavati apara āha nanu anya samprayukte cakṣuṣi anya viṣaya jñānam smṛtiḥ eva pramoṣaḥ tu smaraṇa abhimānasya indriya ādīnām jñāna kāraṇānām kenacid eva doṣa viśeṣeṇa kasyacid eva artha viśeṣasya smṛti samudbodhaḥ kriyate samprayuktasya ca doṣeṇa viśeṣa pratibhāsa hetu tvam karaṇasya vihanyate tena darśana smaraṇayoḥ nirantara utpannayoḥ karaṇa doṣāt eva viveka anavadhāraṇāt  dūra sthayoḥ iva vanaspatyoḥ anutpanne eva ekatva avabhāse utpanna bhramaḥ nanu anāsvādita tikta rasasya api bālakasya pitta doṣāt  madhure tikta avabhāsaḥ katham smaraṇam syāt  ucyate janma antara anubhūta tvāt anyathā ananubhūtatva aviśeṣe atyantam asan  eva kaścid  saptamaḥ  rasaḥ kim iti na avabhāseta tasmāt  pittam eva madhura agrahaṇe tikta smṛtau tad pramoṣe ca hetuḥ kārya gamya tvāt hetu bhāvasya etena anya samprayoge anya viṣayasya jñānasya smṛtitva tad pramoṣau sarvatra vyākhyātau draṣṭavyau ucyate kaḥ ayam smaraṇa abhimānaḥ  nāma na tāvat  jñāna anuviddha tayā grahaṇam na hi ativṛttasya jñānasya grāhya viśeṣaṇa tayā viṣaya bhāvaḥ tasmāt  śuddham eva artham smṛtiḥ avabhāsayati na jñāna anuviddham tathā ca padāt  padārthasmṛtau na dṛṣṭaḥ  jñāna sambhedaḥ jñānasya api śabda arthatva prasaṅgāt  tathā iṣṭa bhū bhāga viṣaya asmṛtiḥ ‘sa sevyaḥ iti grāhya mātra sthā na jñāna parāmarśinī api ca bhūyasyaḥ jñāna parāmarśa śūnyā eva smṛtayaḥ na api sva gataḥ  jñānasya smaraṇa abhimānaḥ  nāma rūpa bhedaḥ avabhāsate na hi nitya anumeyam jñānam anyat vā vastu svata eva rūpa sambhinnam gṛhyate ata eva uktam ‘anākārām eva buddhim anumimīmahe iti anākārām anirūpita ākāra viśeṣām anirdiṣṭa sva lakṣaṇām iti arthaḥ atas  na svatas  smaraṇa abhimāna ātmaka tā na api grāhya viśeṣa nimittaḥ smaraṇa abhimānaḥ pramāṇa grāhyasya eva avikalān adhikasya gṛhyamāṇa tvāt  na api phala viśeṣa nimittaḥ pramāṇa phala viṣaya mātra avacchinna phala tvāt yaḥ punar  kvacid  kadācid  anubhūta care ‘smarāmi iti anuvedhaḥ saḥ vācaka śabda saṃyojanā nimittaḥ yathā sāsnādi mada ākṛtau gauḥ iti abhimānaḥ tasmāt  pūrva pramāṇa saṃskāra samuttha tayā tad viṣaya avabhāsitva mātram smṛteḥ na punar  pratītitaḥ arthataḥ  vā adhikoṃśaḥ asti yasya doṣa nimittaḥ pramoṣaḥ parikalpyeta na ca iha pūrva pramāṇa viṣaya avabhāsi tvam asti puras avasthita artha pratibhāsanāt iti uktam atas  na anya samprayoge anya viṣaya jñānam smṛtiḥ kintu adhyāsaḥ nanu evam sati vaiparītyam āpadyate rajatam avabhāsate śuktiḥ ālambanam iti na etad  saṃvid anusāriṇām anurūpam nanu śukteḥ sva rūpeṇa api avabhāsane saṃvid prayukta vyavahāra yogya tvam eva ālambana arthaḥ sā eva idānīm rajata vyavahāra yogyā pratibhāsate tatra kim iti ālambanam na syāt  atha tathārūpa avabhāsanam śukteḥ pāramārthikam uta ahaḥ na yadi pāramārthikam na idam rajatam iti bādhaḥ  na syāt  na iyam śuktiḥ iti yathā bhavati ca bādhaḥ tasmāt  na eṣa pakṣaḥ pramāṇavān atha śukteḥ eva doṣa nimittaḥ  rajata rūpaḥ pariṇāma ucyate etad api asāram na hi kṣīra pariṇāme dadhani ‘nedam dadhi iti bādhaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na api kṣīram idam iti pratītiḥ iha tu tad ubhayam dṛśyate kiñca rajata rūpeṇa ced  pariṇatā śuktiḥ kṣīram iva dadhi rūpeṇa tadā doṣa apagame api tathā eva avatiṣṭheta nanu kamala mukula vikāsa pariṇāma hetoḥ sāvitrasya tejasaḥ sthiti hetu tvam api dṛṣṭam tad apagame punar  mukulībhāva darśanāt  tathā iha api syāt  na tathā sati tadvat eva pūrva avasthā pariṇāma buddhiḥ syāt  na bādha pratītiḥ syāt  atha punar  duṣṭa kāraṇa janyāyāḥ pratīteḥ eva rajata utpādaḥ iti manyeta etad api na samyak iva katham yasyāḥ pratīteḥ tad utpādaḥ tasyāḥ tāvat  na tad  ālambanam pūrva uttara bhāvena bhinna kāla tvāt na prati iti antarasya puruṣa antara pratīteḥ api tad prasaṅgāt  nanu kim iti puruṣa antara pratīteḥ api tad prasaṅgaḥ duṣṭa sāmagrī janmanaḥ  hi pratīteḥ tad  ālambanam mā evam prati iti antarasya api tadvidhasya rajata antara utpādanena eva upayukta tvāt  prathama pratyayavat  atas  anutpanna samam eva syāt  tad evam pāriśeṣyāt  smṛti pramoṣa eva avatiṣṭheta nanu smṛteḥ pramoṣaḥ  na sambhavati iti uktam tathā ca tantra antarīyā āhuḥ ‘anubhūta viṣaya asampramoṣā smṛtiḥ iti kā tarhi gatiḥ śukti samprayoge rajata avabhāsasya ucyate na indriya ja jñānāt  saṃskāra jam smaraṇam pṛthak eva smaraṇa abhimāna śūnyam samutpannam kintu ekam eva saṃskāra sahitāt  indriyāt  katham etad  ucyate kāraṇa doṣaḥ kārya viśeṣe tasya śaktim nirundhan  eva saṃskāra viśeṣam api udbodhayati kārya gamya tvāt kāraṇa doṣa śakteḥ atas  saṃskāra duṣṭa kāraṇa saṃvalitā ekā sāmagrī sā ca ekam eva jñānam eka phalam janayati tasya ca doṣa utthāpita saṃskāra viśeṣa sahita sāmagrī samutpanna jñānasya ucitam eva śukti gata mithyā rajatam ālambanam avabhāsate tena mithyā ālambanam jñānam mithyājñānam na svatas  jñānasya mithyātvam asti bādhā bhāvāt  bhinna jātīya jñāna hetu sāmagryoḥ katham eka jñāna utpādanam iti ced  na eṣa doṣaḥ dṛśyate hi liṅga jñāna saṃskārayoḥ sambhūya liṅgi jñāna utpādanam pratyabhijñāna utpādanañca akṣa saṃskārayoḥ ubhayatra api smṛti garbham ekam eva pramāṇa jñānam saṃskārān udbodhe tad abhāvāt tasmāt  liṅga darśanam eva sambandha jñāna saṃskāram udbodhya tad sahitam liṅgi jñānam janayati iti vaktavyam ayam eva ca nyāyaḥ pratyabhijñāne api na punar  jñāna dvaye pramāṇam asti tathā bhinna jātīya jñāna hetubhyaḥ  nīla ādibhya ekam citra jñānam nidarśanīyam tatra laiṅgika jñāna pratyabhijñā citra jñānānām aduṣṭa kāraṇa ārabdha tvāt  yathārtham eva avabhāsaḥ iha tu kāraṇa doṣāt atathābhūta artha avabhāsaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ evaṃca sati na anubhava virodhaḥ pratibhāsamānasya rajatasya eva avalambana tvāt atas  māyā mayam rajatam atha punar  pāramārthikam syāt  sarvaiḥ eva gṛhyeta yatas  na hi pāramārthikam rajatam kāraṇa doṣam sva jñāna utpattau  apekṣate yadi apekṣeta tadā tad abhāve na tatra jñāna utpattiḥ āloka abhāve iva rūpe māyā mātra tve tu mantra ādi upahata cakṣuṣa atirikta kāraṇa abhāvāt smṛtiḥ eva na smṛti rūpa tā atra ucyate na tāvat  smṛti tvam asti aparokṣa artha avabhāsanāt  nanu smṛti rūpa tvam api na asti pūrva pramāṇa saṃskāra mātra janya tvāt atra ucyate uktam etad  pūrva pramāṇa viṣaya avabhāsitva mātram smṛteḥ svarūpam iti tad iha nidrā ādi doṣa upaplutam manaḥ adṛṣṭa ādi samudbodhita saṃskāra viśeṣa saha kārya anurūpam mithyā artha viṣayam jñānam utpādayati tasya ca tad avacchinna aparokṣa caitanya sthāvidyā śaktiḥ ālambana tayā vivartate nanu evam sati antar ā iva svapna artha pratibhāsaḥ syāt  kaḥ  vā brūte na antar iti nanu vicchinna deśaḥ anubhūyate svapne api jāgaraṇa iva na tad antar anubhava āśraya tve svapna arthasya upapadyate nanu deśaḥ api tādṛśa eva kutas tad sambandhāt vicchedaḥ avabhāsate ayam api tarhi aparaḥ  doṣaḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ jāgaraṇe api pramāṇa jñānāt antara parokṣa anubhavāt na viṣaya sthā aparokṣatā bhidyate eka rūpa prakāśanāt  atas antara parokṣa anubhava avaguṇṭhita eva jāgaraṇe api arthaḥ anubhūyate anyathā jaḍasya prakāśa anupapatteḥ yathā tamasā avaguṇṭhitaḥ  ghaṭaḥ pradīpa prabhāva guṇṭhanam antareṇa na prakāśībhavati evam yaḥ punar viccheda avabhāsaḥ sa jāgare api māyā vijṛmbhitaḥ sarvasya prapañca jātasya caitanya eka āśraya tvāt tasya ca niraṃśasya pradeśa bheda abhāvāt  prapañca bhedena eva hi tad  kalpita avacchedam sat avacchinnam iva bahis iva antar iva prakāśate athavā diś ākāśau manaḥ mātra gocarau sarvatra adhyāsa ādhārau vidyete iti na paratra iti virudhyate katham tarhi nāma ādiṣu brahma adhyāsaḥ kim atra katham na tatra kāraṇa doṣaḥ na api mithyā artha avabhāsaḥ satyam ata eva codanā vaśāt icchātaḥ anuṣṭheya tvāt mānasī kriyā eṣā na jñānam jñānasya hi duṣṭa kāraṇa janyasya viṣayaḥ  mithyā arthaḥ na hi jñānam icchātaḥ  janayitum nivartayitum vā śakyam kāraṇa eka āyatta tvāt icchā anupraveśa anupapatteḥ nanu smṛti jñānam ābhogena janyamānam manaḥ nirodhena ca nirudhyamānam dṛśyate satyam na smṛti utpatti nirodhayoḥ tayoḥ vyāpāraḥ kintu kāraṇa vyāpāre tad pratibandhe ca cakṣuṣa iva unmīlana nimīlane na punar jñāna utpattau vyāpāra icchāyāḥ tasmāt  brahma dṛṣṭiḥ kevalā adhyasyate codanā vaśāt phalāya eva mātṛ buddhiḥ iva rāga nivṛttaye para yoṣiti tad evam anavadyam adhyāsasya lakṣaṇam smṛti rūpaḥ paratra pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ iti ‘tam kecit ityādinā adhyāsa svarūpe mata antaram upanyasyati sva mata pariśuddhaye katham anyatra śuktikā ādau anya dharmasya artha antarasya rajata ādeḥ jñāna ākārasya bahiṣṭhasya eva vā adhyāsaḥ iti vadanti kecid tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tad viveka agrahaṇa nibandhanaḥ  bhramaḥ iti yatra yasya adhyāsaḥ tayoḥ vivekasya agrahaṇāt  tad nibandhanaḥ ayam ekatva bhramaḥ iti vadanti iti anuṣaṅgaḥ anye tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tasya eva viparīta dharmatva kalpanām ācakṣate iti yatra śuktikā ādau yasya rajata ādeḥ adhyāsaḥ tasya eva śukti śakala ādeḥ viparīta dharma tvasya rajata ādi rūpa tvasya kalpanām avidyamānasya eva avabhāsamāna tām ācakṣate sarvathā api tu iti sva mata anusāri tvam sarveṣām kalpanā prakārāṇām darśayati anyasya anya dharma avabhāsa tvam nāma lakṣaṇam paratra iti ukte arthāt  para avabhāsaḥ siddhaḥ iti yad avādiṣyam tad  na vyabhicarati katham pūrvasmin kalpe jñāna ākārasya bahiṣṭhasya vā śukti dharmatva avabhāsanāt  na vyabhicāraḥ dvitīye api śukti rajatayoḥ pṛthak  sa tora pṛthak avabhāsaḥ abhimānāt  tṛtīye api śukti śakalasya rajata rūpa pratibhāsanāt  pūrva dṛṣṭatva smṛti rūpa tvayoḥ sarvatra avyabhicārāt  na vivādaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tatra ‘smṛti rūpaḥ pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ iti etāvati lakṣaṇe niradhiṣṭhāna adhyāsava ādi pakṣe api nirupapattike lakṣaṇa vyāptiḥ syāt iti tad nivṛttaye ‘paratra iti ucyate katham nirupapattikaḥ ayam pakṣaḥ na hi niradhiṣṭhānaḥ adhyāsaḥ  dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ sambhavī vā nanu keśāṇḍraka ādi avabhāsaḥ  niradhiṣṭhānaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na tasya api tejaḥ avayava adhiṣṭhāna tvāt nanu rajate saṃvid  saṃvidi rajatam iti paraspara adhiṣṭhānaḥ  bhaviṣyati bīja aṅkura ādivat  na etad  sāram na tatra yatas  bījāt  yaḥ aṅkuraḥ tatas  eva tad bījam api tu aṅkura antarāt iha punar  yasyām saṃvidi yad  rajatam avabhāsate tayoḥ eva itara itara adhyāsaḥ tatas  durghaṭam etad  bīja aṅkura ādiṣu api na bīja aṅkura antara paramparā mātreṇa abhimata vastu siddhiḥ pratītitaḥ  vastu tas ca anivṛtta ākāṅkṣa tvāt  tathā ca ‘kuta idam evaṃ iti paryanuyoge ‘dṛṣṭa tvāt evaṃ iti tatra eva dūram vā paridhāvya sthātavyam anyathā hetu paramparām eva avalambya kvacid api anavatiṣṭhamānaḥ  na anavasthā doṣam ativarteta api ca na kvacid niravadhikaḥ  ‘na iti eva bādha avagamaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ yatra api anumānāt āpta vacanāt vā na sarpaḥ iti eva avagamaḥ tatra api ‘kim punar idam iti apekṣā darśanāt puras avasthitam vastu mātram avadhiḥ vidyate pradhāna ādiṣu api jagat kāraṇe triguṇatva ādi bādhaḥ adhigata avadhiḥ eva athavā sarva loka sākṣikam etad  keśoṇḍraka ādau  api tad bādhe tad anuṣaṅga eva bodhe bādhyate na bodhaḥ atas  tad avadhiḥ sarvasya bādhaḥ tena tanmātrasya bādhā bhāvāt  svatas ca viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ kūṭastha aparokṣa eka rasa caitanya avadhiḥ sarvasya bādhaḥ na api adhyastam api asat eva tathā tve pratibhāsā yogāt nanu sarvam eva idam asat iti bhavataḥ  matam ka evam āha anirvacanīyānādi vidyā ātmakam iti udghoṣitam asmābhiḥ atha punar vidyā udaye avidyāyāḥ  nirupākhya tām aṅgīkṛtya asattvamucyeta kāmam abhidhīyatām tathā ca bādhaka jñānam ‘nedam rajatam iti viśiṣṭa deśa kāla sambaddham rajatam vilopayadeva udeti na deśa antara sambandham āpādayati tathā anavagamāt  tathā ca dūra vartinīm rajjum sarpam manyamānasya nikaṭa vartinā āptena ‘nāyam sarpaḥ iti ukte sarpa abhāva mātram pratipadyate na tasya deśa antara varti tvam tad pratipattau  asāmarthyāt  vākyasya na artha apattyā iha bhagna ghaṭa abhāvavat tāvat mātreṇa api tad siddheḥ yatra api sarpa bādha pūrva kaḥ  rajju vidhiḥ akṣa janyaḥ tādṛśa vākya janyaḥ  vā tatra api sa eva nyāyaḥ tathā anavagamāt  tad evam na kvacid niradhiṣṭhānaḥ adhyāsaḥ tasmāt  sādhu uktam paratra iti yadi evam ‘paratra pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ iti etāvat astu lakṣaṇam tathāvidhasya smṛti rūpatva avyabhicārāt  satyam artha labhyasya smṛti tvam eva syāt  na smṛti rūpa tvam na ca smṛti viṣayasya adhyāsa tvam iti uktam yadi evam etāvat astu lakṣaṇam paratra smṛti rūpa avabhāsaḥ iti tatra paratra iti ukte artha labhyasya para avabhāsasya smṛti rūpa tvam viśeṣaṇam na hi parasya asamprayuktasya pūrva dṛṣṭatva abhāve smṛti rūpatva sambhavaḥ satyam vispaṣṭa artham pūrva dṛṣṭa grahaṇam iti yathānyāsam eva lakṣaṇam astu tathā ca loke anubhavaḥ iti udāharaṇa dvayena laukika siddham eva idam adhyāsasya svarūpam lakṣitam kim atra yuktyā iti kathayati śuktikā hi rajatavat avabhāsate iti nanu na śuktikā pratibhāsate rajatam eva pratibhāsate tena śuktikā iti rajatavat iti ca ubhayam na upapadyate ucyate śuktikā grahaṇam uparitana samyak jñāna siddham paramārthataḥ śuktikā tvam apekṣya vatigrahaṇam tu samprayuktasya ārajata svarūpasya mithyā rajata sambheda iva avabhāsanam aṅgīkṛtya mithyātvam api rajatasya āgantuka doṣa nimitta tvāt anantara bādha darśanāt ca kathyate na punar  parama artha abhimatāt rajatāt anya tvam āśritya tatra asamprayukta tvāt rajatasya nedanta avabhāsaḥ tad gataḥ kintu samprayukta gata eva aparokṣa avabhāsaḥ tu saṃskāra janmanaḥ api rajata ullekhasya doṣa balāt indriya jajñāna antarbhāvāt ca itidraṣṭavyam tatra śuktikā udāha raṇena samprayuktasya anātmā rajatam iti darśitam nirañjanasya caitanyasya asmad arthe anidam aṃśasya anātmā tad avabhāsya tvena yuṣmad artha lakṣaṇa āpannaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ adhyastaḥ iti pradarśana artham dvi candra udāharaṇena jīveśvarayoḥ jīvānām ca anātma rūpaḥ  bheda avabhāsaḥ iti darśitam nanu bahis arthe kāraṇa doṣaḥ artha gataḥ sādṛśya ādiḥ indriya gataḥ ca timira ādiḥ upalabhyate tad nimittaḥ ca arthasya sa aṃśa tvāt aṃśa antara avagrahe api aṃśa antara pratibandhaḥ  yujyeta na tu iha kāraṇa antara āyattā siddhiḥ yena tad doṣāt anavabhāsaḥ api syāt  niraṃśasya caitanyasya svayan jyotiṣaḥ tad ayogāt  nanu brahma svarūpam anavabhāsamānam asti eva na tad anavabhāsanāt jīve anavabhāsa viparyāsau bhavataḥ na hi śukteḥ agrahaṇāt  sthāṇa  agrahaṇam viparyāsaḥ  vā nanu na brahmaṇaḥ anyaḥ  jīvaḥ ‘anena jīvena ātmanā u iti śruteḥ atas  tad agrahaṇam ātmana eva tad  evam tarhi sutarām avidyāyāḥ tatra asambhavaḥ tasya vidyā ātmaka tvāt  ‘tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti tad caitanyena eva sarvasya bhāsamāna tvāt  ucyate vidyata eva atra api agrahaṇā avidyā ātmakaḥ  doṣaḥ prakāśasya acchādakaḥ katham gamyate śruteḥ tad arthāpatteḥ ca śrutiḥ tāvat  ‘anṛtena hi pratyūḍhāḥ ‘anīśayā śocati muhyamānaḥ iti evamādyā tad arthāpattiḥ api vidyā eva sarvatra śrutiṣu brahma viṣayā mokṣāya nivedyate tena arthāt idam avagamyate jīvasya brahma svarūpa tā navagamaḥ avidyā ātmakaḥ  bandhaḥ nisargata eva asti iti nanu na jīvaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ anyaḥ iti uktam bāḍham ata eva arthāt jīve brahma svarūpa prakāśa acchādikā avidyā kalpyate anyathā paramārthataḥ tad svarūpa tve tad avabodhaḥ api yadi nitya siddhaḥ syāt  tadā tādātmya upadeśaḥ  vyarthaḥ syāt  atas  anādi siddha avidyā avacchinna ananta jīva nirbhāsā āspadam eka rasam brahma iti śruti smṛti nyāya kovidaiḥ abhyupagantavyam tathā ca smṛtiḥ ‘prakṛtim puruṣam ca eva viddhi anādī ubhau  api iti kṣetra kṣetrajñatva nimittām anādi siddhām avidyām prakṛti śabdena āha ‘māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt iti śruteḥ atas  māyā avacchinna rūpa tvāt ananyat api brahma rūpam ātmanaḥ  na vetti tathā ca uktam ‘anādi māyayā suptaḥ  yadā jīvaḥ prabuddhyate ajam anidram asvapnam advaitam budhyate tadā
 iti nanu pramāṇa antara virodhe sati śrutiḥ tad arthāpattiḥ vā na avidyām nivedayitum alam kim tad  pramāṇam yena saha virodhaḥ niraṃśasya svayan jyotiṣaḥ sva rūpa anavabhāsa anupapattiḥ nanu bhoktuḥ kārya kāraṇa saṅghātāt vyāvṛtta tā svayan jyotiṣaḥ api na prakāśate nanu na bhoktā svayan jyotiḥ kim tu ahaṃpratyayena avabhāsyate yathā svayam prakāśamānatā ahaṅkāraḥ  na pratyayaḥ tathā vakṣyate katham punar  bhoktā svayan jyotiḥ kārya karaṇa saṅghātāt vyāvṛttaḥ  na prakāśate ‘manuṣyaḥ aham i ati mithyā eva ekatā abhimānāt nanu gauṇaḥ ayam na mithyā yathā na gauṇaḥ tathā bhāṣya kāra eva vakṣyati nanu ‘aham i ati yadi deha samāna adhikaraṇaḥ pratyayaḥ na tarhi tad vyatirikta ātmā sidhyati anyasya tathā grāhiṇaḥ pratyayasya abhāvāt  āgama anumānayoḥ api tad virodhe pramāṇatva ayogāt mithyātvāt  tasya na virodhaḥ iti ced  kutas tarhi mithyātvam āgamāt anumānāt vā anyathā avagamāt iti ced  na etad  anyaḥ anya āśraya tā tathā syāt  āgama anumānayoḥ pravṛttau tad mithyā tvam tad mithyā tve tayoḥ pravṛttiḥ iti tasmāt  deha ādi vyatirikta viṣaya eva ayam ahaṅkāraḥ iti ātma vādibhiḥ abhyupeyam anyathā ātma siddhiḥ aprāmāṇikī syāt  atas  gauṇaḥ  manuṣyatva abhimānaḥ ucyate yadi api deha ādi vyatirikta bhoktṛ viṣaya eva ayam ahaṅkāraḥ tathā api tathā anadhyavasāyāt  tad dharmān ātmani adhyasyati dṛśyate hi sva rūpeṇa avabhāsamāne api vastu antara bheda anadhyavasāyāt  tad sambhedena avabhāsaḥ yathā ekasmin  api akāre hṛsu ādi sambhedaḥ atha punar ekāntatas  bhinna eva deha ādeḥ ahaṅkartā avabhāseta rasāt iva gandhaḥ tatas  tad sadbhāve na vipratipattiḥ iti tad siddhaye jijñāsā na avakalpeta jijñāsā uttara kālam tarhi gauṇa eva yuktaḥ katham jijñāsā nāma yukti anusandhānam na hi yuktiḥ pṛthak  jñāna antara jananī kintu siddhasya eva ahaṃpratyayasya viṣaya vivecinī tasmāt  vivikta viṣaya tvāt  vyatirikta ātma anubhava paryanta eva ahaṅkāraḥ  jijñāsā uttara kālam yuktaḥ na yuktaḥ akāra iva hṛsvatva abhimānaḥ nanu tatra api katham anubhava eva evam ahaṅkāre api samānaḥ carcaḥ nanu anubhavaḥ tarka balāt yathā avabhāsinī api akāre sambhavati hṛsvādeḥ pṛthak sataḥ tathā anavagamāt tad na ekasya pṛthaktve api arthāditarasya api pṛthaktvāt  nanu mahat etad indrajālam yad  tarka anugṛhītāt pramāṇāt  yathāyatham asādhāraṇa rūpayoḥ eva avabhāsamānayoḥ ekatva avagamaḥ  na gauṇa iti bāḍham indrajālam eva etad  avidyā kṛta tvāt  tathā hi ahaṃpratyayasya sva viṣaya pratiṣṭhitasya eva sataḥ tad eka pratiṣṭhita tā pratibandha kṛt ana ādi avidyā kṛtam deha ādi pratiṣṭhita tvam api dṛṣṭam atas  deha ādi viṣayatva avirodhi sva viṣaya pratiṣṭha tvam ahaṃpratyayasya atas  yuktyā viṣaya vivecane api sva viṣaya upadarśanena tad pratiṣṭhatva mātram kṛtam na adhikam ādarśitam sva viṣaya pratiṣṭha tvam ca deha ādiṣu ahaṃmama abhimānena na virudhyate iti uktam atas  nyāyataḥ  viṣaya vivecanāt ūrdhvam api na prāc avasthātaḥ  viśiṣyate ahaṃpratyayaḥ tena na kadācid api ‘manuṣyaḥ aham i ati pratyayaḥ gauṇaḥ tad evam svayan jyotiṣa eva sataḥ  jīvasya kārya karaṇa saṅghāta vyatirikta tāyāḥ tathā anavabhāsa darśanāt  amanuṣyaḥ aham i ati ca adhyāsa upalabdheḥ brahma ātmā eka tvasya api tad svarūpasya anavabhāsanam pūrva kāla koṭi rahita prakāśa ācchādita tamaḥ nimittam śruti tad arthāpatti samarpitam tad nimitta ahaṅka āra adhyāsaḥ ca sambhāvyate anādi tvāt ca pūrva dṛṣṭa tvam smṛti rūpa tvam ca pṛthak bhoktṛ viṣaya anubhava phala abhāvāt bhoktṛ caitanya saṃvalita eka anubhava phala tvāt ca paratra para avabhāsasya anyonya sambhedasya vidyamāna tvāt adhyāsa lakṣaṇa vyāptiḥ iha api upapadyate ‘kaḥ ayam adhyāsaḥ  nāme ati kiṃvṛttasya praśna ākṣepe ca samāna vartinaḥ  viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ‘pṛṣṭam anene ati matvā adhyāsa svarūpe abhihite punar  ‘a ākṣiptam maye ati abhiprāyam vivṛṇoti katham punar  pratyak ātmani aviṣaye adhyāsaḥ  viṣaya tad dharmāṇām iti bāḍham evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ adhyāsaḥ sa ca iha na sambhavati katham yatas  sarvaḥ  hi puras avasthite viṣaye viṣaya antara madhyasyati yuṣmad pratyaya apetasya ca pratyak ātmanaḥ aviṣaya tvam bravīṣi na hi aviṣaye adhyāsaḥ  dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ sambhavī vā ucyate na tāvat ayam ekāntena aviṣayaḥ asmad pratyaya viṣaya tvāt nanu viṣayiṇaḥ cit ātmanaḥ katham viṣaya bhāvaḥ parāgbhāvena idantā samullekhyaḥ  hi viṣayaḥ  nāma bhavati tad vaiparītyena pratyagrūpeṇa anidam prakāśaḥ  viṣayī tad  katham ekasya niraṃśasya viruddha aṃśa dvaya sanniveśaḥ atra ucyate asmad pratyayatva abhimataḥ ahaṅkāraḥ sa cedam anidaṃ rūpa vastu garbhaḥ sarva loka sākṣikaḥ tam avahita cetaḥ tayā nipuṇataram abhivīkṣya rūpaka parīkṣakavat  sva anubhavam apracchādayantaḥ  vadantu bhavantaḥ parīkṣakāḥ kim ukta lakṣaṇaḥ na vā iti nanu kim atra vaditavyam asambhinna idaṃrūpa eva aham iti anubhavaḥ katham pramātṛ prameya pramitayaḥ tāvat aparokṣāḥ prameyam karma tvena aparokṣam pramātṛ pramitī punar aparokṣe eva kevalam na karma tayā pramitiḥ anubhavaḥ svayamprakāśaḥ pramāṇa phalam tad balena itarat  prakāśate pramāṇam tu pramātṛ vyāpāraḥ phala liṅgaḥ  nitya anumeyaḥ tatra ‘aham idam jānāmī ati pramātuḥ jñāna vyāpāraḥ karma viṣayaḥ na ātma viṣayaḥ ātmā tu viṣaya anubhavāt eva nimittāt aham iti phale viṣaye ca anusandhīyate nanu na ayam viṣaya anubhava nimittaḥ aham ullekhaḥ kim tu anya eva ātma mātra viṣayaḥ ‘aham i ati pratyayaḥ tasmin  ca dravya rūpa tvena ātmanaḥ prameya tvam jñātṛ tvena pramātṛ tvam iti pramātṛ prameya nirbhāsa rūpa tvāt ahaṃpratyayasya grāhya grāhaka rūpa ātmā tasmāt idam anidaṃrūpaḥ prameya aṃśasya idaṃrūpa tvāt anidaṃrūpa tvāt  pramātṛ aṃśasya na ca etad yuktam anaṃśa tvāt  apariṇāmi tvāt ca ātmanaḥ prameyasya cedaṃrūpatayā parāgrūpa tvāt anātma tvāt  tasmāt nīla ādi jñāna phalam anubhavaḥ svayam prakāśamānaḥ  grāhyam idantayā grāhakam ca anidantayā avabhāsayati grahaṇam ca anumāpayati iti yuktam atas  na idam aṃśaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ  yujyate ucyate tatra idam bhavān praṣṭavyaḥ kim ātmā caitanya prakāśaḥ anubhavaḥ  jaḍa prakāśaḥ uta saḥ api caitanya prakāśaḥ athavā sa eva caitanya prakāśaḥ ātmā jaḍa svarūpaḥ iti tatra na tāvat prathamaḥ kalpaḥ jaḍa svarūpe pramāṇa phale viśvasya anavabhāsa prasaṅgāt  mā evam pramātā cetanaḥ tad balena pradīpena iva viṣayam idantayā ātmānam ca anidantayā cetayate iti na viśvasya anavabhāsa prasaṅgaḥ tad na svayan caitanya svabhāvaḥ api san viṣaya pramāṇena acetanena anugṛhītaḥ prakāśata iti na etad  sādhu lakṣyate kim ca pramāṇa phalena ced  pradīpena iva viṣayam ātmānam ca cetayate tadā cetayati kriyā anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye kalpe ātmā api svayam eva prakāśeta kim iti viṣaya anubhavam apekṣeta atha caitanya svabhāva tve api na ātmā svayamprakāśaḥ viśeṣe hetuḥ vācyaḥ na hi caitanya svabhāvaḥ san svayam parokṣaḥ anyatas aparokṣa iti yujyate kim ca sama tvāt na itara itara apekṣa tvam prakāśane pradīpayoḥ iva tṛtīye api kalpe anicchataḥ api ātmā eva citi prakāśa āpadyate na tad atirikta tathāvidha phala sadbhāve pramāṇam asti katham pramāṇa janyaḥ ced anubhavaḥ tathā sati sva gatena viśeṣeṇa prativiṣayam pṛthak  pṛthak avabhāseta sarva anubhava anugatam ca gaḥ tvavat anubhava tvam aparam īkṣyeta na ca ‘nīla anubhavaḥ pīta anubhavaḥ iti viṣaya viśeṣa parāmarśa śūnyaḥ sva gataḥ  viśeṣaḥ  lakṣyate nanu vinaṣṭa avinaṣṭa tvena viśeṣaḥ sidhyati sidhyet  yadi vinaṣṭa avinaṣṭa tā sidhyet  sā ca janya tve sati tasyām ca siddhāyām janya tvam iti paraspara āyatta sthiti tvena ekam api na sidhyet  etena atisādṛśyāt anubhava bhedaḥ  na vibhāvyata iti pratyuktam bheda asiddheḥ na hi cit prakāśasya sva gataḥ  bhedaḥ  na prakāśate iti yuktimat  yena tad aprakāśanāt sādṛśya nibandhanaḥ  vibhramaḥ syāt  na ca yathā jīvasya svayan jyotiṣaḥ api svarūpam eva sat  brahma rūpa tvam na prakāśate tadvat  syāt iti yuktam abhihitam tatra aprakāśane pramāṇam iha tad na asti na hi sāmānyatodṛṣṭam anubhava virodhe yukti virodhe ca samuttiṣṭhati darśite ca anubhava yuktī tasmāt  cit svabhāva eva ātmā tena tena prameya bhedena upadhīyamānaḥ anubhava abhidhānīyakam labhate avivakṣita upādhiḥ ātma ādi śabdaiḥ abhidhīyate avadhīrita vana abhidhāna nimitta eka deśa avasthānā iva vṛkṣā vṛkṣa ādi śabdaiḥ iti abhyupagantavyam bāḍham ata eva viṣaya anubhava nimittaḥ anidama ātmakaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ  varṇyate satyam evam kintu tathā sati suṣuptepi ‘ahami ati ullekhaḥ syāt  katham nīla anuṣaṅgaḥ  yaḥ caitanyasya sa nīla bhogaḥ nāsau  aham ullekhā arhaḥ aaham i ati ātmā avabhāsate tatra yadi nāma suṣupte viṣaya anuṣaṅga abhāvāt idam jānāmī ati viṣaya tad anubhava parām arśaḥ  na asti mā bhūt  aham iti ātma mātra parāmarśaḥ kim iti na bhavet  nanu aham iti bhoktṛ tvam pratibhāsate tad abhāve katham tathā pratibhāsaḥ na etad  sāram samutkālita upādhi viśeṣam caitanya mātram asmad arthaḥ tatas  sarvadā aham iti syāt  na etad śakyam upādhi parāmarśena caitanyam aham iti ullikhyata iti vaktum tad parām arśaḥ  hi tad siddhi nimittaḥ na svarūpa siddhi hetuḥ sva māhātmyena eva tu svarūpa siddhiḥ tatas ca viṣaya uparāga anubhava ātmatva śūnyaḥ svarūpataḥ aham iti suṣupte api avabhāseta dṛśi rūpatva aviśeṣāt  bhavati eva iti ced  na tathā sati smaryeta hyastana iva ahaṅkāraḥ avināśinaḥ saṃskāra abhāvāt  na smaryate iti ced  hyastanaḥ api na smaryeta nanu asti eva suṣupte aham anubhavaḥ ‘sukham aham asva apsami ati suṣupta utthitasya svāpa sukha anubhava parāmarśa darśanāt na ātmanaḥ anyasya tatra anubhavaḥ sambhavati satyam asti na tad  svāpe sukha anubhava saṃskāra jam smaraṇam kim tarhi sukha avamarśaḥ  duḥkha abhāva nimittaḥ katham svapne tāvat asti eva duḥkha anubhavaḥ suṣupte tu tad abhāvāt sukha vyapadeśaḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca karaṇa vyāpāra uparamāt  yadi punar ‘suptaḥ sukham iti ca tad viṣayam smaraṇam syāt  tadā viśeṣataḥ smaryeta na ca tad asti vyapadeśaḥ api ‘sukham supte na kiñcid mayā cetitam iti hi dṛśyate yad  punar  supta utthitasya aṅga lāghava indriya prasāda ādinā sukha anubhava unnayanam iti tad asat  anubhūtam ced  sukham smaryeta na tatra liṅgena prayojanam yadi evam supta utthitasya katham kasyacid aṅga lāghavam kasya cit na iti ucyate jāgaraṇe kārya karaṇāni śrāmyanti tad apanuttaye vyāpāra uparamaḥ svāpaḥ tatra yadi samyak  vyāpāra uparamaḥ tadā aṅgāni laghūni itarathā gurūṇi iti tad evam na ayam nīla ādi pratyayāt anya eva ātma viṣayaḥ ahaṃpratyayaḥ na api viṣaya anubhavāt eva aham ullekhaḥ tasmāt  brahma vidām eka puṇḍarīkasya loka anugraha eka rasa tayā samyak jñāna pravartana prayojana kṛta śarīra parigrahasya bhagavataḥ  bhāṣya kārasya matam āgamayitavyam tad ucyate yā iyam śruti smṛti itihāsa purāṇeṣu nāma rūpam avyākṛtam avidyā māyā prakṛtiḥ agrahaṇam avyaktam tamaḥ kāraṇam layaḥ śaktiḥ mahā suptiḥ nidrā akṣaram ākāśam iti ca tatra tatra bahudhā gīyate caitanyasya svata eva avasthita lakṣaṇa brahma svarūpa tā ava bhāsam pratibadhya jīvatu āpādikā avidyā karma pūrva prajñā saṃskāra citra bhittiḥ suṣupte prakāśa ācchādana vikṣepa saṃskāra mātra rūpa sthitiḥ anādiḥ avidyā tasyāḥ parameśvara adhiṣṭhitatva labdha pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ  vijñāna kriyā śakti dvaya āśrayaḥ kartṛtva bhoktṛtva eka ādhāraḥ kūṭastha caitanya saṃvalana sañjāta jyotiḥ svayam prakāśamānaḥ aparokṣaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ yad sambhedāt  kūṭastha caitanyaḥ anidam aṃśa ātmadhātuḥ api mithyā eva abhokte ati prasiddhim upagataḥ sa ca suṣupte samutkhāta nikhila pariṇāmāyām avidyāyām kutastyaḥ na ca evam mantavyam āśrita pariṇati bheda tayā eva ahaṅkāra nirbhāse anantarbhūtā eva tad nimittam iti tathā sati apākṛta ahaṅkṛti saṃsargaḥ  bhoktṛtva ādiḥ tad viśeṣaḥ kevalam idantayā eva avabhāseta na ca tathā samasti sa ca pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ anidañcit ātmanaḥ  buddhyā niṣkṛṣya vedānta vādibhiḥ antaḥkaraṇam manaḥ buddhiḥ ahaṃpratyayī iti ca vijñāna śakti viśeṣam āśritya vyapadiśyate parispanda śaktyā ca prāṇaḥ iti tena antaḥkaraṇa uparāga nimittam mithyā eva ahaṅkartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ sphaṭika maṇeḥ iva upadhāna nimittaḥ  lohitimā katham punar  sphaṭike lohitimnaḥ  mithyātvam ucyate yadi sphaṭika pratisphālitā nayana raśmayaḥ  japā kusumam upasarpeyuḥ tadā viśiṣṭa saṃniveśam tad eva lohitam grāhayeyuḥ na hi rūpa mātra niṣṭhaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ na api sva āśrayam anākarṣat rūpa mātram pratibimbitam kvacid upalabdha pūrvam nanu abhijātasya iva padmarāga ādi maṇeḥ japā kusuma ādeḥ api prabhā vidyate tayā vyāpta tvāt  sphaṭikaḥ api lohita iva avabhāsate tathā api svayam alohitaḥ  mithyā eva lohita iti āpadyeta atha prabhā eva lohitaḥ avabhāsate na sphaṭika iti śauklyam api tarhi sphaṭike prakāśeta atha prabhayā apasāritam tad iti ced  sa tarhi nīrūpaḥ katham cākṣuṣaḥ syāt  na ca rūpi dravya saṃyogāt  vāyoḥ api tathātva prasaṅgāt  na prabhā nimittam lauhityam tatra utpannam uttara kālam api tathā rūpa prasaṅgāt  abhyupagamya prabhām idam uktam yathā padmarāga ādi prabhā nirāśrayā api unmukha upalabhyate na tathā japā kusuma ādeḥ tad evam sphaṭi ka maṇau  upadhāna uparāga iva cit ātmani api ahaṅkāra uparāgaḥ tatas  sambhinna ubhaya rūpa tvāt  granthiḥ iva bhavati iti ahaṅkāraḥ  granthiḥ iti gīyate tatra jaḍa rūpa tvāt uparaktasya na tad balāt uparāgasya sākṣāt bhāvaḥ cit rūpasya punar uparāgaḥ tad viṣaya vyāpāra virahiṇaḥ api tad balāt  prakāśate tena lakṣaṇata idam aṃśaḥ kathyate na vyavahārataḥ vyavahārataḥ punar  yad uparāgāt anidam ātmanaḥ ahaṅkartṛ tvam mithyā tad ātmanaḥ tad vyāpāreṇa vyāpriyamāṇasya eva vyāpāra pūrva kaḥ  yasya paricchedaḥ sa eva idam ātmakaḥ  viṣayaḥ ata eva aaham i atya sambhinna idam ātmakaḥ avabhāsaḥ iti vibhramaḥ keṣāñcid  dṛṣṭaḥ ca lakṣaṇataḥ tad vyavahāra arhaḥ api tam ananupatan tad yathā aṅkura ādi phala paryantaḥ  vṛkṣa vikāraḥ  mṛd pariṇāma paramparā pariniṣpannaḥ api ghaṭavalmīkavat  na mṛṇmaya vyavahāram anupatati vyutpanna matayaḥ tu tad vyavahāram api na atīva ulbaṇam manyante ata eva nipuṇataram abhivīkṣya rūpaka parīkṣakavat ahaṅkāram nirūpayatām sambhinnedaṃrūpaḥ saḥ iti abhihitam yad  punar  darpaṇa jala ādiṣu mukha candra ādi pratibimba udāharaṇam tad  ahaṅkartuḥ anidam aṃśaḥ bimbāt iva pratibimbam na brahmaṇaḥ  vastu antaram kim tu tad eva tad pṛthak avabhāsa viparyaya svarūpa tā mātram mithyā iti darśayitum katham punar tad eva tad  eka sva lakṣaṇatva avagamāt  tathā ca yathā bahis sthitaḥ  devadattaḥ  yad sva lakṣaṇaḥ pratipannaḥ tad sva lakṣaṇa eva veśma antar praviṣṭaḥ api pratīyate tathā darpaṇa tala sthitaḥ api na tad  vastu antara tve yujyate api ca arthāt  vastu antara tve sati ādarśa eva bimba sannidhau  eva tad ākāra garbhitaḥ pariṇataḥ iti vācyam viruddha parimāṇa tvāt  saṃśleṣa abhāvāt ca pratimudrā iva bimba lāñchitatva anupapatteḥ tathā sati bimba sannidhi labdha pariṇatiḥ ādarśaḥ tad apāye api tathā eva avatiṣṭheta na khalu saṃveṣṭitaḥ kaṭaḥ nimitta labdha prasāraṇa pariṇatiḥ nimitta apagame tad kṣaṇam eva saṃveṣṭate yathā tathā syāt iti mantavyam yatas cira kāla saṃveṣṭana āhita saṃskāraḥ tatra punar saṃveṣṭana nimittam tathā ca yāvat saṃskāra kṣayam prasāraṇa nimitta anuvṛttau punar saṃveṣṭana upajanaḥ evam cira kāla sannihita bimba nimitta tad ākāra pariṇatiḥ ādarśaḥ tathā eva tad apāye api yāvat āyuḥ avatiṣṭheta na ca tathā upalabhyate yaḥ punar  kamala mukulasya vikāsa pariṇati hetoḥ sāvitrasya tejasaḥ  dīrgha kāla anuvṛttasya api vigame tad sama kālam punar mukulībhāvaḥ sa prathamatara mukula hetu pārthiva apya avayava vyāpāra nimittaḥ tad uparame jīrṇasya punar mukula tā anupalabdheḥ na ādarśe punar tathā pūrvarūpa pariṇāma hetuḥ asti atra āha bhavatu na vastu antaram tad eva tad iti tu na kṣamyate śuktikā rajatasya mithyārūpasya api satya rajata eka rūpa avabhāsitva darśanāt mā evam tatra hi bādha darśanāt  mithyābhāvaḥ na iha sa bādhaḥ  dṛśyate yaḥ punar  darpaṇa apagame tad apagamaḥ na sa bādhaḥ darpaṇe api tad prasaṅgāt  nanu tattvam asi vākyāt bādhaḥ  dṛśyate mā evam tatra atattvam i ati bimba sthānīya brahma svarūpa tā pratibimba sthānīyasya jīvasya upadiśyate anyathā na atat tvam asī ati syāt  kintu‘na tvam asī ati bhavet  ‘na rajatamastī ativat  kim ca śāstrīyaḥ api vyavahāraḥ pratibimbasya pāramārthikam iva bimba eka rūpa tvam darśayati ‘nekṣeta udyantam ādityam na astam yantam kadācana na uparaktam na vāri stham na madhyam nabhasaḥ  gatam iti yaḥ tu manyate na parāk pravaṇa pravṛtta nayana raśmibhiḥ bimbam eva bhinna deśa stham gṛhyate kintu darpaṇa pratisphālitaiḥ parāvṛttya pratyaṅmukhaiḥ sva deśa stham eva bimbam gṛhyate iti tam anubhava eva nirākaroti iti na parākramyate katham punar  paricchinnam ekam eka svabhāvam vicchinna deśa dvaye sarva ātmanā avabhāsamānam ubhayatra pāramārthikam bhavati na vayam viccheda avabhāsam pāramārthikam brūmaḥ kim tu eka tvam vicchedaḥ tu māyā vijṛmbhitaḥ na hi māyāyām asambhāvanīyam nāma asambhāvanīya avabhāsa caturā hi sā nanu sati eva bimba eka tā avagame pratibimbasya tad gataḥ  viccheda ādi mithyā avabhāsaḥ tathā brahma ekatā avagame api jīvasya viccheda ādi mithyā avabhāsaḥ  na nivartitum arhati ucyate devadattasya acetana aṃśasya eva pratibimba tvāt  sa cetana aṃśasya eva vā pratibimba tve pratibimba hetoḥ śyāma ādi dharmeṇa iva jāḍyena api āskandita tvāt na tad  pratibimbam bimba eka rūpa tām ātmanaḥ  jānāti acetana tvāt  tathā ca anubhavaḥ ‘na bimba ceṣṭayā vinā pratibimbam ceṣṭate iti yasya hi bhrāntiḥ ātmani paratra vā samutpannā tad gatena eva samyak jñānena sā nivartate yaḥ tu jānīte devadattaḥ pratibimbasya ātmanaḥ abhinna tvam na sa tad gatena doṣeṇa saṃspṛśyate na api jñāna mātrāt pratibimbasya nivṛttiḥ tad hetoḥ darpaṇa ādeḥ pāramārthika tvāt  jīvaḥ punar  pratibimba kalpaḥ sarveṣām na pratyakṣaḥ cit rūpaḥ na antaḥkaraṇa jāḍyena askanditaḥ sa ca ahaṅkartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ  rūpam manyate na bimba kalpa brahma eka rūpa tām atas  yuktaḥ tad rūpa avagame mithyātva apagamaḥ nanu tatra vibhrāmyataḥ  vibhrama hetuḥ darpaṇa alaktaka ādi parama artha vastu sannihitam asti na tathā iha kiñcid  sarvatra eva cit vilakṣaṇe vibhrama vilāsa abhimānina iti mā bhūt āśaṅka iti rajju sarpam udāharanti nanu tatra api yadi nāma ida ānīm asannihitaḥ sarpaḥ tathā api pūrva nirvṛtta tad anubhava saṃskāraḥ samasti eva bāḍham iha api ahaṅkartṛ tā tad saṃskārayoḥ bīja aṅkurayoḥ iva anādeḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt  tad saṃskāraḥ  vibhrama hetuḥ vidyate tatra yadi api anirvacanīya tayā eva aruṇa ādinā sphaṭika ādeḥ sāvayava tvena sambheda yogyasya api asambheda avabhāsaḥ siddhaḥ tathā api tadā asaṅgī iva sphaṭika pratibimbam utprekṣate rajjvām punar  sarpa buddhiḥ eva na tad sambhinna tvam asambhinna tvam vā tasyām tena ‘asaṅgaḥ  na hi sajjate ‘asaṅgaḥ  hi ayam puruṣaḥ ityādi śruti samarpita asaṅga tā ātmanaḥ  na spaṣṭam darśitā iti tad artham ghaṭa ākāśa udāharaṇam tatra hi tad parāmarśāt ṛte na bheda rūpa kārya samākhyāḥ sva gatā dṛśyante etad ca sarvam udāharaṇa jātam śruti tad nyāya anubhava siddhasya tad asambhāvanā parihārāya buddhi sāmya artham ca na vastuna eva sākṣāt  siddhaye tad evam yadi api caitanya eka rasaḥ anidam ātmaka tvāt aviṣayaḥ tathā api ahaṅkāre vyavahāra yogyaḥ  bhavati iti gauṇya āvṛttyā asmat pratyaya viṣaya tā ucyate prameyasya ca vyavahāra yogyatva avyabhicārāt  nanu vyavahāra yogya tve adhyāsaḥ adhyāsa pariniṣpanna ahaṃpratyaya balāt vyavahāra yogya tvam iti prāptam itaretara āśraya tvam na anādi tvena pratyukta tvāt  tatra evaṃbhūtasya ahaṅkartuḥ idam aṃśasya jñāna saṃśabditaḥ  vyāpāra viśeṣaḥ sa karma tvāt  karma kāraka abhimukham sva āśraye kañcid avasthā viśeṣam ādadhāti sva āśraya vikāra hetu tvāt  kriyāyāḥ sa ca prāpnoti kriyā hita kartṛ stha viśeṣavat karma sambandhaḥ jñātuḥ jñeya sambandhaḥ iti gīyate tena viṣaya viśeṣa sambaddham eva antaḥkaraṇe caitanyasya avacchedakam karmakārakam api pradhāna kriyā siddhau sva vyāpāra āviṣṭam caitanya vivartta tvāt pradhāna kriyā hita pramātṛ avasthā viśeṣa avacchinna apara ukṣata eka rūpām aparokṣa tām abhivyanakti tatas ca ātmanaḥ antaḥkaraṇa avasthā viśeṣa upādhi janitaḥ  viśeṣaḥ viṣaya anubhava saṃśabditaḥ  viṣaya sthāparokṣa eka rasaḥ phalam iti kriyā eka viṣaya tā phalasya yujyate evam ca ahaṅkartā sva aṃśa caitanya balena vyāpāra āviṣṭa tayā ca pramātā iti buddhi stham artham puruṣaḥ cetayata iti ucyate tatra ca pramātuḥ svayan jyotiṣaḥ  viṣaya sambandha sañjāta viśeṣaḥ anubhavaḥ aparokṣa tayā sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭaḥ api kārakāṇām sambhūya pradhāna kriyā sādhana tvāt  yena saha sādhanam tad niṣṭha eva na anyatra karmakārakam api yena saha sādhanam tasya eva aparokṣam gantṛ sambandha iva grāmasya nanu nīla ādi viṣayaḥ api ced aparokṣa svabhāvaḥ nīla ātmikā saṃvid iti uktam syāt  atas  sa eva māhāyānika pakṣaḥ samarthitaḥ mā evam paraspara vyāvṛttau nīla pītau  avabhāsete aparokṣatā tu na tathā eka rūpa avagamāt viccheda avabhāse api atas  na tad svabhāva tā yadi syāt  tadvat eva vyāvṛtta svabhāva tā api avabhāseta na ca tathā kim ca taiḥ api nīla ātmaka saṃvidaḥ anya eva parāgvyāvṛttaḥ aparokṣaḥ pratyagavabhāsaḥ sva rūpa mātre paryavasitaḥ  vikalpa upeyate pratīyate ca nīla saṃvid  pratyak vyāvṛttet antayā grāhya rūpā tatas ca vastu dvayam grāhya grāhaka rūpam itaretara vyāvṛttam siddham na etad  dvayoḥ api sva rūpa mātra niṣṭhayoḥ kutaḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ katham punar  ‘idam aham jānāmī ati tayoḥ grāhya grāhaka tā avabhāsaḥ na ayam tad avabhāsaḥ kintu ‘aham i ati ‘idam i ati ‘jā nāmī ati ca paraspara vyāvṛttā vikalpā ete katham punar  teṣu kaṭākṣeṇa api anyonyam anīkṣamāṇeṣu ayam sambandha avagamaḥ tad vāsanā sameta sam anantara pratyaya samuttham saṅkalana ātmakam pratyaya antaram etad  na iha sambandha avagamaḥ kim punar  evam anubhavān ārūḍhām eva prakriyām viracayati bhavān   kṣaṇa vidhvaṃsinaḥ kriyā anupapatteḥ sthāyi tve hi sati aham ullekhyasya sthāyinā eva nīla ādinā kriyā nimittaḥ sambandhaḥ tatas ca kriyā nimitta eva nīla ādeḥ api aparokṣatā syāt  na ca sthāyi tvam asti yadi evam aaham i ati saṃvidaḥ pratikṣaṇam sva lakṣaṇa bhedena bhāvyam sa kim vidyate na vā iti sva saṃvidama gūha mānaiḥ eva abhidhīyatām   atha atyanta sādṛśyāt  na bhedaḥ avabhāsate iti saṃvidaḥ api ced  svarūpam na avabhāsate āyātam āndhyam aśeṣasya jagataḥ   api ca tad rūpa pratibhāse sādṛśya kalpanā pramāṇa viruddhā niṣpramāṇikā ca   tad rūpa pratīteḥ vyāmoha tvāt  na pramāṇa viruddha tā na api aprāmāṇika tā nirbīja bhrānti ayogāt iti ced  na itaretara āśraya tvāt siddhe vyāmohe sādṛśya siddhiḥ pramāṇa virodha abhāvāt pramāṇa sadbhāvāt ca siddhe ca sādṛśye tad nimittā vyāmoha siddhiḥ syāt etad  avyāmohe api tulyam etad  siddhe hi sādṛśya kalpanāyā aprāmāṇika tve pramāṇa virodhe ca tad rūpa pratīteḥ avyāmoha tvam avyāmoha tve ca asyāḥ sādṛśya kalpanāyāḥ niṣpramāṇaka tvam pramāṇa virodhaḥ ca na etad  svārasikam hi prāmāṇyam pratīteḥ anapekṣam tathā ca tad prāmāṇyāt sādṛśya kalpanā niṣprāmāṇikī pramāṇa viruddhā ca na tu sādṛśya kalpanā svatas siddhā yena prāmāṇyam āvahet  aprāmāṇya pūrvikā eva sā atha ante kṣaya darśana ādau kṣaya anumānam atas  bhinna tvāt  sādṛśya kalpanā iti ādau sattā darśanāt ante api sā kim na anumīyate kṣaya anubhava virodhāt iti ced  iha api tad rūpa sattvāt anubhava virodhaḥ na hi ubhayoḥ anubhavayoḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ   atha manyeta yaḥ asau sthira tvena abhimataḥ aham ullekhaḥ sa kim kāñcid artha kriyām kuryāt vā na vā yadi na kuryāt  asat lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ na parama artha vastu atha kuryāt  na tarhi sthāyī sthāyinaḥ artha kriyā yogāt katham ayogaḥ ittham ayogaḥ sa tām kurvan krameṇa kuryāt yaugapadyena vā na tāvat  krameṇa pūrva uttara kālayoḥ tasya viśeṣa abhāve api kim iti pūrvasmin  eva kāla uttara kāla bhāvinīm api na kuryāt  na api yaugapadyena yāvat jīva kṛtyam ekasmin  eva kṣaṇe kṛtam iti uttara kāle tad virahāt asat lakṣaṇatva prāpteḥ atas artha kriyā kāri tvāt eva na sthāyī tena pratikṣaṇam bhinneṣu aham ullekheṣu tad buddhiḥ sādṛśya nibandhana iti ucyate atha kā iyam artha kriyā yad abhāvāt asat lakṣaṇatva prāptiḥ sva viṣaya jñāna jananam prāptam tarhi sarvāsām eva saṃvidām sva saṃvidita rūpa tvena sva viṣaya jñāna ajananāt asat lakṣaṇa tvam na santāna antare api tad jananam anaindriyaka tvāt  anumāne api artha janyatva abhāvāt sārvajñye api na sākṣāt  sva saṃvidam janayati saṃsāra saṃvid eka rūpatva prasaṅgāt  atad rūpa tve tad viṣayatva ayogāt atha kṣaṇa antara utpādaḥ artha kriyā cara makṣaṇasya asat lakṣaṇatva prasaṅgaḥ na ca sarvajña jñāna jananena arthavat tvam caramatva anupapatteḥ mukti abhāva prasaṅgāt  na ca saṃvid saṃvidaḥ  viṣayaḥ saṃvid ātmanā bheda abhāvāt pradīpasya iva pradīpa antaram kiñca na artha kriyātaḥ sattvam bhavati sva kāraṇa niṣpannasya kārya jananāt  atas  pratītiḥ vaktavyā tatra tasyāḥ  anyatas  sattva pratītiḥ tasyāḥ  api anyatas  iti anavasthānāt na kvacid  sattān avagamaḥ iti śūnyam jagat abhaviṣyat  nanu sva jñāna artha kriyāyāḥ svayaṃsiddha tvāt na anavasthā na tarhi artha kriyātaḥ sattā avagamaḥ na hi svarūpam eva svasya artha kriyā yad  punar  krameṇa artha kriyā na yujyate pūrva uttara kālayoḥ tasya viśeṣa abhāvāt iti na eṣa doṣaḥ sthāyinaḥ api kāraṇasya sahakāri savyapekṣasya janakatvāt  viśeṣa abhāva āditya yuktam atha kāraṇasya anya apekṣā na yuktā akāraṇasya api natarāmiti asahakāri viśvam syāt  atha akāraṇam kāraṇa utpattaye apekṣata iti ced  atha tad  kāraṇasya kāraṇam akāraṇam vā kāraṇam ced  na apekṣitum arhati akāraṇam ced  natarām atha na apekṣā hetūnām sahakāriṇī iti brūyāt  darśanena bādhyeta dṛṣṭam hi sahakārya pekṣa tvam hetūnām tasmāt  yathā eva hetoḥ hetu tvam sati kārye kena api atarkaṇīyena krameṇa jñāyate sati eva hetau kāryasya darśanāt  tathā sameta saha kāriṇī eva darśanāt  sahakāri apekṣasya tad vijñeyam yaḥ tu manyate sahakāri janita viśeṣaḥ  hetuḥ kāryam janayati anyathā anupakāriṇaḥ apekṣā yogāt iti sa vaktavyaḥ viśeṣasya sa hetuḥ ahetuḥ vā ahetuḥ ced  viśeṣa utpattau na apekṣyeta tatra kevalā eva sahakāriṇaḥ  viśeṣam utpādayeyuḥ tatas ca kāryam syāt  atha hetuḥ sahakāribhiḥ ajanita viśeṣaḥ tam eva katham kuryāt  viśeṣasya vā janane anavasthā atha matam na sarvam kāryam sahakāri janita ātma bheda hetu janyam samagreṣu hetuṣu tāvatī eva abhavat aṅkura ādi tathā kiñcid sannihita sahakāri hetu janyam yathā akṣepakārī indriya ādi jñānam tatra ādyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ sahakāri sannidhāna mātra labhyaḥ akṣepakārī indriya ādi jñānavat iti na anavasthā anupakurvan  api tarhi sahakārī apekṣyeta na hi tatra hetoḥ sahakāribhya ātma bhedaḥ na anupakurvan  apekṣyate atiprasaṅgāt  svarūpe tu na upakaroti kintu kārye tad siddheḥ tad na āntarīyaka tvāt nityopi tarhi anādheya atiśayaḥ  bhāvaḥ kārya siddhaye kṣaṇika iva sahakāriṇam apekṣata iti kim na abhyupeyate yathā eva kṣaṇikaḥ  bhāvaḥ sahakāri samavadhāne eva kāryam janayati sāmagrī sādhya tvāt  tathā nityaḥ api svarūpa anupayogi tve api sahakāri samavadhānam kārya upayogāt apekṣeta atha matam kṣaṇikaḥ api na eva apekṣate janya janakasya svayam anya apekṣā anupapatteḥ kāryam tu yad anya sannidhau bhavati tad  tasya anya sannidhau  eva bhāvāt  anyathā ca abhāvāt  nityasya tu janakasya sarvadā janana prasaṅgaḥ kaḥ  hetuḥ anya apekṣāyāḥ kṣaṇikaḥ tu yaḥ  janakaḥ  bhāvaḥ sa na purastāt  na paścāt iti na pūrva uttara kālayoḥ kārya utpādaḥ idam ayuktam vartate   kim atra ayuktam sati niyame api nirapekṣa tvam tathā hi yaḥ kaścid  kasyacid  kvacid niyamaḥ sa tad apekṣā prabhāvitaḥ anapekṣa tve niyama anupapatteḥ evam hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ kārya arthibhiḥ ca viśiṣṭānām hetūnām upādānam tatra yadi na kṣaṇikam kāraṇam sahakāriṇam apekṣate na api tad  kāryam katham niyamaḥ tathā hi hetu paramparā pratibandhāt  na hetuḥ svarūpe sahakāriṇam apekṣate na kārye svayan janana śakteḥ na api kāryam ekasya api śaktimat tvena prasahya jananāt  tatra sahakāri sannidhi niyamaḥ anarthakaḥ syāt  kākatālīyam ucyate tathā ca kārya kāraṇa vyavahārāḥ sarva eva utsīdeyuḥ tasmāt  kṣaṇikasya api bhāvasya svayam janakasya svarūpa anupayoginī api sahakāriṇi kārya siddhaye apekṣā vācyā kāryasya eva vā sāmagrī sādhya tvāt  tatra niyamāt  tathā nitye api iti na viśeṣam paśyāmaḥ tad evam ahaṅkartuḥ sadā eka rūpa avagamāt sthāyi tve api artha kriyā sambhavāt na nīlasya sva gata aparokṣatva mātreṇa māhāyānika pakṣaḥ samarthyate kintu grāhakasya ahaṅkartuḥ ātmanaḥ sthāyinaḥ abhāve sa ca eka rūpaḥ anubhavāt  yukti balāt ca prasādhitaḥ nanu na anumeya ādiṣu aparokṣa tā dṛśyate ucyate na anumeya ādiṣu aparokṣa tvam sva jñāna utpattau  avyāpṛta tvāt liṅga ādīnām eva kutaścid  sambandha viśeṣāt viśiṣṭa eka artha jñāna hetu tvāt prameyasya ca sva jñāna utpatti hetu tve pramāṇa abhāvāt  alam prasaṅga āgata prapañcena sva avasara eva etad  sugata mata parīkṣāyām nipuṇataram prapañcayiṣyāmaḥ tad evam ahaṅkāra granthiḥ asmad śabda saṃśabditaḥ pratyayaḥ ca asau ādarśa iva pratibimbasya anidañcit samvalita tvena tasya abhivyakti hetu tvāt atas  tasya viṣayavat  bhavati iti upacāreṇa anidañcit ātma dhātuḥ asmad pratyaya viṣaya ucyate sa punar evaṃbhūtaḥ  jāgrat svapnayoḥ aham ullekha rūpeṇa suṣupte tad saṃskāra rañjita agrahaṇa avidyā pratibaddha prakāśa tvena ca gatāgatam ācaran saṃsārī jīvaḥ vijñāna ghanaḥ vijñāna ātmā prājñaḥ śarīrī śārīraḥ ātmā samprasādaḥ puruṣaḥ pratyagātmā kartā bhoktā kṣetrajñaḥ iti ca śruti smṛti pravādeṣu gīyate kiñca na kevalam asmad pratyaya viṣaya tvāt adhyāsa arhaḥ aparokṣa tvāt ca tad sādhana artham āha pratyagātma prasiddheḥ iti na hi ātmani aprasiddhe sva para saṃvedyayoḥ viśeṣaḥ na ca saṃvedya jñānena eva tad siddhiḥ akarma kāraka tvāt ati prasaṅgāt  na ca jñāna antareṇa bhinna kāla tve saṃvedya sambandhān avagamāt sva para saṃvedyā viśeṣāt na hi eka kālam viruddha viṣaya dvaya grāhi jñāna dvaya utpādaḥ na hi devadattasya agra pṛṣṭha deśa sthita artha vyāpi gamana kriyā dvaya āveśaḥ  yugapad  dṛśyate āha mā bhūt  calana ātmakam kriyā dvayam yugapad  pariṇāma ātmakam tu bhavati eva mā evam parispanda ātmakam api bhavati aviruddham yathā gāyan gacchati iti pariṇa ātmakam api na bhavati viruddham yathā yauvana sthāvira hetuḥ tasmāt  pratyagātmā svayam prasiddhaḥ sarvasya hāna upādāna avadhiḥ svayamaheyaḥ anupādeyaḥ sva mahimnā eva aparokṣa tvāt adhyāsa yogyaḥ nanu na kvacid aparokṣa mātre adhyāsaḥ  dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ sarvatra akṣi samprayogitayā purovasthita aparokṣa eva dṛśyate iti āśaṅkya āha na ca ayam asti niyamaḥ iti apratyakṣe api hi ākāśe iti parokṣe iti arthaḥ athavā akṣa vyāpāram antareṇa api aparokṣa ākāśe bālāḥ ayathārtha darśinaḥ talam indranīla tamāla patra sadṛśam malina tām ca dhūma ādikam anyat ca nīlotpala samāna varṇa tā ādi adhyasyanti evam aviruddhaḥ iti sambhāvanām nigamayati yathā ākāśasya akṣa vyā pāram antarā api parokṣa tā tathā darśayiṣyāmaḥ anu brahma vidyām anartha hetu nibarhaṇīm pratijānatā avidyā anartha hetuḥ sūcitā tatas  sā eva kartṛtva ādi anartha bījam upadarśanīyā kim idam adhyāsaḥ prapañcyate iti āśaṅkya āha tam etam evaṃlakṣaṇam adhyāsam paṇḍitāḥ pramāṇa kuśalāḥ ‘avidye ati manyante tad vivekena ca vastu svarūpa avadhāraṇam vidyām āhuḥ adhyastā tad rūpa sarpa vilayanam kurvat  vastu svarūpam rajjuḥ eva iti avadhārayat vijñānam vidyā iti prasiddham eva loke brahma vidaḥ  vadanti yadi evam adhyāsa iti prakramya punar tasya avidyā abhidhāna vyākhyāne yatna gauravāt  varam avidyā iti eva upakramaḥ kṛtaḥ na etad  sāram avidyā iti eva ucyamāna ācchādaka tvam nāma yad  tasyāḥ tattvam tad eva abhihitam syāt  na atad rūpa avabhāsitayā anartha hetu tvam atas atad rūpa avabhāsi tvam adhyāsa śabdena prakṛta upayogi tayā upakṣipya punar tayā avidyā śabda tayā vidyā mātra apanodana arha tvam darśanīyam tad etad āha yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tad kṛtena doṣeṇa guṇena vā aṇu mātreṇa api sa na sambadhyate iti avāstavam anartham darśayati vāstava tve hi ‘jñāna mātrāt tad vigamaḥ iti pratijñā hīyeta evam tāvat  ‘yuṣmad asmadi atyādinā ‘mithyā jñāna nimittaḥ satya anṛte mithunīkṛtya aham idam mama idam iti naisargikaḥ ayam loka vyavahāraḥ iti antena bhāṣyeṇa siddhavat upanyastam ātmānātmanoḥ ita retara viṣayam avidyā ākhyam adhyāsam siṣādhayiṣuḥ tasya lakṣaṇam abhidhāya tad sambhavam ca ātmani darśayitvā punar tatra sadbhāva niścayam upapattita upapādayitum icchan  āha tam etam avidyā ākhyam ātmānātmanoḥ ita retarādhyāsam puraskṛtya sarve pramāṇa prameya vyavahārā laukikā vaidikāḥ ca pravṛttāḥ sarvāṇi ca śāstrāṇi vidhi pratiṣedha mokṣa parāṇi iti mokṣa para tvam ca śāstrasya vidhi pratiṣedha virahita tayā upādāna parityāga śūnya tvāt sva rūpa mātra niṣṭha tvam aṅgīkṛtya pṛthak  kriyate katham punar avidyāvat viṣayāṇi pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni śāstrāṇi ca iti bāḍha mukta lakṣaṇā avidyā pratyak dṛśyapi sambhavet  na etāvatā tad sambhavaḥ sidhyati tena nidarśanīyaḥ saḥ pramātāram āśrayanti pramāṇāni tena pramātā pramāṇānām āśrayaḥ na avidyāvān anupayogāt iti abhiprāyaḥ athavā katham avidyāvat viṣayāṇi pratyakṣa ādīni śāstrāṇi ca pramāṇāni iti sambandhaḥ avidyāvat viṣaya tve sati āśraya doṣa anugamāt apramāṇāni eva syuḥ iti ākṣepaḥ ucyate deha indriya ādiṣu ahaṃmama abhimāna hīnasya pramātṛtva anupapattau pramāṇa pravṛtti anupapatteḥ iti bhāṣya kārasya vastu saṅgraha vākyam asya eva prapañcaḥ ‘nahi indriyāṇi anupādāye atyādiḥ na hi deha indriya ādiṣu aham mama abhimāna hīnasya suṣuptasya pramātṛ tvam dṛśyate yatas  dehe aham abhimānaḥ indriya ādiṣu mama abhimānaḥ ādi śabdena bāhu ādi avayava grahaṇam deha śabdena sa śiraskaḥ  manuṣyatva ādi jāti sambhinnaḥ avayavi abhimataḥ na śarīra mātram dehaḥ aham iti pratīti abhāvāt  sarvaḥ  hi ‘manuṣyaḥ aham ‘devaḥ aham i ati jāti viśeṣa eka adhikaraṇa caitanya eva pravartata iti sva sākṣikam etad  na sva tvena sambandhinā manuṣya avayavinā tad anusyūtena vā cakṣuḥ ādinā pramātṛ ādi vyavahāraḥ sidhyati bhṛtya ādi manuṣya avayavinā api prasaṅgāt  apara āha ātma icchā anuvidhāyi tvam kārya karaṇa saṅghātasya ātmanā sambandhaḥ tasya api tasya yathā iṣṭa viniyojaka tvam tena sambandhaḥ tatas  ātmanaḥ pramātṛ ādikaḥ sarvaḥ kriyā kāraka phala vyavahāraḥ tathā ca uttiṣṭhāmi iti icchayā uttiṣṭhati upaviśati ca na ca bhṛtya ādiṣu tad asti tena tatra pramātṛ ādi vyavahāra abhāvaḥ  na mithyāmukhya abhimāna abhāvāt iti na etad  saṃvidi bahu mānavataḥ  yuktam tathā hi ‘manuṣyaḥ aham i ati sva sākṣikā saṃvid  ‘na me manuṣyaḥ iti gauṇī iti ced  bhavān eva atra pramāṇam api ca icchā api pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ sa katham apariṇāmina ātmanaḥ syāt  pariṇāmi antaḥkaraṇa samvalita ahaṅkartṛ tvam antareṇa tathā ca anubhavaḥ ‘aham uttiṣṭhāmī ati icchayā uttiṣṭhati upaviśati ca tasmāt  yad kiñcid etad  atas  svayam asaṅgasya avikāriṇaḥ avidyā dhyāsam antareṇa na pramātṛ tvam upapadyate tena yadi api pramātṛtva śakti sanmātram pramāṇa pravṛttau nimittam tad eva tu avidyā dhyāsa vilasitam iti avidyāvat viṣaya tā pramāṇānām ucyate tathā nirapekṣāṇām sva sāmarthyena artha siddhim vidadhatām bādha anupalabdheḥ prāmāṇyam avidyāvat viṣaya tvam ca vidhi mukha upadarśitam ‘na ne ati śakyam apahnotum doṣaḥ tu āgantuka eva mithyātve hetuḥ na naisargikaḥ tathā upalabdheḥ na ca sarva sādhāraṇe naisargike doṣa buddhiḥ tathā hi kṣudh pipāsā upajanite santāpe śaśvat anuvartamāne jāṭhara agni kṛta vikāre anna pāna niṣyande vā na roga buddhiḥ janasya muhūrta mātra parivartini mande jvare pratiśyāye vā alpa kapha prasūtau  api roga buddhiḥ anaisargika tvāt  anaisargikam ca doṣam abhipretya uktam ‘yasya ca duṣṭam karaṇam yatra ca mithyā iti pratyayaḥ sa eva asamīcīnaḥ pratyayaḥ na anyaḥ iti itas ca etad evam paśu ādibhiḥ ca aviśeṣāt tathā ca paśu ādayaḥ pramātṛtva ādi vyavahāra kāle pravṛtti nivṛtti audāsīnyam bhajamānāḥ kārya kāraṇa saṅghāta eva āhaṃmānam kurvanti iti prasiddham loke tad eka rūpa yogakṣemā hi manuṣyā janmata eva paśu ādibhyaḥ adhikatara viveka matayaḥ śāstra ādheya sāmparāyikam ati sāmarthyā api atas  tad eka rūpa kārya darśanāt kārya kāraṇa saṅghāte api ātma abhimānaḥ samānaḥ  yuktaḥ nanu paśu ādīnām api kārya kāraṇa saṅghāte ahaṅkāra anubandha iti kutas avasīyate yena siddhavat abhidhīyate ucyate prauḍham atibhya eva pratyakṣa ādi vṛtta kuśalaiḥ ātmā vyutpādyate anyathā tad anarthakatva prasaṅgāt  evam eva pramāṇa vicāra viraham sarvaḥ sampratipadyeta nanu gopāla aṅganā ādayaḥ pramāṇa viraham eva vartamāna deha pāte api sthāyinam bhoktāram manyamānāḥ tad artham ācaranti na tad abhijña vyavahāra mātra pramāṇaka tvāt  tathā ca te pṛṣṭāḥ kaḥ para loka sambandhī iti ‘na vidmaḥ  viśeṣataḥ prasiddhaḥ  loke iti pratibruvanti tasmāt  yuktam uktam paśu ādīnām ca prasiddhaḥ aviveka pūrvakaḥ pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad sāmānya darśanāt  vyutpattimatām api puruṣāṇām pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad kālaḥ samānaḥ iti evam tāvat  pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni cakṣuḥ ādi sādhanāni tāni ca na adhiṣṭhāna śūnyāni vyāpriyante adhiṣṭhānam ca dehaḥ na tena anadhyastātma bhāvena āsaṅgasya avikāriṇaḥ caitanya eka rasasya ātmanaḥ pramātṛ tvam upapadyate iti anubhava ārūḍham avidyāvat viṣaya tvam pratyakṣa ādīnām upadiśya paśu ādi vyavahāra sāmyena kāryataḥ api āpādya śāstram punar  pratipanna ātma viṣayam eva tena na tatra adhyāsa pūrvikā pravṛttiḥ iti viśeṣam āśaṅkya tasya api avidyāvat viṣayatva pradarśanāya āha śāstrīye tu vyavahāre yadi api buddhi pūrva kārī na aviditvā ātmanaḥ para loka sambandham adhikriyate iti nanu phala naiyamika naimittika prāyaścitta codanā vartamāna śarīra pātāt ūrdhva kāla sthāyinam bhoktāram antareṇa api pramāṇa tām aśnuvata eva yathā ca etad evam tathā ‘eka ātmanaḥ śarīre bhāvāt iti adhikaraṇa ārambhe darśayiṣyāmaḥ satyam evam tathā api sakala śāstra paryālocanā pariniṣpannam prāmāṇikam artham aṅgīkṛtya āha bhāṣya kāraḥ tathā ca vidhi vṛtta mīmāṃsā bhāṣya kāraḥ api utsūtram eva ātma siddhau parākrāntavān tad  kasya hetoḥ ‘dharma jijñāse ati kārya artha vicāram pratijñāya tad avagamasya prāmāṇye anapekṣa tvam kāraṇam anusara tā sūtrakāreṇa viśeṣa abhāvāt sva rūpa niṣṭhānām api vākyānām prāmāṇyam anusṛtam manyate tathā ‘codanā hi bhūtam bhavantam bhaviṣyantam sūkṣmam vyavahitam viprakṛṣṭam iti evaṃjātīyakam artham śaknoti avagamayitum iti vadan codanā śeṣa tvena api svarūpa avagame anapekṣa tvam aviśiṣṭam avagacchati iti avagamyate sa ca svarūpa avagamaḥ kasmin katham vā iti dharma mātra vicāram pratijñāya tatra eva prayatamānena bhagavatā jaimininā na mīmāṃsitam upayoga abhāvāt bhagavān  tu punar bādarāyaṇaḥ pṛthak  vicāram pratijñāya vyacīcarat  samanvaya lakṣaṇena tatra ca deha antara upabhogyaḥ svargaḥ sthāsyati tad ca sarvam kārya karaṇa saṅghātāt anyena bhoktrā vinā na sidhyati tad siddhiḥ ca na āgama mātra āyattā pramāṇa antara gocarasya tad abhāve tad virodhe vā śilā plavana vākyavat aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt  atas tad siddhau parākrāntavān tena satyam vinā api tena sidhyet  prāmāṇyam asti tu tad  tasmin vidyamāne na tena vinā pramāṇyam sidhyati phala ādi codanānām iti matvā āha śāstrīye tu vyavahāre yadi api vidyamāne buddhi pūrva kārī na aviditvā ātmanaḥ para loka sambandham adhikriyate iti tathā api na vedānta vedyam iti kim tad iti ata āha asaṃsārya ātmata tvam na tad  adhikāre apekṣyate anupayogāt adhikāra virodhāt ca aśanāya ādi atītam iti asaṃsārya ātma tattvam darśayati aśanāya ādi upaplutaḥ  hi sarvaḥ  jantuḥ svāsthyam alabhamānaḥ pravartate tad apāye svāsthye sthitaḥ  na kiñcid upādeyam heyam vā paśyati apeta brahma kṣatra ādi bhedam iti prapañca śūnyam eka rasam darśayati prāk  ca tathābhūta ātma vijñānāt pravartamānam śāstram avidyāvat viṣaya tvam na ativartate iti ‘tattvam asī ati vākya artha  agamāt arvāk vidyā kṛtam saṃsāram aham ullekham āśritya pravartamānam śāstram na avidyāvat viṣaya tvam ativartate tasmāt  yuktam uktam pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇānām śāstrasya ca avidyāvat viṣaya tvam tad eva darśayati tathā hi ‘brāhmaṇaḥ  yajete atyādīni śāstrāṇi ātmani atadadhyāsam āśritya pravartante varṇavayaḥ adhyāsaḥ ‘aṣṭa varṣam brāhmaṇam upanaya nīte atyādiḥ āśrama adhyāsaḥ ‘na ha vai snātvā bhikṣete ati avasthā adhyāsaḥ ‘yaḥ  jyok āmayāvī syāt  sa etām iṣṭim nirvapedi ati ādi śabdena‘yāvat jīvam juhuyādi ati jīvana adhyāsaḥ evam adhyāsa sadbhāvam prasādhya ‘smṛti rūpaḥ ityādinā ‘sarvathā api tu anyasya anya dharma avabhāsa tām na vyabhicarati iti antena sarvathā api lakṣitam nirupacaritam atat āropam adhyāsaḥ  nāma atasmin  tad buddhiḥ iti avocām iti parāmṛśati kasya yuṣmad arthasya kasmin  asmad arthe tad viparyayeṇa ca adhyāsaḥ iti vivekataḥ pradarśayitum atasmin ayuṣmad arthe anidañciti tad buddhiḥ yuṣmad artha avabhāsaḥ iti arthaḥ tad āha tad yathā putra bhārī ādiṣu ityādi nanu praṇava eva visvaraḥ na hi putra ādīnām vaikalyam sākalyam vā ātmani mukhya madhyasyati mukhyaḥ  hi atadāropaḥ  darśayitum prārabdhaḥ satyam sa eva nidarśyate katham tad yathā bālake prātiveśya mātra sambandhinā kenacid  vastra alaṅkāra ādinā pūjite nirupacaritam ātmānam eva pūjitam manyate pitā pūjayitā api pitaram eva apūpujam iti manyate yatas  na bālakasya pūjitatva abhimānaḥ avyakta tvāt  tathā eva rājānam upahantu kāmaḥ anantaraḥ  vijigīṣuḥ tad rāṣṭre grāma mātram api upahatya tam eva upaghnantam ātmānam manyate saḥ api upahataḥ asmi iti santapyate tad evam prasiddha vyatirekasya ātmani mukhya  eva adhyāsaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ kim u vaktavyam kṛśa sthūla ādi abhimānasya mukhya tvam iti kathayitum āha aham eva vikalaḥ sakalaḥ  vā iti bāhya dharmān ātmani adhyasyati iti bāhyeṣu putra ādiṣu pūjā ādeḥ dharma mātrasya eva yuṣmad arthasya adhyāsaḥ asmad arthaḥ ca ahaṃpratyayi sambhinna eva anidañcidaṃśaḥ  viṣayaḥ na punar  śuddha eva ahaṃpratyayina iva adhyāse adhyāsa antarānā skanditaḥ tathā deha dharmān kṛśatva ādīn iti dharmiṇaḥ api dharma śabdaḥ tu manuṣyatva ādi dharma samavāyina eva adhyāsaḥ na ‘dehaḥ aham i ati kathayitum tad nimittaḥ ca śāstreṇa itas ca itaḥ ca niyamaḥ kriyate tathā indriya dharmān mūkatva ādīn iti dharma mātram tathā antaḥkaraṇa dharmān kāma ādīn iti dharma grahaṇam antaḥkaraṇam iti ahaṃpratyayinaḥ vijñāna śakti bhāgaḥ abhidhīyate tasya dharmāḥ kāma ādayaḥ evam ahaṃpratyayinam iti dharmi grahaṇam pratyayāḥ kāma ādayaḥ asya iti pratyayī aham ca asau pratyayī ca iti ahaṃpratyayī tam aśeṣa sva pracāra sākṣiṇi pratyak ātmani adhi asya iti sva śabdena ahaṅkāra granthiḥ saṃsāra nṛtya śālāmūla stambhaḥ abhidhīyate tasya pracāraḥ kāma ssaṅkalpa kartṛtva ādiḥ anekavidhaḥ pariṇāmaḥ yad nimittam brahma ādi sthāvara anteṣu pradīpta śirāḥ  iva para vaśaḥ  jantuḥ bambhrami iti tam pracāram aśeṣam asaṅgitayā avikāri tvena ca hāna upādāna śūnyaḥ sākṣāt avyavadhānam avabhāsayati citidhātuḥ sa eva deha ādiṣu idantayā bahis bhāvam āpadyamāneṣu prātilomyena añcatī iva upalakṣyate iti pratyak ucyate ātmā ca nirupacarita svarūpa tvāt tatra adhyasya tam ca pratyagātmānam iti yadi yuṣmad arthasya eva pratyagātmani adhyāsaḥ syāt  pratyagātmā na prakāśeta na hi śuktau rajata adhyāse śuktiḥ prakāśate prakāśate ca iha caitanyam ahaṅkāra ādau tathā yadi caitanyasya eva ahaṅkāra ādau  adhyāsaḥ  bhavet tadā na ahaṅkāra pramukhaḥ prapañcaḥ prakāśeta tad ubhayam mā bhūt iti anubhavam eva anusaran  āha tam ca pratyak ātmānam sarva sākṣiṇam tad viparyayeṇa antaḥkaraṇa ādiṣu adhyasyati iti na atra vivaditavyam itaretara adhyāse pṛthak avabhāsanāt  na mithyā gauṇaḥ ayam iti tathā anubhava abhāvāt  mukhya abhimānaḥ na hi dṛṣṭe anupapannam nāma nanu antaḥkaraṇe eva pratyak ātmanaḥ śuddhasya adhyāsaḥ anyatra punar  caitanya adhyāsa pariniṣpanna aparokṣyam antaḥkaraṇam eva adhyasyate ata eva ‘tad viparyayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ tad dharmāṇām ca viṣaye adhyāsaḥ  mithyā iti bhavitum yuktam iti uktam anyathā caitanya mātra eka rasasya kutaḥ dharmāḥ ye adhyasyeran satyam āha bhavān api tu anyatra antaḥkaraṇam sa citkam eva adhyasyamānam yatra adhyasyate tasya eva ātmanaḥ kārya karaṇa tvam āpādya svayam avidyamānam iva tiraskṛtam tiṣṭhati cit rūpam eva sarvatra adhyāse svatas  paratas  vā na viśiṣyate tena ucyate tam ca pratyak ātmānam sarva sākṣiṇam tad viparyayeṇa antaḥkaraṇa ādiṣu adhyasyati iti ata eva buddhi ādiṣu eva cit rūpam anusyūtam utprekṣamāṇā buddhi manaḥ prāṇa indriya śarīreṣu ekaikasmin cetana tvena ahaṅkartṛ tvam yojayantaḥ  bhrāmyanti evam ayam anādiḥ anantaḥ  naisargikaḥ adhyāsa iti nigamayati nanu upanyāsa kāle naisargikaḥ ayam loka vyavahāra iti loka vyavahāraḥ  naisargika uktaḥ katham iha adhyāsaḥ  nigamyate anādiḥ iti ca adhika āvāpaḥ atra ucyate tatra api pratyak ātmani ahaṅkāra adhyāsa eva naisargi kaḥ  loka vyavahāraḥ abhipretaḥ sa ca pratyagātmā anādi siddhaḥ tasmin naisargikasya anādi tvam artha siddham atas  prakrama anurūpam eva nigamanam na ca adhika āvāpaḥ nanu bhavet anādiḥ anantaḥ katham yadi syāt tad prahāṇāya katham vedāntā ārabhyante antavat tve api tarhi katham svatas anyatas  vā tad siddheḥ tasmāt  anantasya prahāṇāya vedāntā ārabhyante iti ukte arthāt eṣa eva prahāṇa hetuḥ asati asmin anantaḥ iti niścīyate ‘mithyā pratyaya rūpa iti rūpa grahaṇam lakṣaṇataḥ tathā rūpyate na vyavahārataḥ iti darśayitum ‘kartṛtva bhoktṛtva pravartakaḥ iti anartha hetu tvam darśayati heya tā siddhaye tena kartṛḥ bhoktuḥ ca sataḥ  mithyājñānam doṣa pravartanam iti yeṣām matam tad nirākṛtam bhavati sarva loka pratyakṣaḥ iti ‘deha indriya ādiṣu ahaṃmama abhimāna hīnasye ati upanyasya‘nahi indriyāṇi anupādāye atyādinā yaḥ anubhavaḥ  mithyātva siddhaye anusṛtaḥ tam nigamayati evam tāvat  sūtreṇa arthāt upāttayoḥ viṣaya prayojanayoḥ siddhaye jīvasya abrahma svarūpa tvam adhyāsa ātmakam upadarśya asya anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāya iti prayojanam nirdiśati hetoḥ prahāṇyā hi hetumataḥ prahāṇiḥ ātyantikī yatas  nanu anartha hetuḥ adhyāsaḥ anādiḥ sa katham prahīyate tathā hi manuṣya ādi jāti viśeṣa mātra adhyāsaḥ tatas  vivikte api nyāyataḥ ahaṃpratyaye anādi tvāt  pūrvavat avikalaḥ  vartate na ayam doṣaḥ tad tvam asi ityādi vākyāt brahma rūpa avagāhi jñāna antara utpatteḥ iṣṭa tvāt  tad hi brahmaṇaḥ avacchidya eva caitanyasya brahma rūpatva pracchādanena jīva rūpatva apādi kāmana ādi siddhām avidyām ahaṅkāra ādi vikṣepa hetum nirākurvat eva utpadyate tatas  kāraṇa nivṛttau tad kāryam ‘aham i ati jīve bhoktṛtva rūpa tā sa parikarā nivartata iti yujyate ahaṃpratyayaḥ punar anādi siddhaḥ anādi siddhena eva kārya karaṇa mātreṇa sahabhāvāt avirodhāt  na sva rūpa viveka mātreṇa nivartate na api jñāna antaram utpannam iti viśeṣaḥ nanu niratiśaya ānandam brahma śrūyate brahma avāpti sādhanam ca brahma vidyā ‘sa yaḥ  ha vai tad  paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavatī atyādi śrutibhyaḥ tasmāt niratiśaya sukha avāptaya iti vaktavyam kim idam ucyate ‘anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāye ati nanu ca anarthasya api sa mūlasya prahāṇam śrūyate brahma vidyā phalam ‘tarati śokam ātma vit ‘juṣṭam yadā paśyati anyam īśam asya mahimānam iti vīta śokaḥ iti ca ubhayam tarhi vaktavyam śrūyamāṇa tvāt  puruṣa artha tvāt ca na vaktavyam katham ‘a ātmā ekatva vidyā pratipattaye iti ātmanaḥ  jīvasya brahma ātmaka tā śāstrasya viṣayaḥ tena ānanda ātmaka brahma svarūpa tā prāptiḥ jīvasya viṣaya tayā eva saṃvṛttā na ca sā viṣayāt bahis  yena pṛthak nideśa arhā syāt  sa mūla anartha hāniḥ tu bahis  śāstra viṣayāt brahma ātma rūpāt anartha hetu prahāṇam api tarhi na pṛthak nirdeṣṭavyam yatas  sarveṣu vedānteṣu alaukika tvāt brahmaṇaḥ tad pratipādana pūrvakam eva jīvasya tad rūpa tā pratipādyate tad yathā ‘sat eva somya idam agra āsīdi ati upakramya ‘a etad ātmyam idam sarvam tad  satyam sa ātme atyavasānam nirasta samasta prapañcam vastu tad pada abhidheyam samarpayat ekam vākyam tathā sati tādṛśena tad padārthena saṃsṛjyamānaḥ tvampadārthaḥ parākṛtya eva nirlepam anartha hetum agrahaṇam anyathā grahaṇam ca tathā niścīyata iti yadi evam brahma ātmā avagatinā antarīyakam anartha hetoḥ avidyāyāḥ prahāṇam na śabdasya tatra vyāpāraḥ tena pṛthaṅinardiśyate yuktam ca etad  na hi viparyāsa gṛhītam vastu tad nirāsāt ṛte tattvataḥ  nirṇetum śakyam tasmāt  pūrva avasitam atad dharmam nirasyadeva tattva avadyoti vākyam tattvam avasāyayati nanu ca naña ādeḥ nirāsa kṛtaḥ  nirasyamāna vācinaḥ ca padasya aśravaṇāt katham tad nirasyadeva iti ucyate na idam rajatam iti yatra viparyāsa mātram nirasyate na vastu tattvam avabodhyate tatra tathā bhavatu iha punar  vijñānam eva tādṛśam utpannam yad  virodhi nirākaraṇam antareṇa na sva artham sādhayitum alam tulā unnamana vyāpāra iva ānamananā antarīyakaḥ tathā hi unnamana vyāpāraḥ sva viṣayasya tulā dravyasya ūrdhva deśa sambandham na sādhayitum alam tad kālam eva tasya adhas deśa sambandham anāpādya na ca unnamana kārakasya hasta prayatna ādeḥ ānamane api kāraka tvam prasiddhi abhāvāt anubhava virodhāt ca tad evam viparyāsa gṛhīte vastuni tattva avadyoti śabda nimitta ātmanaḥ  jñāna vyāpāraḥ  ‘nā aham kartā brahmā ahami ati grāhayati ‘nedam rajatam śuktikā iyam i ati yathā tasmāt  ‘śuktikeyam i ati eva nirākāṅkṣam vākyam ‘nedam rajatami atyanuvādaḥ ata eva ākhyāta padasya vākya tve kriyā jñānāt eva tad sādhana mātre api pratīti siddheḥ pada antarāṇi niyamāya anuvādāya vā iti nyāya vidaḥ tathā ca āhuḥ ‘yajati codanā dravya devatā kriyam samudāye kṛtārthatva ādi ati apare tu ‘yajñam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ  dravyam devatā tyāgaḥ iti katham kriyā mātra vācinaḥ  dravya devatā abhidhānam na āntarīyakam tad viṣaya jñāna nimitta tvam vihāya pratyakṣa bādhasya api ayam eva prakāraḥ asamprayukta viṣaya tvāt bādhasya tad evam aśābdam avidyā vilayam manvānaḥ śruti nyāya kovidaḥ  bhagavān bhāṣya kāraḥ  viṣayāt  pṛthak  nirdiśati asya anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāya iti caturthī prayogaḥ api vidyā sāmarthya siddhim abhipretya na tad artham upādānam prayojana tvam ca puruṣa ākāṅkṣāyā eva astu na hi vidyā gavā ādivat  taṭasthā sidhyati yena āptiḥ pṛthak upādīyeta sā hi veditra āśrayā vedyam tasmai prakāśayanti eva udeti satyam evam anyatra prakṛte punar viṣaye vidyā uditā api na pratiṣṭhām labhate asambhāvana abhibhūta viṣaya tvāt tathā ca loke asmin deśe kāle ca idam vastu svarūpata eva na sambhavati iti dṛḍha bhāvitam yadi tad  katham cit  daiva vaśāt upalabhyeta tadā svayam īkṣamāṇaḥ api tāvat na adhyavasyati yāvat  tad sambhavam na anusarati tena samyak jñānam api sva viṣaye apratiṣṭhitam anavāptam iva bhavati tena tad svarūpa pratiṣṭhāyai tarkam sahāyīkaroti ata eva pramāṇānām anugrāhakaḥ tarkaḥ iti tarka vidaḥ atha kaḥ ayam tarkaḥ  nāma yuktiḥ nanu paryāya eṣaḥ sva rūpam abhidhīyatām idam ucyate pramāṇa śakti viṣaya tad sambhava pariccheda ātmā pratyayaḥ nanu evam tarkasa apekṣam svam artham sādhayataḥ anapekṣatva hāneḥ aprāmāṇyam syāt  na syāt  sva mahimnā eva viṣaya adhyavasāya hetutvāt  kva tarhi tarkasya upayogaḥ viṣaya asambhava āśaṅkāyām tathā anubhava phala anutpattau tad sambhava pradarśana mukhena phala pratibandha vigame tathā ca tattvam asi vākye tvam padārthaḥ  jīvaḥ tad padārtha brahma svarūpa tām ātmanaḥ asambhāvayan viparītam ca rūpam manvānaḥ samutpanne api jñāne tāvat  na adhyavasyati yāvat tarkeṇa virodham apanīya tad rūpa tām ātmanaḥ  na sambhāvayati atas  prāk  vidyā uditā api vākyāt  anavāptā iva bhavati avāpti prakāraḥ ca vedānteṣu eva nirdiṣṭaḥ sākṣāt anubhava phala uddeśena tena ucyate vidyā pratipattaye iti nanu ātmā ekatva vidyā pratipattiḥ na anartha hetu prahāṇāya prabhavati tathā hi jīvasya kārya kāraṇa saṅghātāt anyatva pratipatteḥ brahma svarūpa tā pratipattiḥ na viśiṣyate ubhayatra api ahaṅkāra grantheḥ manuṣya abhimāna paryantasya avikalam anuvartamāna tvāt ucyate bhavatu tatra avidyāyā anivartita tvāt  tad  iha punar apasārita avidyā doṣam brahma ātma jñānam udayam āsādayat  katham tad nimittam bhoktrādi granthi pravāham na apanayati na hi jīvasya brahma ātmā avagamaḥ tad viṣayānavagamamabādhamānaḥ udeti nanu brahma jñānāt agrahaṇa apāye tad nimittasya ahaṅkāra grantheḥ tad kālam eva abhāvaḥ prasajyeta na saṃskārāt api agrahaṇa anuvṛtteḥ sambhavāt  bhaya anuvṛttivat  tathā hi samyak jñānāt  nivṛttam api bhayam sva saṃskārāt anuvartate kampa ādi nimittam ca bhavati tathā grahaṇam api sva saṃskārāt anuvartate ahaṅkāra grantheḥ ca nimittam bhavati iti na kiñcid anupapannam asti nanu na sarve vedāntā vidyā artham eva ārabhyante tad eka deśaḥ krama mukti phalāya aiśvaryāya abhyudaya artham karma samṛddhaye ca upāsanāni vividhāni upadiśan upalabhyate satyam upāsana akarma tu brahma tad ca apākṛta aśeṣa prapañcam jīvasya nijam rūpam iti nirūpayitum akhila prapañca janma ādi hetu tayā prathamam sarva ātmakam sarvajñam sarva śakti ca brahma lakṣitam asyām ca avasthāyām anapākṛtya eva brahmaṇi prapañcam tena tena prapañcena upadhīyamānam brahma tasmai tasmai phalāya upāsya tvena vidhīyate darśa pūrṇamāsa arthāḥ praṇayanam iva gaḥ dohana uparaktam paśubhyaḥ tasmāt  tad artha upajīvitvāditarasya ātmā ekatva vidyā pratipattaye sarve vedāntā ārabhyanta iti na virudhyate nanu abrahma upāsanāni api vedānteṣu dṛśyante prāṇa ādi viṣayāṇi satyam tāni api kārya brahma avāpti krameṇa mukti phalāni eva vakṣyati etad  sūtra kāraḥ ‘kārya atyaye tad adhyakṣeṇa sahātas  param abhidhānāt iti yathā ca ayam arthaḥ sarveṣām vedāntānām tathā vayam asyām śārīrakamīmāṃsāyām pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ iti pratijñāte arthe vedāntānām tātparyam upadarśayitum samanvaya sūtra pramukhaiḥ sūtra vākyaiḥ grathitaḥ  nyāyaḥ iti darśayati śarīram eva śarīrakam śarīrake bhavaḥ śārīrakaḥ  jīvaḥ tam adhikṛtya kṛtaḥ  granthaḥ śārīrakaḥ tad iha vedāntānām jīvasya tattvam adhikṛtya pravṛttānām brahma rūpa tāyām paryavasānam iti kathayitum praṇītānām śārīrakam jīva tattvam adhikṛtya kṛta tvam asti iti śārīraka abhidhānam mumukṣu tve sati anantaram brahma jñānam kartavyam iti yadi api etāvān sūtrasya śrautaḥ arthaḥ tathā api arthāt  brahma jñānasya mokṣaḥ prayojanam nirdiṣṭam bhavati tathā hi puruṣa artha vastu kāmanā anantaram yatra pravṛttiḥ upadiśyate tasya tad sādhana tvam api arthān nirdiṣṭam pratīyate tathā sati kutas  tad  mokṣa sādhanam brahma jñānam bhavati iti apekṣāyām arthāt  asmāt śāstrāt bhavati iti śāstrasya brahma jñānam viṣayaḥ  nirdiṣṭaḥ tad evam mumukṣu tvā anantaram brahma jñāna kartavyatā upadeśa mukhena
