vedāntānām viṣaya prayojana nirdeśe api ārtham sūtrasya vyāpāram darśayitvā tad apekṣitam api arthāt  sūtritam avidyā ātmaka bandham uparvaṇya pratijñāta artha siddhaye hetu ākāṅkṣāyām asmin  eva tam pradarśayiṣyāma iti vyākhyeya tvam upakṣipya vyākhyātu kāmaḥ prathamam tāvat  prayojana viṣayayoḥ upādāne nimittam āha vedāntamī māṃsā śāstrasya vyāci khya asitasya idam ādimam sūtram atha atas  brahma jijñāsā iti ayam asya arthaḥ śāstrasya ādiḥ ayam ādau ca pravṛtti aṅga tayā prayojanam viṣayaḥ ca darśanīyaḥ sūtram ca etad  atas  yaḥ kaścid arthaḥ śabda sāmarthyena artha balāt vā utprekṣitaḥ sa sarvaḥ tad artham eva iti bhavati ayam artha kalāpaḥ tad mahima adhigataḥ evam sūtrasya ādi tvena kāraṇena sūtra tayā ca viṣaya prayojanam tad siddhi karam ca avidyā ākhyam bandham tad sāmarthya avagatam āpādya tatra sūtra sāmarthyam darśayitum pratipadam vyākhyām ārabhyate tha dvitīya varṇakam siddhā eva nanu brahma jijñāsā ‘atha atas  dharma aji jñāse ati sakala veda artha vicārasya udita tvāt brahma jñānasya ca codanā lakṣaṇa tvena dharma svarūpa tvāt atas  siddhā eva brahma jijñāsā api abhyadhika āśaṅkā bhāvāt iti atra kecid abhyadhika āśaṅkām darśayantaḥ  brahma jijñāsām pṛthak  ārabhante kā iyam atra abhyadhikā śaṅkā codanā lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ  dharmaḥ iti bruvatā vidheḥ prāmāṇyam darśitam atra keṣucid vākyeṣu vidhiḥ eva na śrūyate ‘sat eva somya idam agra āsīt u iti evamādiṣu yatra api vidhiḥ śrūyate ‘a ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ ‘tasmin yad antar tad anveṣṭavyam tad vāva vijijñāsitavyam u iti tatra yadi api kṛtyā aviśeṣeṇa vidhau smaryante tathā api yaḥ  bhāva abhidhāyī tavya pratyayaḥ sa kriyāyām puruṣam niyoktum śaknoti yatra punar  karma prādhānyena ucyate tatra dravye guṇa bhūtām kriyām na kārya antara sambandhi tvena vidhātum śaknoti dravya paratve ca anutpādya tvāt  avikārya tvāt  anāpya tvāt  asaṃskārya tvāt  saṃskṛtasya ca kārya antare upayoga abhāvāt asaṃskārya tvam atas  ‘a ātmānam upāsīte ati ātmana īpsitatama tvam na sambhavati atha punar viparītaḥ  guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ saktu nyāyena kalpyeta tatra api na jñāyate kim tad upāsanam katham ca ātmanā tad  kriyata iti atha jñāyate jñānam upāsanam ātmā ca viṣaya bhāvena tad nirvartayati iti evam tarhi tad eva āyātam jñānena ātmā apyata iti tad ca kṛta karaṇam anarthakam nitya āpta tvāt ātmanaḥ saṃskārya tve ca upayoga abhāva uktaḥ atas  vidhi abhāvāt avivakṣita arthā vedāntāḥ iti dharma jijñāsā anantaram snāne prāpta idam ārabhyate atha atas  brahma jijñāsā iti anantaram brahma jijñāsitavyam na snātavyam iti abhiprāyaḥ karma abhidhāyinaḥ api kṛtya pratyayāt niyoga saṃpratyayāt na niyoktṛ tvam nirākartum śakyate ‘kaṭaḥ tvayā kartavyaḥ ‘grāmaḥ tvayā gantavyaḥ itivat  yad tu uktam dravya paratve prayojana abhāvāt ānarthakyam niyogasya iti tad asat  avidyā ucchet asya upalabhyamāna tvāt  avidyā ca saṃsāra hetu bhūtā apare punar evam ārabhante brahmaṇi pratyakṣa ādi pratyaya antarāṇām asambhavāt  pariniṣpanne vastuni pratipatti hetu tayā sambhāvita sāmarthyānām api āmnāyasya punar  kārya viṣaya tayā sutarām asambhavam manvānasya bhavati saṅkarṣa paryante eva veda artha vicāra avasānām iti buddhiḥ tad nirāsa artham punar  pratijñātam iha api sarveṣu eva ātma jñāna vidhāneṣu kārya niṣṭhatām varṇayanti samām tattva avabodhaḥ ca kāryam adhikāri niyoga viṣaya tayā avagamāt  iti tatas  tad vicāra artham śāstram ārabdhavyam iti atra ucyate na ārabdhavyam gata artha tvāt katham yaḥ tāvat  prathama  ārambha prakāraḥ karmaṇi kṛtya pratyaye na niyoga saṃpratyaya iti tad  svayam eva vidhāyaka tvam darśitam prasiddham ca etad  ‘svādhyāyaḥ adhyetavyaḥ iti evamādīnām vidhāyaka tvam na atra adhika āśaṅkā kāraṇam kiñcid  nanu caturvidhasya api kriyā phalasya ātmani asambhava uktaḥ yadi evam saktu nyāyaḥ  bhaviṣyati tad api na ātma viṣaya jñānasya nitya siddha tvāt iti uktam siddhasya eva punar abhyāsaḥ  vidhi nimitta upāsana ākhyaḥ  bhaviṣyati abhyudaya phale hiraṇya dhāraṇavat  nanu na vidhānataḥ api ātma viṣaya jñāna santānaḥ kartavyaḥ sa tu nityam ātmani jāgrataḥ siddhaḥ evam tarhi artha aviruddheṣu kāleṣu ātmani eva cetassamādhānam bhaviṣyati yad  punar ātma jñānāt avidyā ucchedaḥ tad ucchedāt saṃsāra nivṛttiḥ phalam iti upanyastam tad asat  aham iti ātmānam nityam eva jānāti sarvaḥ  lokaḥ na ca saṃsāraḥ  nivṛttaḥ atha punar ahaṃpratyaya avaseyāt anyat eva ātma rūpam parākṛta bhoktṛ bhoktavya bhoga granthi jñeya tvena ātma jñāna vidhinā jñāpyata iti tad asat  vidhiḥ hi sāmānyatas  siddhasya kriyā ātmanaḥ  viśeṣa siddhau prabhavati na atyantam asiddha sadbhāve tad yadi nāma jñānam loke siddham tathā api nirasta prapañca ātma viṣayam asiddham ākāśa muṣṭi hananavat  na vidhātum śakyam atha tādṛś ātma jñānam siddham kim vidhinā yad api mata antaram pratyakṣa ādeḥ agocara tvāt śāstrasya ca kārya artha tvāt saṅkarṣa paryanta eva vicāre veda artha parisamāptau prāptāyām vedānteṣu api kārya niṣṭhatā samānā brahma tattva avabodhaḥ ca kāryam adhikāri niyoga viṣaya tayā avagamāt  atas  tad vicārāya śārīraka ārambhaḥ iti tad api uktena nyāyena brahma avagamasya siddha tve asiddha tve ca kāryatva asambhavena pratyuktam aparam matam satyam kārya viṣayaḥ  vedaḥ na tu tāvat mātre tasmin sati yaḥ  yaḥ arthaḥ avagamyate sa sa veda arthaḥ yathā rūpe sati cakṣuṣaḥ pravṛttiḥ na ca rūpa mātram cakṣuṣaḥ  viṣayaḥ kim tu tasmin sati dravyam api evam iha api vastu tattvam api viṣayaḥ katham tad  ucyate ‘idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti na tāvat  sarva ātma rūpa tā ātmana upadiśyate yadi sarva rūpa tā ātmana upadiśyeta tatas  sarvasya acetana tvāt  tad rūpa tve boddhṛtva hānau bodhaka tvam śabdasya hīyeta atas  sarvasya ātma svabhāva tā vidhīyate anātma svarūpa vilayena hi vastunaḥ avagatiḥ dṛṣṭā nanu atra vidhiḥ na śrūyate kalpyatām tarhi vidhiḥ kim pratīte vidhi arthe vidhiḥ kalpyate uta apratīte yadi pratīte kalpyate kalpanāvaiḥ yathyam artha pratīti artham hi śabdaḥ  mṛgyate pratīte arthe śabdam kalpayatā kim kṛtam syāt  atha apratīta eva vidhi arthe vidhim kalpayitvā tatas arthaḥ pratipattavya iti apūrvam pramāṇa kauśalam nanu aśrūyamāṇa vidhiṣu api ‘tasmāt  pūṣā prapiṣṭa bhāgaḥ adantakaḥ  hi ityādiṣu vidhiḥ kalpitaḥ satyam yuktam tatra pūṣṇaḥ piṣṭa dravya sambandhaḥ samāsa abhihitaḥ  na siddhaḥ  vartate na api kutaścid bhaviṣyati iti pramāṇa abhāvāt  na api vidhinā kenacid  pada eka vākyatā yena vapa utkhanana ādivat  kathañcid ālambanam kalpyeta atas  nirālambanatva parihārāya kārya para tā kalpyata iti nanu iha api ātma padam cetanasya bhoktuḥ vācakam sa ca niyojya tvāt niyogam ākṣipati na etad  sāram niyogaḥ  hi puruṣa viśeṣam anāśritya anupalabdhaḥ  loke tam ākṣipet  viśva jit ādiṣu puruṣaḥ punar  kim niyogam antareṇa na upalabdhaḥ  loke yena vidhi kalpanā bhavet  atha api bhavatu nāma vidhiḥ na asau dhātunā vinā kevalaḥ  labhyate dhātunā eva saha kalpyate kaḥ asau dhātuḥ yadi tāvat  kartavyam iti tatra anātma svabhāva tā na nivṛttā prapañcasya yathā ‘amī piṣṭa piṇḍāḥ siṃhāḥ kriyantāmi ati piṣṭa svabhāva tā na nivṛttā itikartavya tā ca anirdiṣṭā tatra sa ākāṅkṣam vacanam anarthakam syāt  atha jñātavya iti adhyāhriyeta evam api sa eva doṣaḥ anātma svabhāva tā na nivṛtta iti aśakya artha upadeśaḥ ca na hi vastu vastu antarātmanā jñātum śakyate evam tarhi jñātavya iti adhyāhriyeta tatra dhātu artha unuvādaḥ pratyayaḥ vidhāyakaḥ kutas  prāpteḥ anuvādaḥ abhidhānata iti brūmaḥ evam tarhi vidhānam anarthakam svādhyāya kāle eva niṣpanna tvāt jñānasya punar  kartavya tayā codyate yathā mantreṣu prayoga vacanaḥ tatra vidhāyakaḥ iti iha api prayoga vacanaḥ  vidhāyakaḥ nanu mantreṣu sva arthasya anyatas  siddha tvāt  pratyaya para tvam yujyate iha tu sva artha vidhi parāṇām śabdānām pratyaya para tvam virudhyate na eṣa doṣaḥ anya artham api kṛtam anya artham bhavati tad yathā śāli artham kulyāḥ praṇīyante tābhyaḥ ca pānīyam pīyata upaspṛśyate ca evam iha api yathā padārthānām vidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ kramasya api vidhāyakaḥ evam sva arthasya vidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ pratyayasya api vidhāyakaḥ  bhaviṣyati tad etad anirūpitam iva dṛśyate katham mantrāḥ svādhyāya vidhinā upādāpitāḥ sva arthasya anyatas  siddha tvāt  tam pramātum aśaknuvantaḥ pramāṇa tvāt  pracyutāḥ vrīhi ādivat  prameya tām āpannāḥ śruti ādi pramāṇaiḥ yuktam yad viniyujyeran viniyuktāḥ ca anuṣṭheyasya anuṣṭhāna kāle smṛti apekṣasya smāraka tayā gṛhyeran  iti iha tu ‘idam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti yad  pada samanvaya nimittam sarvasya ātma svabhāva tā agrāhi vijñānam tad  sva viṣayasya anyatas asiddhatvāt prameya paratvāt na vidheḥ viṣayaḥ atha vidheḥ viṣayaḥ  na prameyam avagamayitum alam na yugapad u bhayam sambhavati vairūpya prasaṅgāt  nanu evam sati guṇa karmaṇām sarvatra vidhānam nirākṛtam syāt  na nirākṛtam syāt  yatra pramāṇa antara siddham guṇa karmaṇaḥ karmakārakam tatra tasya utpatti ādi anyatamam phalam tad vidhīyate yatra punar  pramāṇa antarāt asiddhaḥ  jñānasya karma bhūtaḥ  viṣayaḥ sa tena eva pramīyamāṇaḥ  na siddhavat uddeśyaḥ yena tad uddeśena tatra atiśaya ādhānāya jñānam vidhīyate tasmāt atra yugapad ubhayā sambhavāt  bhavati eva vairūpya prasaṅgaḥ na ca sa eva samanvayaḥ sva avayavāt vidheḥ vibhaktaḥ kārya kṣamaḥ avāntara vākyasya pramāṇatva ayogāt atha arthavāda padānām iva parasparataḥ saṃsṛjya kañcid artham avabodhya vidhi sambandham anubhavet iti abhiprāyaḥ tad asat  yuktam arthavāda padāni sva artha phala rahitāni tatra paryavasāna abhāvāt phalavat aṅga tām aśnuvīran  iti iha punar aparāmṛṣṭa vidhiḥ pada samanvayaḥ sva artham avagamayan nirasta nikhila prapañca avagraham apāsta atiśaya ānanda nitya anubhava eka rasam śivam advaitam ātma tattvam avagamayet  tatra kutaḥ vidhi śeṣa tā kṛtam kṛtyam prāptam prāpaṇīyam ‘a ātma lābhāt na param vidyayate iti smṛteḥ atha punar  śābda jñānāt na tathā anubhavaḥ tena sākṣātkaraṇāya vidhiḥ iti kim tad  jñānam anubhavāya vidhīyate pratyakṣa ādīnām tāvat agocaraḥ ‘na cakṣuṣā gṛhyate ityādi mantra varṇāt śābdam ca na iṣyate bhavatā satyam na śābda jñānam vidhi vikalam anubhavāya alam vihitam tu anubhava hetuḥ iti tad ayuktam yad tāvat svādhyāya adhyayana vidhi grāhitāt  pada samanvayāt  svabhāvataḥ samutpannam tad  tāvat na vidhīyate prameya para tayā vidhi viṣayatva anupapatteḥ iti uktam atha punar tad eva jñānam santanuyāt iti vidhīyate tad  katham labhyata upāsti dhyāyatyoḥ jñāna santāna vācinoḥ anyatarasya api upādānam antareṇa na api jñānena eva sva santānaḥ  lakṣyate sāhacarya ādya vyabhicarita sambandha abhāvāt na api abhyāsāt sākṣāt bhāvaḥ siddhaḥ na api śrūyate yena tad uddeśena jñāna santānaḥ  vidhīyeta nanu kim atra śravaṇena svayam eva sākṣātkāra karaṇāya puruṣa artha tvāt abhimukhaḥ puruṣaḥ siddhaḥ ca jñāna abhyāsaḥ śāstra śravaṇa ādau sākṣātkaraṇe hetuḥ yadi evam kim vidhinā svayam eva puruṣa arthe nirjñāte hetau pravartate yad  punar  nidarśanam śāli artham kulyāḥ praṇīyante iti yuktam tatra pratyakṣata ubhaya artha tāyāḥ  upalabhyamāna tvāt  iha punar  nidarśanam nyāyataḥ pratipattavyam sa ca nyāyaḥ  na yugapad  sambhavati iti uktam yad api idam uktam padārthānām vidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ kramasya api vidhāyakaḥ evam aikātmyasya pratipādakaḥ samanvayaḥ  vidhi viṣayam api jñāpayiṣyati iti tad api apeśalam yad  tāvat  pratyekam prayāja ādi vidhayaḥ taiḥ punar  na teṣām eva vidhānam na api te krama śabda abhidheyāḥ prayoga vacanaḥ api prayuñjānaḥ tān eva prayuṅkte na te krama iti uktam na ca kramaḥ  nāma ekāntatas  na asti eva tad buddhi śabdayoḥ nirālambanatva prasaṅgāt  tatra kramaḥ  nāma vastu bhūtaḥ  dharmaḥ  vidyata eva ta eva kenacid upādhinā vanavat  krama buddhi śabda ālambanam bhaveyuḥ smṛti vijñānam eva vā anuṣṭhāna kāle yathā upalabdhi padārthān parāmṛśet  sarvathā asti tāvat  ekaika padārtha ālambana jñāna atiriktam jñāna antaram tad ca eka tvāt  kartuḥ aneka tvāt ca padārthānām yugapad anuṣṭhānāsambhavāt apekṣitam sannihitam ca prayoga vacanena gṛhyata iti yuktam na tathā iha jñāna dvayam asti yad aikātmye vidhi viṣaya tve ca varteta tasmāt iha vidheya abhāvāt vidhāna aśravaṇāt adhi āhāre ca pramāṇa abhāvāt  na prayoga vacanaḥ asti yaḥ  mantrāṇām iva jñānasya api punar  prayogam vidhāsyate tasmāt asat etad  kārya viṣayaḥ api vedaḥ  vastu tattvam avabodhayati iti yad  punar  nidarśanam cakṣū rūpe sati dravyam api bodhayati evam kārye sati tattvam api vedaḥ avagamayati iti yuktam tatra yad yad avabodhayati cakṣuḥ tatra svatantram eva pramāṇam iha punar  yatra tātparyam tasya prameya tā na yad yad pratīyate tasya tasya iti vaiṣamyam āha mā bhūt jñāna dvayam yaḥ ayam ābhidhānikaḥ pratyayaḥ sa vidhi viṣaya eva bhavatu tasmin vihite arthāt  sarvasya ātma svabhāva tā sidhyati sa viṣaya tvāt avagamasya evam api avivakṣitaḥ arthaḥ śabdāt  vivakṣitaḥ tu arthāt iti śobhata itarām vākya artha vittā na ca niyogataḥ pratipatti vidhiḥ vāstavam saṃsargam gamayati bhavanti hi parikalpita viṣayā api pratipattayaḥ codanā lakṣaṇāḥ phalavatyaḥ ‘vācam dhenum upāsīte ati evamādyāḥ etad eva atra yuktam atatparasya pratyakṣa ādi virodhe tathā adhyavasāya hetutva ayogāt tasmāt  kārya niṣṭhe vede vastu tattva siddhiḥ manoratha eva atas  ahaṃpratyaya avaseya eva ātmā na tasya śabda avaseyam atīndriyam rūpa antaram asti śabdasya tatra sāmarthya abhāvāt evam ca sati ‘ayam ātmā brahma ‘eṣa ta ātma antaryāmyamṛtaḥ iti brahma antaryāmya ādi śabdā ahaṃpratyaya avaseya eva ātmani kathañcid vartante tena ‘sa ātmā tad tvam asi u iti vidyamānaiḥ āropitaiḥ ca guṇaiḥ ātma upāsanam mokṣa phalam ca vidhīyate iti yuktam atas  kārya anuraktasya veda arthasya sambhavāt  tasya ca sarva ātmanā vicārita tvāt  kim aparam avaśiṣṭam yad  brahma jijñāsā ārambham prayuñjīta ucyate syāt etad evam yadi sarva eva veda arthaḥ  vicārya tvena ‘atha atas  dharma jijñāse ati upakrāntaḥ  vicāritaḥ ca syāt  yāvatā kārya niṣṭha eva veda bhāgaḥ  vicāritaḥ  na vastu tattva niṣṭhaḥ tathā hi śāstra ārambhaḥ  vyākhyātṛbhiḥ evam nirūpitaḥ katham dharmaḥ  nāma kaścid  sādhayituḥ kāla antare śreyassādhanaḥ  loka ākhya pramāṇa ābhāsa utthena jñānena sāmānyatas  viṣayīkṛtaḥ tad viśeṣam prati vipratipannāḥ parīkṣakāḥ kecid agnihotra ādikam dharmam ācakṣate kecid caitya vandana ādikam tatra agnihotra ādi lakṣaṇa eva dharmaḥ abhipretaḥ na tad pratipādakānām veda vākyānām vicārauvasaraḥ  na api vivakṣita artha tvam atas  caitya vandana ādīnām eva anyatamaḥ  dharmaḥ tad pratipādakānām buddha ādi vākyānām eva anyatamam vicāryam na vā tad api na hi pauruṣeye vākye śabda śakti anusāreṇa arthaḥ api tu tena vivakṣitaḥ iti evam āśaṅkite dharmāya veda vākyāni vicārayiṣyan tad artha vivakṣā vicāra avasara pradarśana artham ‘atha atas  dharma jijñāsā iti sūtrayāmāsa jaiminiḥ vedam adhītya anantaram dharma jijñāsā kartavyā na snānam guru kula nivṛtti rūpam iti darśayitum iti evam sthite śāstra ārambhe na sarva veda artha viṣayam śāstram iti pratītiḥ kintu dharma atiriktaḥ api siddha rūpaḥ  veda arthaḥ asti sa ca paryudastaḥ  jaimininā nyāya antara viṣaya tvāt iti gamyate tad  katham yad  tāvat idam ucyate dharmaḥ  nāma loka pravādāt  sāmānyatas  siddhaḥ tasya sva rūpa pramāṇayoḥ vipratipattau  agni hotra ādiḥ api veda arthaḥ  dharma tayā vicāra padavīm upārohati yatas  tasya api vicārauvasaraḥ  vidyate tena vivakṣitaḥ asau na ca adhyayana mātrāt kṛtakṛtya tā atas adhyayana anantaram na guru kulāt nivarttitavyam kintu veda arthaḥ  dharmaḥ kim vā anya eva iti jijñāsām arhati iti vaditum dharma grahaṇam yuktam atha atas  dharma jijñāsā iti na veda artha jijñāsā iti yatas  na veda artha tayā jñāne pravṛttiḥ yad  punar  dharmasya sva rūpa pramāṇa kathanāya dvitīyam sūtram tad  veda pramāṇa kaḥ  dharma iti syāt  kim idam ‘codanā lakṣaṇaḥ iti tad  nūnam na sarvaḥ  vedaḥ  dharma eva kārya ātmake paryavasyati kaścid asya bhāgaḥ kārya tā śūnye vastu tattve api vartate iti manyate nanu codanā grahaṇasya anyat eva prayojanam ‘cuda preraṇe iti preraṇa karmaṇaḥ codanā iti rūpam tatas  preraṇa ātmakaḥ  vidhiḥ apuruṣa arthe prerayitum aśaknuvan pada antara abhihitam api svarga ādikam bhāvanā karma tām āpādayati eka pada upādānāt  saṃnihita taram dhātvartham vihāya iti kathayitum iti na etad  sāram adhyayana vidhiḥ adhyayane māṇavakam prerayan adhyayanasya puruṣa artha rūpa artha avabodhaka tvam anāpādya na śaknoti prerayitum pāramparyeṇa api apuruṣa arthe vidhera paryavasānāt  atas  tad artham na codanā grahaṇam veda grahaṇena api tad siddheḥ api ca veda grahaṇam eva yuktam asandehāt  codanā grahaṇe hi sandehaḥ syāt  loke api vidyamāna tvāt  atha veda adhikaraṇe ‘vedān  ca eke sannikarṣam i ati viśeṣa abhidhānāt vaidikatva siddhiḥ iti saḥ ayam ābhāṇa kaḥ  loke ‘piṇḍam utsṛjya karam leḍhī ati sūtrakārasya api akauśalam pradarśitam syāt  tatas codanā grahaṇāt acodana ātmakaḥ api veda bhāgaḥ abhipreta iti gamyate yena veda artha mātrasya dharma tvam mā bhūt iti codanā iti avocat  tad evam sūtrakāra eva sva śāstra viṣaya atiriktam veda bhāgam avicāritam asūsucat nanu ‘dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam ‘tad bhūtānām kriyā arthena samāmnāyaḥ ‘āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt iti ca sarvasya kārya artha tvam darśitam satyam tad  prakrama balāt  tad niṣṭhaḥ  veda bhāga iti gamyate na sarvatra api ca ‘dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam i ati na sarvasya karma avabodhanam artha ucyate katham veda adhyayana anantaram snāna vidhāyakam āmnāyam upalabhya vedasya anarthakatva āśaṅkite ‘atikramiṣyāma imam āmnāyam anatikrāmantaḥ  vedam arthavantam santam anarthakam avakalpayema dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam iti artha sadbhāvaḥ pradarśitaḥ  na artha antara asadbhāvaḥ saḥ ayam ayoga vyavacchedaḥ  na anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ karma śabdena dharma eva kārya tvāt abhihitaḥ yatas  tad avabodha pravṛttaḥ  vedasya arthavat tvam mṛgayate kim vedasya arthaḥ  vidyate na vā sa ca dharma tvena avagantum śakyate na vā iti tasmāt  na karma avabodhanam eva veda arthaḥ abhipretaḥ  bhāṣya kṛtaḥ yad  punar  ‘āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt ānarthakyam atad arthānām i ati tatra yadi ānarthakyam artha abhāvaḥ tad asat  yatas  evam eva bhūta artham anuvadanti iti darśitaḥ arthaḥ atha niṣprayojana tvam svādhyāya adhyayana vidhiḥ niṣprayojanam akṣara mātram api na grāhayati iti bhavatu ‘saḥ arodi ititya ādīnām apuruṣa artha pratipādaka tvāt  eka vākya tvāt  pṛthak kārya kalpanā anupapatteḥ kalpayitum ca aśakya tvāt yāni punar  apāsta aśeṣa aśivam ātmānam anubhava paryantam avabodhayanti vākyāni tāni anavadya prayojana tvāt bhavantitarām eva prayojanavanti atas  svayam apuruṣa artha tvāt tad artha upakāri tayā kathañcid  puruṣa arthaḥ tāvaka tvena prayojanavat tvam uktam na sarvasya eva akriyā artha tvena ānarthakyam āśaṅkya kriyā artha tvena arthava tvam uktam tathā ca tadvidhāni eva tatra vākyāni udāhṛtāni yad api kecid  śāstra prasthānam anyathā varṇayanti na hi kila evam śāstram prasthitam kim veda lakṣaṇaḥ  dharmaḥ uta buddha vākya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ iti kim tarhi adhīta vedasya yaḥ arthaḥ avagataḥ tatra eva vipratipattayaḥ santi kim ayam asau uta ayam iti tad nirākaraṇa arthaḥ śāstra ārambhaḥ iti tatra api na nikhila veda artha vicāra pratītiḥ tad  katham tathā sati ‘atha atas  veda artha jijñāsā iti syāt  yatas  na dharma iti kṛtvā vicāraḥ kintu veda artha  iti satyam tathā api śāstra kārāṇām puruṣa artha siddhi artham śāstra praṇayanam tatas ca puruṣa artha kathana artham dharma grahaṇam iti evam tarhi dharma iti eva kṛtvā vicāraḥ  bhavatu tasya puruṣa artha tvāt sandigdha tvāt ca tathā ca uttaram api sūtram anuguṇam bhavati ‘codanā lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ  dharmaḥ iti dharma svarūpa vipratipatti nirāsa param itarathā veda artha vipratipattau tad nirāsa artham ‘codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  veda arthaḥ iti syāt  yatas  na dharma grahaṇe sati veda artha vipratipattiḥ śakyā nirākartum katham yad  tāvat  codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  yaḥ arthaḥ sa dharma iti dharma tvam jñāpyeta tadā sa eva veda arthaḥ  na anya iti na labhyate atha punar  sa dharma iti nāma nāmi sambandhaḥ vidhīyate tad aprakrāntam niṣprayojanam atiprasaṅgaḥ ca āpadyeta atha api kathañcid  dharma śabdena veda artha  eva ucyate iti kalpyeta tathā sati codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  veda arthaḥ  na artha vāda ādi lakṣaṇaḥ iti siddha prāmāṇya veda artha vicāraḥ ayam syāt  uttara lakṣaṇavat  tatra anantaram prāmāṇya pratipādanam na yujyeta ‘vṛttam pramālakṣaṇa am iti ca mantra artha vādeṣu ca kārya artha tve vipratipattiḥ na syāt  sā ca uttaratra eva nirasyate atas  pūrva uktena nyāyena kārya niṣṭha eva veda bhāgaḥ  vicārya tayā prakrāntaḥ  vicāritaḥ ca na vastu niṣṭhaḥ iti atas  vastu tattva niṣṭham veda bhāgam vicārayitum idam ārabhyate atha atas  brahma jijñāsā iti iti paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ādi śrī śaṅkara bhagavat pāda antevāsi vara śrī padma pāda ācārya kṛtau pañcapādikāyām jijñāsā sūtra avataraṇam nāma dvitīya varṇakam samāptam atha tṛtīyam varṇakam tatra atha śabda ānantarya arthaḥ parigṛhyate na adhikāra arthaḥ bahma jijñāsāyā anadhikārya tvāt  ityādi bhāṣyam tad  jijñāsā śabdasya avayava arthena arthavat tve yujyate adhikriyā yogyasya brahmaṇaḥ tad jñānasya vā prādhānyena anirdeśāt pradhānasya ca id chāyā anadhikārya tvāt  ayam tu jijñāsā śabdaḥ  vicāra vacanaḥ  mīmāṃsā para paryāyaḥ prayuktaḥ abhiyuktaiḥ ‘idam atas  jijñāsante kim kratu guṇakam upāsanam svāmi karma uta rtvij karme ati idantu jijñāsyam kim nu khalu imau tapya tāpakau  ekasya ātmanaḥ  bhedau uta jāti antaram iti dharmamīmāṃsā bhāṣya kāraḥ api saṅghātam eva prāyuṅkta ‘dharmam jijñāsi tum icchedi ati saṅghāta vācya tvāt vicārasya anyathā evam avakṣyat  ‘dharmam jñātum icchedi ati ata evam dharmāya jijñāsā ‘dharma jijñāse ati saṅghātasya arthavat tvam aṅgīkṛtya caturthī samāsaḥ  darśitaḥ tad anusāreṇa ca etāni bhāṣyāṇi ‘evam veda vākyāni eva ebhiḥ vicāryante ‘veda vākyāni vicārayitavyāni ‘katham veda vākyāni vicārayet i ati ca punar ca ‘kratu artha puruṣa arthayoḥ jijñāsā ‘kratu artha puruṣa arthau jijñāsyete iti iha api bhāṣya kāraḥ  vakṣyati ‘tasmāt  brahma jijñāsitavyam i ati punar ca ‘vedānta vākyamīmāṃsā tad avirodhi tarka upakaraṇā niḥśreyasa prayojanā prastūyate iti atas  saṅghātasya arthavat tvāt adhikāra artha tā yujyate śāstra vacanaḥ  hi jijñāsā śabdaḥ tena brahma jijñāsā adhikṛtā veditavyā iti ucyate na ayam jijñāsā śabdaḥ parityakta avayava arthaḥ kevala mīmāṃsā aparyāyaḥ prayujyamānaḥ  dṛśyate na api smaraṇam asti na ca avayava arthena arthavat tve sambhavati samudāyasya artha antara kalpanā yuktā nanu na vayam kalpayāmaḥ darśitaḥ śiṣṭa prayogaḥ na tasya anyathā siddha tvāt katham anyathā siddha tvam antarṇīta vicāra artha tvāt jijñāsā śabdasya tathā hi vicāra pūrvaka sādhya jñāna viṣaya icchā jijñāsā śabdāt  pratīyate na upadeśa mātra sādhya jñāna viṣayā evam prayoga pratyayayoḥ darśanāt  tena jijñāsā śabdasya avayava arthena arthavat tvāt  yuktam uktam brahma jijñāsāyā anadhikārya tvāt iti nanu evam api kuta etad  antarṇītam vicāram āśritya śabdataḥ guṇa tve api artha lakṣaṇena prādhānyena brahma tajjñānayoḥ adhikāra yogya tvāt ca adhikriyamāṇa tvam aṅgīkṛtya adhikāra artha tvam kim iti na gṛhyate yena śabda lakṣaṇena prādhānyena icchāyāḥ  anadhikārya tvāt ānantarya artha tvam eva parigṛhyata iti ucyate śāstrasya anārambha prasaṅgāt adhikāra arthatva anupapatteḥ adhikāra artha tve hi aprayojanam śāstram kāka danta parīkṣāvat ana ārabhyam syāt  tatra kasya adhikāra ucyeta nanu brahma jñānam prayojanam tad arthaḥ śāstra ārambhaḥ na brahma jñāne arthitva anupapatteḥ brahma jñānāt hi manasaḥ api viyogāt nikhila viṣaya anuṣaṅga nivṛttiḥ śrūyate sā ca sārvabhauma upakramam brahma loka avasānam utkṛṣṭa utkṛṣṭa sukham śrūyamāṇam sa upāyam nivartayati atas  brahma jñānāt udvijate lokaḥ kutas tatra pravṛttiḥ nanu ānanda rūpa tā api brahma jñānāt āpyate atas tad artham pravartate tatra mā evam na hi brahma ānandaḥ ananubhūta pūrvaḥ anubhūta bhogya sukha abhilāṣam mandīkartum utsahate yena tad ujjhitvā brahma jñāne pravarteta nanu paritṛpta rūpa tā api brahma jñānāt  atas  paritṛptaḥ kim kāmayate atṛpti nimittaka tvāt  kāmasya tathā ca śrutiḥ ‘āpta kāmaḥ ātma kāma iti smṛtiḥ api ‘a ātma lābhāt na param vidyate ‘etat buddhvā buddhimān syāt  kṛtakṛtyaḥ ca bhārate ati na tṛpteḥ eva udvega darśanāt viṣaya viccheda ātmikāyāḥ tathā ca vaktāraḥ  bhavanti ahaḥ kaṣṭam kim iti sṛṣṭiḥ evam na babhūva yad  sarvam eva bhoktum sāmarthyam atṛptiḥ bhogyānām ca akṣayaḥ iti rāgi gītam ślokam api udāharanti ‘api vṛndāvane śūnye śrṛgāla tvam sa icchati na tu nirviṣayam mokṣam kadācid api gautama iti mā bhūd brahma jñāna arthitā veda artha tvāt eva brahma jñānam kartavyam svādhyāya adhyayanasya artha avabodha phalaka tvāt  syāt etad evam yadi artha avabodha phala adhyayana kriyā syāt  sā hi adhīyamāna avāpti phala tvāt akṣara grahaṇa antā atha akṣara grahaṇam niṣprayojanam iti na tatra paryavasānam vidheḥ bhavatu tarhi saktūnām gatiḥ tad api na akṣarebhyaḥ prayojanavat artha avabodha darśanāt na tarhi niṣprayojanāni akṣarāṇi atas tad paryantam adhyayanam na niṣphalam atas akṣara grahaṇāt eva niyoga siddheḥ phala prayukta eva artha avabodhaḥ api ca akṣara grahaṇa antaḥ  vidhiḥ niṣprayojanaḥ iti na sarvatra prayojanavat artha avabodha paryanta tā kalpayitum api śakyate tatra avaśyam kalpanīya akṣara grahaṇa anta tā tad yathā rājanyasya satra vaiśya stoma bṛhaspati savānām āmnānam vaiśyasya ca aśvamedha rājasūya satrāṇām pāṭhaḥ na ca teṣām anadhyayanam eva svādhyāya śabdena sakala veda vācinā adhyayanasya vihita tvāt  nanu ca aśrūyamāṇa adhikāraḥ adhyayana vidhiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ca akṣara grahaṇe artha avabodhaḥ sa kalpanām adhikārasya nirundhan svayam adhikārasya hetuḥ sampadyate dṛṣṭa adhikāreṣu pratyakṣataḥ tad upalabdhau  adhikāra siddhiḥ atas artha avabodha paryantaḥ svādhyāya adhyayana niyogaḥ tena niyoga sidhi artham eva sakala veda artha vicāraḥ atra ucyate bhavet adhyayana vidheḥ artha avabodhaḥ prayojanam na adhikāra hetu tā adhyayanāt prāc asiddha tvāt prāk  ca adhikāra jñānena prayojanam atas  na vidheḥ dṛṣṭa adhikāra tvena artha avabodha siddhiḥ yadi evam adhikāra śravaṇāt artha avabodhe ca pratipakṣa kalpanā anupapatteḥ tasya ca adhikāra hetutva anabhyupagamāt apravṛttiḥ eva adhyayane prāptā atra kecid āhuḥ ācārya karaṇa vidhi prayuktasya adhyayanasya anuṣṭhānam ādhānasya iva kāma śruti prayuktasya iti tad ayuktam iti apare katham ‘aṣṭa varṣam brāhmaṇam upanayīte ati yadi ayam ācāryasya niyogaḥ māṇavakaḥ  na niyuktaḥ  bhavati aniyuktasya ca svādhyāya adhyayane pravṛttiḥ na sambhavati kiñca anyat ācārya karaṇa vidhiḥ anityaḥ ‘brāhmaṇasya adhikāḥ pravacana yājana pratigrahāḥ iti vṛtti arthaḥ adhikāraḥ atas  sva icchātaḥ pravṛttiḥ upanayana ākhyaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ  nityaḥ akaraṇe doṣa śravaṇāt  ‘ata ūrdhvam trayaḥ api ete yathākālam asaṃskṛtāḥ sāvitrīpatitā vrātyā bhavanti ārya vigarhitāḥ na etaiḥ apūtaiḥ vidhivat āpadi api hi karhicit  brāhmān yaunān  ca sambandhān ācaret  brāhmaṇaḥ kvacid iati saṃskāraḥ ca svādhyāya adhyayana arthaḥ evam ca svādhyāya adhyayanam api nityam tathā ca nindā śravaṇam ‘a śrotriyā ananuvākyā anagnayaḥ śūdra sadharmāṇaḥ  bhavantī ati evam ced  katham nityam anityena prayujyate iti vācyam nanu katham ācārya karaṇa vidhiḥ anityaḥ yāvatā vṛtti arthaḥ  hi saḥ na hi kaścid vinā dhanena jīviṣyati tathā ca uktam ‘jīviṣyati vinā dhanena iti anupapannam i ati atas  sarveṣām sarvadā samīhita phalaḥ san katham anityaḥ syāt  bhavet evam nitya tā phala vaśena na śabdāt  tathā hi phalasya nitya samīhita tvāt avaśya kartavyatā vāstavī tatra asati śabda vyāpāra icchātaḥ kartavya tā pratipattiḥ syāt  na kartavya tā pratipatteḥ icchā śābdyām hi nitya kartavya tā pratipattau śabdasya sarvadā sarvān pratyeka rūpa tvāt icchā api tad vaśa vartinī tathā eva syāt  aucitya ādi bhāve api kasyacid  kathañcid  kvacid  kadācid icchāyāḥ pramāṇataḥ tāvān nityaḥ tena nityena tathāvidham eva prayujyate iti na nitya anitya saṃyoga virodhaḥ phala vaśāt tu tad kartavya tā pratipattau yadi api nitya abhilaṣitam phalam tathā api upāya antarāt api tad siddheḥ tad eka upāya tve api ālasyāt āyāsa asahiṣṇu tayā vā kāmasya kuṇṭhībhāve na kartavyatāyāḥ pratipattiḥ iti anitya tve sati na tena nityasya prayojya tvam upapadyate nanu pituḥ putra utpādana vidhiḥ anuśāsana paryantaḥ śrūyate ‘tasmāt putram anuśiṣṭam lokyam āhuḥ tasmāt enam anuśāsatī ati atas  putra utpādanasya nitya tvāt  tasya ca anuśāsana paryanta tvāt  tad ākṣipta tvāt ca upanayana adhyayanayoḥ katham ācārya karaṇa vidhiḥ anityaḥ syāt  katham vā adhyayanasya artha avabodha paryanta tā na bhavet  ucyate na anena putra anuśāsanam vidhīyate putra utpādana vidhi śeṣa tvena svatantram eva vā kintu sampatti karma vidhi śeṣaḥ ayam artha vādaḥ tena eka vākya tvāt  atas  yathāprāptam anuśāsanam anuvadati kim tad anuśāsanam katham vā tad  prāptavat anu udyate ucyate nityasya putra utpādana vidheḥ prayojanam yad  pitṝṇām lupta piṇḍa udaka kriyāṇām naraka pāta śravaṇāt  pitṛ piṇḍa udaka kriyā ādi anuṣṭhānena naraka pāta trāṇam na ca śāstrīyeṇa parijñānena vinā tad anuṣṭhānam sambhavati tena pitrā nityam ātmanaḥ putra utpādana adhikāram parisamāpayitum putrasya avaśya kartavya artha viṣayam garbha aṣṭa varṣeṇa brāhmaṇena tvayā upanayana ākhyaḥ saṃskāraḥ kārayitavyaḥ yaḥ svādhyāya adhyayana arthaḥ  vihita iti yad anuśāsanam tad iha anu udyate ‘tasmāt enam anuśāsati iti tathā ca liṅgam ‘śvetaketuḥ hāruṇeya āsa tam ha pitā uvāca śvetaketaḥ vasa brahmacaryam na vai somī asmad kulīnaḥ ananūcya brahmabandhuḥ iva bhavatī ati tad evam anityena ācārya karaṇa vidhinā katham nityam prayujyata iti vācyam kim ca ācārye preta ācārya antara karaṇam na prāpnoti na hi adhikārī pratinidhīyate na api adhikāraḥ adhikārī sva adhikāra sidhi artham sādhana antara bhrā īṣe sādhana antaram pratinidhāya sva adhikāram nirvartayati iti yuktam evam eṣā bahu doṣā kalpanā dṛśyate tasmāt  māṇavakasya eva eṣa niyogaḥ katham guṇa kartṛ vyāpāra sambaddhaḥ  vidhiḥ pradhāna kartṛ sthaḥ  bhavati yathā ‘etayā grāma kāmam yājayet i ati grāma kāmasya yāgaḥ  vidhīyate guṇa kartṛ vyāpāraḥ prāptaḥ anūdyate tasya yājanasya vṛtti artha tvāt  evam iha api guṇa kartṛ vyāpāraḥ  vṛtti artha tvena prāptaḥ anūdyate atra eke pratyavatiṣṭhante yuktam ‘yājayet i ati pradhāna kartṛ vyāpāra abhidhāyinaḥ  yajateḥ parasya guṇa kartṛ vyāpāra abhidhāyinaḥ śabda antarasya ṇica upādānāt  tasya ca avidheya tvāt  pradhāna kartṛ vyāpārasya abhidhānam iha punar ekaḥ  nayatiḥ māṇavakasya vyāpāram brūyāt  ācāryasya vā na tāvat  māṇavakasya nayati artha kartṛ tvam karma kāraka tvāt  tasya atas anabhidheya vyāpāraḥ katham niyujyeta na hi para vyāpāre paraḥ  niyoktum śakyate sva vyāpāre hi puruṣasya niyogaḥ tasmāt na eṣa māṇavakasya niyogaḥ tad evam ācārya karaṇa vidhi prayukta tvāt adhyayanasya na atra adhikāra cintayā manaḥ khedayitavyam iti ucyate māṇavakasya eva ayam niyogaḥ na ācāryasya iha kiñcid vidheyam asti katham yad tāvat ‘upanayīte atyasya abhidhāna taḥ  nyāyataḥ ca nirūpyamāṇaḥ artha  etāvān pratīyate ātmānam ācāryam kartum kañcid ātma samīpam ānīya adhyāpayet  iti etad ca sarvam vṛtti artha tvena brāhmaṇasya anyata eva prāptam na atra vidhātavyam tatra kam adhyāpayet  iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām ‘brāhmaṇam aṣṭa varṣam i ati viśeṣasya vidhāyakam etad  syāt  tatra prāpte vyāpāre artha dvaya vidhānam ekasmin vākye na śakyate vaktum vākya bheda prasaṅgāt  atas  na ācāryasya kiñcid  vidheyam iha asti nanu māṇavakasya api na kiñcid  vidheyam asti asti iti brūmaḥ katham yadā eva ‘upanayīte ati śabdataḥ nyāyataḥ ca ātmānam ācāryam kartum upanayanena saṃskṛtya kañcid adhyāpayet iti pratīyate tadā eva yāga śrutau dravya devatā mātra pratītivat adhyayana artha upanayana saṃskāryaḥ api sāmānyatas  pratīyate tasya ca prekṣāvataḥ  niṣprayojane pravartayitum aśakyatvāt  vidyamānasya api adhyayane artha avabodhasya prāc asiddheḥ pravṛtti hetutva asiddheḥ vidhitaḥ avaśya kartavyatām pratipadya svayam eva pravartate tena ‘aṣṭa varṣam brāhmaṇam upanayīte ati aṣṭa varṣaḥ  brāhmaṇa upasarpet ācāryam iti arthaḥ grāma kāmam yājayet  grāma kāmaḥ  yajeta iti yathā nanu evam api adhikāraḥ  na labhyate asti atra adhikāra hetuḥ nityam nimittam vayaḥ viśiṣṭā jātiḥ jāti viśiṣṭam vayaḥ  vā nanu jāti vayasī viśeṣaṇam upādeyasya anupādeya viśeṣaṇam adhikāra hetuḥ iti sthitiḥ satyam asti iyam sthitiḥ kintu kartuḥ adhikāra iti api sthitā nyāya vidaḥ kim ca iha na māṇavakaḥ  jāti vayaḥ viśiṣṭa upādeya upanayane kim tu upanayanam eva tad artham vidhīyate saṃskārasya saṃskārya uddeśena vidhānāt  atas  saṃskāryasya avacchedaka tvam vayaḥ jāti avacchinnam sat  bhavati nitya nimittam māṇavakasya saṃskāryatva iti tad evam upanayanasya adhyayana artha tvāt tasya ca sa adhikāra tvāt tena ca adhikāreṇa sa adhikāraḥ adhyayana vidhiḥ akṣara grahaṇa mātreṇa ca adhikāra siddhiḥ artha avabodhaḥ tu kāraṇa antarāt iti nanu ca evam adhītaḥ  vedaḥ  dharma jijñāsāyā hetuḥ jñātaḥ anantaram dharmaḥ  jijñāsitavyaḥ iti veda eva ādhītonya nirapekṣaḥ  dharma jijñāsāyā hetuḥ iti vadanti satyam tathā eva tad  kaḥ  vā anyathā vadati adhīta vedaḥ  hi avaśya karaṇīyāni nitya naimittikāni akaraṇe pratyavāya janakāni karmāṇi pratipadyate tāni anantaram eva avaśya vicāraṇīyāni katham etāni anuṣṭheyāni iti atas  prāk adhyaya nāt apratipatteḥ ayogya tvāt adhīta veda tvam eva anya nirapekṣam artha avabodha hetuḥ iti gīyate na tathā brahma jñānam avaśya kartavyam akaraṇe pratyavāya hetuḥ iti pramāṇam asti tasmāt adhīta vedena avaśya kartavyā dharma jijñāsā na evam brahma jijñāsā tad eva brahma jijñāsāyā adhikārān arha tvāt arhayoḥ ca brahma tajjñānayoḥ anarthyamāna tvāt  jijñāsā anupapannā maṅgalasya api vākya arthe samanvaya abhāvāt  śruti mātra upayogāt ca sādhu uktam atha śabda ānantarya arthaḥ parigṛhyate na adhikāra artha iti nanu prakriyamāṇāt  pūrva prakṛtam api kiñcid  niyamena pratīyate atha śabdāt  tatas tad pratipatti artham kim iti na gṛhyate ucyate na etad ānantaryāt  vyatiricyate katham evam tad  prakriyamāṇasya niyamena pūrva vṛttam bhavati yadi tasya anantaram tanmātra apekṣam tad prakriyeta evam sati prakriyamāṇasya hetu bhūtaḥ arthaḥ pūrva nirvṛttaḥ  bhavati anyathā yasmin kasmiṃścid  pūrva vṛtta apekṣāyām anuvāda adṛṣṭa artha tvayoḥ anyataratva prasaṅgāt  atas  hetu bhūtaḥ arthaḥ apekṣitavyaḥ tad etad āha pūrva prakṛta apekṣāyāḥ ca phalata ānantarya avyatirekāt iti sati ca ānantarya artha tve yathā dharma jijñāsā pūrva vṛttam veda adhyayanam niyamena apekṣate evam brahma jijñāsā api yad  pūrva vṛttam niyamena apekṣate tad  vaktavyam svādhyāya anantar yantu samānam iti yena vinā niyamena anantarasya na prakriyā sa tādṛśaḥ  hetuḥ pūrva nirvṛttaḥ  vaktavyaḥ yasya anantara brahma jijñāsā prakriyate svādhyāya adhyayanantu samānam sādhāraṇaḥ  hetuḥ dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ atas ca ‘atha atas  brahma jijñāse ati punar atha śabdena tad mātra apekṣaṇam vyartham syāt  athavā samānam na atyantam apekṣitam na svayam eva sāmarthyam janayitum prayoktum ca śaktam atas  samānaḥ  hetuḥ na avaśyam niṣpādaka iti arthaḥ nanu iha karma avabodha ānantaryam viśeṣaḥ tathā ca vṛtti antare varṇitam akarmaṇām adhikāra paramparayā śabdataḥ vā saṃskāra tayā vā yathā vibhāgam tārdathya avagamāt  niḥśreyasa prayojana tvāt ca anantarya vacanaḥ atha śabdaḥ adhigata anantaram i ati anyaiḥ api sva vṛttau varṇitam atatra atha atas śabdau prathama  eva adhyāye prathama sūtre varṇitau atha iti pūrva prakṛtām dharma jijñāsām apekṣya anantaram brahma jijñāsā prārambha arthaḥ ata iti pūrva nirdiṣṭasya eva arthasya hetu tām ācaṣṭe brahma jijñāsām pratī ati atra āha na dharma jijñāsāyāḥ prāk api adhīta vedāntasya brahma jijñāsā upapatteḥ iti vedānta adhyayanam yadi api kevalam na puṣkalam kāraṇam tathā api na tena vinā utpadyate brahma jijñāsā upapadyate tu dharma avabodhanam vinā api iti abhiprāyaḥ katham tatra tāvat  dharma jijñāsāyām trayam vṛttam dvādaśa lakṣaṇe pratipādita nyāya sahasram tad anugraha upajā taḥ ca vākya artha nirṇayaḥ vākya arthaḥ ca agnihotra ādikam karma tatra yaḥ prathama sūtre atha śabda upādāna sūcitaḥ  nyāyaḥ svādhyāyasya artha avabodha upayoga pratipatti hetuḥ yad api autpattika sūtre śabda arthayoḥ sambandha nityat tvena vedāntānām ca apauruṣeya tvena kāraṇena anapekṣa tvam nāma prāmāṇya kāraṇam uktam tad ubhayam i hāpi upayujyate apekṣita tvāt  itarasya purna nyāya kalāpasya na brahma jijñāsāyām upayoga usti yatas  na nirasta aśeṣa prapañcam brahma ātmā eka tvam pratijñātam tatra na tad pratipādane tad pratipādana sāmarthye vā śabdānām kaścid  nyāyaḥ abhihitaḥ yad punar  prathama tantra siddha nyāya upajīvanam asmin  api tantre tad  sa guṇa vidyā viṣayam tatra ca mānasī kriyā upāsanā vidheyāniti aphalā dharma viśeṣa eva tad evam nyāya kalāpasya na brahma jijñāsāyām upayogaḥ atas  na tad apekṣaḥ atha śabdaḥ yad punar  svādhyāya sya artha avabodha upayoge anapekṣa tvena svatas prāmāṇya siddhau ca nyāya dvayam tad  apekṣitam api na kevalam brahma jijñāsā kāraṇam svādhyāyavat eva tena na tad apekṣaḥ atha śabdaḥ yaḥ punar vākya artha nirṇayaḥ sa na katham api brahma jijñāsāyām upayujyate na hi anya viṣayam jñānam anyatra pravṛttau hetuḥ pratipattau kadācid  syāt api yathā anumāna ādau tad api iha na asti dharma brahmaṇoḥ sambandha anirūpaṇāt atas  karmaṇām upa yogaḥ pariśiṣyate tathā ca taiḥ api uktam karmaṇām adhikāra paramparayā śabdataḥ vā saṃskāra tayā vā yathā vibhāgam tārdathya avagamāt iti atra idam nirūpyate kā iyam adhikāra paramparā katham vā tārdathya miti yathā tāvat  prāsāda mārurukṣoḥ sopāna paramparā kramaśas  prāpyamāṇā prāsāda ārohaṇa hetuḥ na tathā iha brahma jijñāsām cikīrṣoḥ karmāṇi sahasra saṃvatsara paryantāni tad kriyā hetu tayā sthitāni pramāṇa abhāvāt  atha kāma upahata manāḥ tad abhimukhaḥ  brahma jijñāsāyām na avatarati karmabhiḥ tu kāmā vāptau tad upaśamāt  brahvajijñāsāyām avatarati tathā ca sārvabhaumatva ādi uttarottara śata guṇa utkarṣa avasthitān brahma loka avāpti paryantān kāmān avāpayanti adhikāra paramparayā karmāṇi brahma lokāt  param kāmayitavya abhāvāt  nirviṣayasya ca kāmasya anupapatteḥ dagdha indhana agnivat  kāma upaśame brahma jijñāsām karoti karma anuṣṭhāna ānantaryam tarhi vaktavyam na dharma avabodha ānantaryam katham vā kāma āptiḥ kāma upaśama hetuḥ dṛṣṭānta sāmarthyāt  yathā haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmā vardhamānaḥ api sarva haviḥ prakṣepe sarvam dagdhvā svayam śāmyati evam viṣaya indhanaḥ kāmaḥ  yāvat viṣayam vardhamānaḥ api tad kṣaye kṣīṇa indhana agnivat  svayam śāmyati iti yuktam satyam yuktam yadi hairaṇyagarbhaḥ  bhogaḥ  na kṣīyeta kṣīyate tu kṛtaka tvāt  paricchinna viṣaya tvāt ca tad kṣaye pūrvavat anavāptaḥ avāptavyaḥ iti kāmaḥ samullasati eva atas  viṣayasya kṣaya ādi doṣa darśanāt kāma upaśamaḥ  hiraṇyagarbhasya api tathā ca uktam ajñānam apratigham yasya vairāgyam ca jagatpateḥ aiśvaryam ca eva dharmaḥ ca saha siddham catuṣṭayam iti tasmāt  sarvatra kāmasya viṣaya doṣa darśanam eva uccheda kāraṇam nitya vastu darśanam ca rasa varjam rasaḥ api asya param dṛṣṭvā nivartate iti smṛteḥ na ca evaṃlakṣaṇa āgamaḥ asti hiraṇyagarbha upabhogāt  nikhila viṣaya avāptau kāma ucchedaḥ  bhavati iti nanu kāma avāptau svastha hṛdayaḥ kārya antara kṣamaḥ  bhavati iti sarveṣām sva saṃvedyam etad  satyam tad utkalikā upaśamāt tad utkalikā upaśamaḥ ca tadā sāmarthya hāneḥ sati ca sāmarthye svacchanda upabhoga sambhavāt yadi punar ekāntatas  nivṛtta kāmaḥ  bhavet  na tam viṣayam punar  saṅga upāyet  tasmāt  na karmaṇām kāma nirbahaṇa dvāreṇa brahma jijñāsā yogya ta āpādanam atas  na karma avabodha apekṣaḥ api atha śabdaḥ bhavatu tarhi saṃskāra dvāreṇa karmaṇām pūrva vṛtta tvam `yasya ete aṣṭācatvāriṃśat saṃskārāḥ aṣṭau ca ātma guṇāḥ sa brahmaṇaḥ sāyujyam gacchatī ati `mahāyajñaiḥ ca yajñaiḥ ca brāhmī iyam kriyate tanuḥ i ati `jñānam utpadyate puṃsām kṣayāt pāpasya karmaṇaḥ yathā ādarśa tala prakhye paśyanti ātmānam ātmanī ati ca smṛteḥ `vividiṣanti yajñena dānena tapasā anāśakene ati `yena kenacana yajeta api darvi homena anupa hata manā eva bhavatī ati ca śruteḥ vakṣyati ca sūtra kāraḥ aata eva āśrama karma apekṣā `sarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśvavat i ati ca satyam evam yadi samāna janma anuṣṭhitam eva karma saṃskurvat  brahma jijñāsā yogyatva hetuḥ syāt  na ca naiyogike phale kāla niyamaḥ asti teva pūrva janma anuṣṭhita karma saṃskṛtaḥ  dharma jijñāsām tad anuṣṭhānam ca apratipadyamāna eva brahma jijñāsāyām pravartate iti na niyam ā iva tad apekṣaḥ atha śabdaḥ  yujyate etena ṛṇa apāka raṇa dvāreṇa api niyamena pūrva vṛtta tvam pratyuktam tathā ca śruti smṛtī `yadi vetarathā brahmacaryāt eva pravrajet `tasya āśrama vikalpam eke bruvate iti tasmāt  sādhu uktam dharma jijñāsāyāḥ prāk api adhīta vedāntasya brahma jijñāsā upapatteḥ iti atha api syāt  na hetu tvena anantara vṛtta karma avabodha apekṣam atha śabdam brūmaḥ api tu krama pratipatti artham yathā `hṛdayasya agre avadyati atha jihvāyāḥ  atha vakṣasaḥ iti tad etad ayuktam nyāya sūtre api ca eka kartṛ kāṇām bahūnām yugapad anuṣṭhāna asambha vāt avaśi ambhāvini krame brūyāt api tad niyamam atha śabdaḥ eka kartṛka tvam ca śeṣa śeṣiṇoḥ śeṣāṇām ca bahūnām eka śeṣi sambaddhānām adhikāra antara prayuktti upa jīvinām ca bhavati na itarathā na hi dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ eteṣām anyatama tve pramāṇam asti tad idim āha yathā ca hṛdaya ādi avadānānām ānantarya niyamaḥ kramasya vivakṣita tvāt  na tathā iha kramaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ śeṣa śeṣi tve adhikṛta adhikāre vā pramāṇa abhāvāt  dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ iti atha api syāt  na hetu tvena anantara vṛtta karma avabodha apekṣam atha śabdam brūmaḥ api tu krama pratipatti artham yathā ‘hṛdayasya agre avadyati atha jihvāyāḥ  atha vakṣasaḥ iti tad etad ayuktam nyāya sūtre api ca eka kartṛ kāṇām bahūnām yugapad anuṣṭhāna asambha vāt avaśi ambhāvini krame brūyāt api tad niyamam atha śabdaḥ eka kartṛka tvam ca śeṣa śeṣiṇoḥ śeṣāṇām ca bahūnām eka śeṣi sambaddhānām adhikāra antara prayuktti upajīvinām ca bhavati na itarathā na hi dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ eteṣām anyatama tve pramāṇam asti tad idam āha yathā ca hṛdaya ādi avadānānām ānantarya niyamaḥ kramasya vivakṣita tvāt  na tathā iha kramaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ śeṣa śeṣi tve adhikṛta adhikāre vā pramāṇa abhāvāt  dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ iti atha api syāt  yathā āgneya ādīnām ṣaṇṇām yāgānām ekam phalam svarga viśeṣaḥ evam dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ api ekam phalam svargaḥ tatas  krama apekṣāyām tad niyama arthaḥ atha śabda iti yathāvā dvādaśabhiḥ api lakṣaṇaiḥ dharma ekaḥ  jijñāsyaḥ pratilakṣaṇam aṃśa antara pariśodhanayā yathā avā asmin  api tantre caturbhiḥ api lakṣaṇaiḥ ekam brahma jijñāsyam tatra ca aṃśa antara pariśodhanena lakṣaṇānām krama niyamaḥ evam tantra dvayena ekam brahma jijñāsyam tatra krama niyama arthaḥ atha śabda iti āśaṅkya āha phala jijñāsya bhedāt ca dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ iti sambandhaḥ tam eva bhedam kathayati abhyudaya phalam dharma jñānam tad ca anuṣṭhāna apekṣam abhyudayaḥ phalam dharma jñānasya iti prasiddham eva na kasyacid  visaṃvādaḥ tad api na jñānasya phalam api tu jñeyasya tasya api na jñeya tvāt eva phalam kintu anuṣṭhīyamāna tvāt  niḥśreyasa phalam tu brahma jñānam na ca anuṣṭhāna antara apekṣam iti brahma jñānasya phalam apavargaḥ sa ca nitya siddhaḥ avyavahitaḥ sva saṃvedyaḥ yatas avidyā saṃsāra hetuḥ na ca avidyām anivartayantī vidyodā iti tad evam atyanta vilakṣaṇa tvāt prasthāna bhedāt ca na phala dvāreṇa api eka upanipātaḥ tena na krama ākāṅkṣā tantra dvayasya jijñāsyam punar atyanta vilakṣaṇam yatas  kāryaḥ  dharmaḥ puruṣa vyāpāra tantraḥ sva jñāna kāle asiddha sattākaḥ prathame tantre jijñāsyaḥ iha tu nitya nirvṛttam puruṣa vyāpāra anapekṣam brahma jijñāsyam kim ca codanā pravṛtti bhedāt ca idam aparam pramāṇa upādhi prameya vailakṣaṇyam dharma codanā hi prerayantī puruṣam asati viṣaye prerayitum asamarthā satī viṣayam api avabodhayati brahma pramāṇam punar bodhayati eva kevalam na avabodhe puruṣaḥ preryate avabodhaḥ  hi yathāvastu yathāpramāṇam codeti na puruṣasya icchām api anuvartate tatra kutas  preryeta yathā akṣa arthayoḥ sannikarṣe sati tena sannikarṣeṇa akṣa  agamya artha jñāne puruṣaḥ  na niyujyate tadvat  anicchataḥ api svayam utpatteḥ brahmaṇi tu nitya siddha tvāt na preraṇā sambhavati ‘brahma codane ati codanā śabdaḥ  bhāṣye pramāṇa vivakṣayā prayuktaḥ na preraṇā vivakṣayā tad āha yā hi codanā dharmasya lakṣaṇam sā sva viṣaye viniyuñjānā eva puruṣam avabodhayati brahma codanā punar  puruṣam avabodhayati eva kevalam avabodhasya codanā janya tvāt na puruṣaḥ avabodhe niyujyate yathā akṣa artha sannikarṣeṇa artha avabodhe tadvat  tad evam jijñāsi aikya nibandhanā api na krama apekṣā tantra dvayasya yena tad apekṣaḥ atha śabdaḥ  vyākhyāyeta ata upasaṃharati tasmāt  kim api vaktavyam yad anantaram brahma jijñāsā upadiśyata iti ucyate nitya anitya vastu vivekaḥ iha amutra artha phala bhoga virāgaḥ śama dama ādi sādhana sampad  mumukṣu tvam ca iti uktam purastād adhikāra artha tve atha śabdasya śāstra ārambha vaiyarthyam pravṛtti abhāvāt iti pravṛtti abhāve ca kāraṇam uktam akhila sukha bhogāt hiraṇyagarbha avāpti paryantāt nivartayati brahma jijñāsā kriyamāṇā tena tatas  udvegaḥ  lokasya kutas tatra pravṛttiḥ iti tasmāt  yāvat asya hiraṇyagarbha avāpti paryantasya bhogasya utpāda paricchedābhyām vināśi tvāt anitya tvam na avaiti vinaśyat api idam kūṭastha nitya vastu paryantam eva vinaśyati anyathā nirupādānasya punar utpatti asambhavaḥ iti vartamānasya api asambhavāt abhāvaḥ abhaviṣyat iti nirūpaṇāt  nitya anitya vastu vivekaḥ  yāvat na jāyate yāvat ca abhimukha vināśa darśanāt  bhuñjānasya api bhogān sraj  candana vastra alaṅkāra bhogān iva agni praveśa artham bhoga artha vyāpāra janita duḥkha anubhavāt ca tad nimittām nirvṛtim api alabhamānaḥ  bhogāt  viraktaḥ tatas  mumukṣu tvam tad sādhana śama dama uparama titikṣā samādhāna sampannaḥ  bhūtvā yāvat na ālambate tāvat  brahma jijñāsām kaḥ pratipadyeta kathañcid  vā daiva vaśāt  kutūhalāt vā bahu śrutatva buddhyā vā pravṛttaḥ api na nirvicikitsam brahma ātma tvena avagantum śaknoti yathā ukta sādhana sampatti virahāt  anantarmukha cetā bahis eva abhiniviśamānaḥ tasmāt  varṇita vastu kalāpa ānantaryam abhipretya atha śabdam prayuktavān ācāryaḥ tad āha bhāṣya kāraḥ teṣu hi satsu prāk api dharma jijñāsāyā ūrdhvam ca śakyate brahma jijñāsitum jñātum ca na viparyaye tasmāt atha śabdena yathā ukta sādhana sampatti ānantaryam upadiśyata iti atas śabdaḥ  hetu artha iti syāt etad  kṛtakatva paricchedau na ekāntatas kṣayiṣṇu tām gamayataḥ paramāṇuṣu pāka ja lohitasya kṛtakasya teṣām ca paricchinnānām nityatva abhyugamāt  vede api ‘akṣayyam ha vai cāturmāsya yājinaḥ sukṛtam bhavati ‘apāma somam amṛtā abhūme atyādi puṇya phalasya akṣayitva śravaṇāt  atas  viṣaya bhogāt  na niyamena virāgaḥ  vivekinām api na api kūṭastha nitya vastu avaṣṭambhena mumukṣu tvam tatas ca na śama dama ādi parigrahaḥ yatas  na tādātmyam bhoktuḥ sambhāvyate na api tad avāptiḥ duḥkha abhāve api sukha bhoga abhāvāt na anavadyaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ atas ajīrṇa bhayānna āhāra parityāgaḥ bhikṣu bhayāt na sthālyā anadhiśrayaṇam doṣeṣu pratividhātavyam iti nyāyaḥ atas  na tasya brahma jijñāsāyām hetu tvam iti atas tasya hetutva pradarśana arthaḥ atas śabdaḥ katham yasmāt veda eva agnihotra ādīnām śreyaḥ sādhanānām anitya phala tām darśayati ‘tad yathā iha karma citaḥ  lokaḥ kṣīyate evam eva amutra puṇya citaḥ  lokaḥ kṣīyate u ityādinā nanu puṇyasya api akṣayya phala tvam veda eva aha iti uktam na tasya vastu bala pravṛtta anumāna virodhe artha vādasya nityatva pratipādana asāmarthyāt  paramāṇūnām pāka jasya ca tad guṇasya anitya tvāt  atas  bhavati anityatva darśanam viṣaya bhogānām mumukṣu tve hetuḥ yad punar mumukṣutva abhāve nimittam uktam tatra āha tathā brahma jñānāt api param puruṣa artham darśayati brahma vid āpnoti param ityādi ata upasaṃharati tasmāt yathā ukta sādhana sampatti anantaram brahma jijñāsā kartavyā iti yatas  paripūrṇaḥ  hetuḥ anantaram avaśyam kāryam ārabhate atas  kartavyā iti āvaśyaka tām āha bhāṣya kāraḥ yatas  dvaita anuṣaṅgāt atitarām udvijamānena brahma ātma tvam ca hasta prāptam iva manyamānena pravartitavyam eva brahma jijñāsāyām pradīpta śirasā iva jala rāśau spṛśatā iva ca susvādu phalam aṅguli agreṇa agra pāda sthena evam satyarthāt  dharma jijñāsāyā niyamena pūrva vṛtta tvam atha śabdena pūrva uktena nyāyena nirākriyate brahmaṇaḥ  jijñāsā brahma jijñāsā iti antarṇīta vicāra artha anvaye hi caturthī samāsaḥ syāt  na śabda abhidheya iti avayava artham aṅgīkṛtya ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ  darśitaḥ brahma śabdasya artha nirdeśa avasare prāpte sūtrakāra eva nirdekṣyati iti kathayati brahma ca vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇam janma ādyasya yata iti tatra yad anyaiḥ vṛtti kāraiḥ brahma śabdasya artha antaram āśaṅkya nirasyate na khalu brāhmaṇa jātiḥ iha gṛhyate pratyakṣa siddha tvāt  jijñāsyatva abhāvāt  na api tad kartṛkā jijñāsā traivarṇikā adhikārāt na api jīva parigrahaḥ tad kartṛ tve viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyāt karma tve nitya siddha tvāt  na śabda rāśeḥ grahaṇam tasya dharma jijñāsā autpattika sūtrābhyām arthavattva pramāṇa tvayoḥ nirūpita tvāt na api hiraṇyagarbhasya tad avāpteḥ api viraktasya brahma jijñāsā upadeśāt na api tad kartṛka tā jñāna vairāgyayoḥ saha siddha tvāt  iti tad api na kartavyam iti āha ata eva na brahma śabdasya jāti ādi artha antaram āśaṅkitavyam iti brahmaṇa iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī vṛtti antare tu śeṣa lakṣaṇā vyākhyātā tām nirasyati na śeṣa iti tatra hetum āha jijñāsya apekṣa tvāt jijñāsāyā iti atha api syāt  anyat  jijñāsyam iti tad artham āha jijñāsya antara anirdeśāt ca iti punar  śeṣa ṣaṣṭhī iva ādi āha nanu śeṣa ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe api brahmaṇaḥ  jijñāsā karma tvam na virudhyate sambandha sāmānyasya viśeṣa niṣṭha tvāt iti yadi api ‘śeṣe ṣaṣṭhī ati sambandha mātre ṣaṣṭhī vihitā tathā api vyavahāraḥ  viśeṣam avalambate bahavaḥ ca sambandha viśeṣāḥ tatra avaśyam anyatamaḥ pratipattavyaḥ anyathā vyavahāra anupapatteḥ tatra prakaraṇa upapadayoḥ viśeṣa hetvoḥ abhāvāt arthāt viśeṣa kriyā upādānāt  kāraka tvena eva sambandhaḥ tatra api sa karmikāyāḥ karma kārakam abhyarhitam iti karma tvam brahmaṇaḥ  na virudhyate evam api sādhāraṇe śabde abhipretam artham vihāya artha antaram parigṛhya punar tad dvāreṇa abhipretam artham pratipadyamānasya vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ syāt  tad āha evam api pratyakṣam brahmaṇaḥ karma tvam utsṛjya sāmānya dvāreṇa parokṣam karma tvam kalpayataḥ  vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ syāt iti nanu kim iti vyarthaḥ śeṣa ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe sāmānyena yad  kiñcid  brahma sambandhi yena yena jijñāsitena vinā brahma jijñāsitam na bhavati tad sarvam jijñāsya tvena pratijñātam syāt  atas  na viśiṣṭa sambandhaḥ vivakṣyate sāmānye tasya api antar bhavāt iti yadi ucyate tad āha na vyarthaḥ brahma āśrita aśeṣa vicāra pratijñāna artha tvāt iti ca iti svayam eva para uktam āśaṅkya uttaram āha na pradhāna parigrahe tad apekṣitānām artha ākṣipta tvāt iti saṅkṣepataḥ  vastu saṅgraha vākyam etad eva prapañcayati brahma hi jñānena āptum iṣṭatama tvāt  pradhānam tasmin pradhāne jijñāsā karmaṇi parigṛhīte yaiḥ jijñāsitaiḥ vinā brahma jijñāsitam na bhavati tāni artha ākṣiptāni eva iti na pṛthak  sūtrayitavyāni yathā ‘rājā asau gacchatī atyukte sa parivārasya rājñaḥ  gamanam uktam bhavati tadvat iti yasmāt  brahma avāptiḥ puruṣa arthaḥ tena tad  jñānena āptum iṣṭatamam atas tad artha tvāt pravṛtteḥ pradhānam tad  tasmin pradhāne jijñāsyamāne yena jijñāsitena vinā na sampūrṇā jijñāsā tad  sāmarthyāt eva tādarthyena jijñāsyate na pṛthak abhidhānena kṛtyam asti yathā ‘rājā asau gacchatī atyukte yāvatā parivāreṇa vinā rājñaḥ  gamanam na sampadyate tāvataḥ  gamanam ākṣiptam iti na pṛthak abhidhīyate loke tadvat iha api svarūpa pramāṇa yukti sādhana prayojanāni brahma jñāna paripūrṇa tā artham arthāt eva jijñāsya tvāt na pṛthak  sūtrayitavyāni kiñca śāstra pravṛttiḥ eva karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhīm gamayati katham evam hi śāstram ārabdhavyam ‘puṇya citaḥ  lokaḥ kṣīyate u ityādi śruteḥ nyāyataḥ ca puṇyasya kṣaya darśanāt  viraktasya ‘brahma vid āpnoti parami atyādi śruteḥ brahma jñānāt puruṣa artha siddhiḥ para iti atas tad jñātum icchataḥ śrutyā ‘yataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti evamādyayā tad pratipādana pūrvakam ‘tad vijijñāsasva iti sākṣāt eva karma tayā jñeya tvena anuśāsanam yad  tad idam ‘atha atas  brahma jijñāse ati sūcitam tena karma ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe śruti nyāya sūcana param sūtram tad anugatam bhavati anyathā lakṣyān anugatam asambaddham syāt  tad āha śruti anugamāt ca iti vastu saṅgraha vākyam tad prapañcaḥ ‘yataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante ityādyāḥ ca śrutayaḥ ‘tad vijijñāsasva tad  brahma iti pratyakṣam eva brahmaṇaḥ  jijñāsā karma tvam darśayanti tad ca karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe sūtreṇa anugatam bhavati tasmāt  brahmaṇa iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī jñātum icchā jijñāsā iti jijñāsā padasya avayava artham kathayati icchā pradarśana artham tatas ca icchāyāḥ phala viṣaya tvāt  tad jñānasya apavarga paryanta tā sūcitā bhavati tad āha avagati paryantam jñānam sanvācyāyāḥ  icchāyāḥ karma phala viṣaya tvāt icchāyā iti avagatiḥ iti sākṣāt anubhava ucyate jñānantu parokṣe anubhavān ārūḍhe api sambhavati sannihite api asambhāvita viṣaye anavasita rūpam iti uktam purastāt  tad āha jñānena hi pramāṇena avagantum iṣṭam brahma brahma avagatiḥ hi puruṣa arthaḥ brahma rūpa tā sākṣāt karaṇam iti arthaḥ tad etad śāstra antarbhūtam sūtram anena ca prayojya sambandhinoḥ jijñāsā mumukṣā kriyayoḥ ekasyāḥ kāraṇa antara siddhāyāḥ pūrva vṛtta tayā hetu tvam arthāt upāttam itarasyāḥ tad anantaram tad prayuktāyāḥ kartavyatā śrutyā abhihitā tatra jānāti eva asau mayā etad  kartavyam iti upāyantu na veda tatas tasya upāyaḥ kathanīyaḥ śāstrasya ca sambandha abhidheya prayojanāni vaktavyāni itarathā prekṣā rahitam iva sarvam āpadyeta atas anena eva sūtreṇa idam api sarvam sūcitam iti kathayitum āha tasmāt  brahma jijñāsitavyam iti antarṇīta vicāra artha vidheyatva aṅgīkāreṇa mīmāṃsitavyam iti arthaḥ etad uktam bhavati brahma jñāna kāmena idam śāstram śrotavyam yasmāt  brahma jñānam anena śāstreṇa nirūpyate tena prayojyasya abhimata upāyaḥ śāstram iti arthāt  śāstrasya sambandha abhidheya prayojanam kathitam bhavati iti paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ādi śrī śaṅkara bhagavat pāda antevāsi vara śrī padma pāda ācārya kṛtau pañcapādikāyām prathama sūtra artha varṇanam nāma tṛtīya varṇakam samāptam tad  punar brahma prasiddham vā syāt  aprasiddham vā yadi prasiddham na jijñāsitavyam atha aprasiddham na eva śakyam jijñāsitum iti prayojana viṣaya sambandhān ākṣipati katham prasiddha śabdena pratipannam ucyate tad  yadi pratipannam anyena kenacid  tadā asya śāstrasya na viṣayaḥ kasmāt  pratipādya tvena hi viṣaya tā pratipanne ca tasmin  akiñcit karam śāstram iti na asya viṣayaḥ syāt  tatas ca anena anavagamān na asya prayojanam brahma avagatiḥ syāt  atas  prayojanam api ākṣiptam atha aprasiddham na śakyam jijñāsitum katham yad  na kadācid api buddhau samārūḍha viśeṣam katham tad  pratipādyeta atas  pratipādana aśakteḥ na tad  spṛśati api śāstram prasiddham punar yadi nāma anena pratipādyate prasiddha tvāt eva tathā api na tena arthena nirālambanam aprasiddham punar ālambanam api na syāt  atas  na kenacid arthena sambaddham śāstram iti sambandha ākṣiptaḥ asti tāvat  brahma ityādinā tritayam api samādhatte śrotṛ pravṛtti artham nanu prekṣāvatā visaṃvādakena praṇītam śāstram na īdṛśaḥ  niṣprayojanam nirviṣayam asambaddham ca ārabhate iti tad gauravāt eva pravartante śrotāraḥ kim anena prayāsena satyam bhavati sāmānyena prayojanavattva pratītiḥ praṇetṛ gauravāt  na tu tāvat mātreṇa pravṛttiḥ abhipreta prayojanāya hi pravartante na tad  nirdeśāt ṛte śakyate avagantum evam api prayojana viśeṣa eva nirdiśyatām na ca viṣaya bhāvam anāpannam aśakya pratipādanam ca prayojanam bhavati chidi kriyā viṣaya eva vṛkṣaḥ chinnaḥ prayojanam iti ucyate daṇḍa ādeḥ api mṛd viṣayasya mṛdā iva ghaṭa avasthā prayojanam satyam evam tathā api yathā cikitsā ajñānasya caraka suśruta ātreya prabhṛtīni bahūni yathā vā taṇḍula niṣpatti prayojanā avaghāta nakha nirbheda dalana kriyā bahvyaḥ tatra na avaśyam ekatra eva pravṛttiḥ tathā iha api anyasmāt api kathañcid  brahma avagati siddhau na avaśyam atra eva pravṛttiḥ atas ananya sādhāraṇaḥ  viṣayaḥ  vaktavyaḥ yathā arjunasya ayam viṣaya iti ananya sādhāraṇa tā pratīyate tena ananya sādhāraṇa tvāya viṣayaḥ  nirdeśyaḥ pravṛtti aṅga tvena sambandhaḥ api vaktavyaḥ pravṛtti aṅga tvena eva yathā sādhu śabda parijñānam vyākaraṇa ārambhāt  prāk  na kenacid sādhyate tena na kenacid  sambaddham atas tad arthī na kvacid  pravartate yathā vaudana niṣpattiḥ eka kriyā niyatā api na gamana ādi eka kriyā asādhyā tena na tayā sambandhaḥ tatas ca na gamana ādi kriyāyām odana arthī pravartate tena puruṣa artha rūpa tā ananya siddha tā tad pratipādya tā ca iti bhidyante viṣaya sambandha prayojanāni tāni ca trīṇi api pravṛtti aṅgam na apuruṣa arthe kāka danta parīkṣāyām tuṣa kaṇḍane vā pravartate prekṣāvān na api puruṣa arthe cikitsā jñāne suśruta ādi siddhe carake niyamena pravartate na api taṇḍuleṣu dalana siddheṣu avaghāte na api ananya siddhe api sādhu śabda parijñāne puruṣa arthe atad sādhane vaidyaka ādau kaścid  pravartate gamane vānodana sādhane tatra vipratipattyā ekāntatas prasiddha tām aprasiddha tām ca nirasya śakya pratipādyamāna tām ananya siddha tām ca darśayan viṣaya sambandhau samarthitavān ‘niḥśreyasa prayojanā prastūyate iti ca prayojanam nanu brahma vedāntānām viṣayaḥ śāstram ca teṣām brahma pratipādana anusaraṇa upāya nyāya viṣayam tad  katham śāstrasya viṣaya sambandhau bhavataḥ prayojanantu kadācid  syāt api praṇāḍyā dharma artha viṣayayoḥ iva śāstrayoḥ kāma avāptiḥ nanu āgneya ādīnām svarga phalānām prayāja ādi iti kartavya tāvat  vedāntānām api artham avabodhayatām itikartavya tā mīmāṃsā tena artha avabodhe vedāntānām upakāraka tvāt  bhavati śāstram api tad viṣayam na hi śāli bījasya aṅkuram janayataḥ sahakāriṇaḥ  jala ādeḥ aṅkuraḥ na kāryam tena yadi api vedāntā eva brahma avabodhe kāraṇam mīmāṃsā ceti kartavyatā bhāgam pūrayati tathā api brahma viṣayā eva na hi chettuḥ udyamana nipātana lakṣaṇaḥ  vyāpāraḥ paraśu viṣayaḥ  na vṛkṣa viṣayaḥ tad artha tvāt karaṇasya ca dvāra tvāt  anyathā anyatra kartṛ vyāpāraḥ anyatra phalam iti vaiyadhikaraṇyam syāt  ucyate viṣaya upanyāsaḥ yuktam yatra yad upakāram antareṇa phala utpattiḥ eva na sidhyati tasya api tad viṣaya tvam iha punar vinā api mīmāṃsayā sambandha grahaṇa tad anusmaraṇa buddhi sannidhāna mātra upakṛtam vākyam artham avagamayati na aparam apekṣate nanu saṃśaya viparyāsa nirāsa dvāreṇa nirṇaya hetu tvāt nirṇayasya ca nirṇeya pradhāna tvāt bhavati nirṇeyam vastu nirṇaya hetoḥ viṣayaḥ na etad sāram yatra hi anekam vijñānam vākya śravaṇe sati jāyate mīmāṃsā nirapekṣam eva tatra ekam vākya janyam eka artha niyata tvāt ekasmin prayoge vākyasya itarāṇi punar  sāmānyatodṛṣṭa nibandhanāni tatra mīmāṃsayā loka prasiddha śabda śakti anusāriṇyedam śabda janitam jñānam iti tad ālambanam veda artha  iti jñātvā anyat upekṣate na punar nirṇaya jñāna utpattau vyāpāraḥ śāstrasya yathā cakṣuḥ kutaścid nimittāt samprayukte api sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ  vā iti saṃśaya ātmakam puruṣa eva iti vā viparyaya svarūpam jñānam utpādya punar nimitta antara anugṛhītam sannirṇaya ātmakam samyak rūpam jñānam utpādayati na evam śabdaḥ  mīmāṃsāyāḥ prāk  saṃśayitam viparyastam vā jñānam utpādya punar tadanu mahān nirṇaya ātmakam samyak jñānam vā janayati kintu prāk eva mīmāṃsā anugrahāt sva sāmarthya janyam jñānam ajījanadeva tasmāt na brahma viṣayam śāstram atra ucyate yadi api vākya artha jñānam śāstra anugrahāt prāk eva udeti tathā api sva utpatti sama kāla samutthena tatra sāmānyatodṛṣṭa nibandhanena artha antara niveśinā sama kakṣa abhimatena jñānena virodhāt unmajjana nimajjanam iva anubhavat asyām avasthāyām saṃśaya jñāna koṭi nikṣiptam sat  mīmāṃsayā śabda śakti anusaraṇe sati pratipakṣa jñānasya anutpattau nimajjana abhāvāt niścalam nirṇaya jñānam iva jātam iti lakṣaṇayā mīmāṃsayā nirṇayaḥ kriyata iti ucyate na punar  sākṣāt nirṇaya jñāna hetu tvāt tad evam lakṣaṇayā vedāntānām brahma viṣayāṇām sahakāri kāraṇam mīmāṃsā iti brahma jñāna viṣayam śāstram abhidhīyate tad ca idam trayam api avaśyam vaktavyam prayojanam viṣayaḥ sambandhaḥ ca śāstra ādau śrotuḥ pravṛtti aṅga tvena yadi api praṇetṛ gauravāt eva sa prayojana tvam śāstrasya tathā api na prayojana viśeṣa siddhiḥ tad pratyaya mātreṇa nirdeśāt ṛte tasmāt tad nirdeśyam nirdiṣṭe api tasmin  tasya aśakya pratipādana tām manvānaḥ  vihata śraddha tvāt na pravarteta iti sādhyaḥ  nirdeśyaḥ śakya pratipādana pratipattau  api anyatas  siddhe arthe nirdiṣṭe na eva pravṛttiḥ iti ananya sādhyaḥ api nirdeśyaḥ tad etad trayam ekatra samavetam vibhaktam ca upalabhyata iti alam ati vistareṇa ‘asti tāvat  brahme atyādinā prasiddhatva pradarśanena aprasiddha tām nirākurvan śakya pratipādya tayā sambandham samarthitavān katham brahma śabdaḥ tāvat jāti jīva kamala āsana śabda rāśīnām na anyatama abhiprāyeṇa sūtre prayuktaḥ anupapatteḥ iti uktam atas  nūnam anyat eva kiñcid abhidheyam abhipretya ayam prayukta iti gamyate tena svarga apūrva devatā ādi arthavat pada prayogāt eva kaścid arthaḥ asti iti avasīyate na etad sāram na hi padam cakṣuḥ ādivat apratīta pūrva eva arthe jhaṭiti vijñānam janayati yena apūrvam anyatas asiddham artham pada prayogāt eva pratīmaḥ svarga ādi arthaḥ api na eva pada prayogāt eva siddhaḥ atra ucyate yasmin vākya ekam padam muktvā itareṣām padānām arthaḥ prasiddhaḥ sa kim eka padārthān avagama aparādhena tyajyatām uta bahu padārtha prasiddhi balena aprasiddhaḥ api kathañcid agamyeta iti tatra nigama nirukta vyākaraṇānām evaṃrūpa padārtha anugama hetūnām vidyamāna tvāt  tad balena artham anugamya vākya artha avagatiḥ yuktā na punar eka aprasidhyā prasiddha padārtha saṃsargaḥ tyaktum yuktaḥ na hi prasiddhiḥ aprasidhyā tyajyate prasiddhi balena aprasiddham api kalpyata iti nyāyāt  nanu nigama ādi vaśena artha anugame sarvatra eva kathañcid artha anvayasya anugantum śakya tvāt avyavasthitaḥ padārthaḥ syāt  tatas ca vākya arthaḥ  na avadhāryeta na tarhi nigama ādīnām arthavat tā bhavati arthavat tā yatra sva arthāt anyatra api viniyogāt  prayogaḥ tatra katham abhidadhyāt  iti apekṣāyām tad gatasya eva avayava artha anvaya leśasya anugamāt evam tarhi eka artha niyamāya prayoga paratantra tā mṛgyate tad antareṇa api prayogam eka artha niyama eva kathañcid nigama ādi vyāpriyeta iti na kaścid  doṣaḥ tad atra brahma śabde vyutpādyamāne bṛṃhateḥ dhātoḥ vṛddhi karmaṇaḥ artha anugamāt prayoga anugame ca asati viśiṣṭa artha viṣayasya apekṣika mahat tvasya aparigrahāt sarvatas  niravagraha mahattva sampannam vastu vākya artha anvayi brahma padāt anugamyate tatas ca kāla kṛta avaccheda nimittasya alpa tvasya abhāvāt  sadā sattvāt nityam kiñcid vastu brahma padāt  pratīyate tathā rūpa antara sadbhāve tad rūpa vikala tvāt tad avaccheda kṛtam alpa tvam syāt  tad ca brahma padāt eva apāsyate tasmāt ekarasam advaitam vastu brahma padāt  pratīyate etena deśa kṛtaḥ api paricchedaḥ  nirākṛtaḥ veditavyaḥ vastu antara sadbhāve hi tad apekṣayā etāvati sadbhāvaḥ na atas  paramasti iti syāt  etasmāt  vyāvṛtta iti tad abhāve na paricchinna buddhiḥ bhavati buddha tvam ca bṛhatī artha anvayāt eva katham abodha ātmakam hi vastu bhogyam atas  bhoktāram prati śeṣa tvāt nikṛṣṭam cetanaḥ punar na kasyacid guṇa bhāvam eti tena utkṛṣṭam sarvasmāt  buddha svarūpam kiñcid  iti bṛhatti artha anvayam eva anusṛtya gamyate amuktam iti ca avidyā kāma karma paratantraḥ tairitaḥ ca amutas ca paśuvat nīyamānaḥ  nikṛṣṭaḥ  bhavati brahma śabdaḥ tu sva artha prakṣepeṇa vācyam kiñcid gamayan sadā eva avidyā ādi saṃsāra bījān ākalita tayā tasya utkṛṣṭa mahat tvam āvedayati ‘sarvajñam sarva śakti samanvitam ca tad i ati brahma śabdāt eva avagamyate katham yadi kiñcid aviditam tena kutaścid vā kāryāt  vyāvartate śaktiḥ āpekṣikaḥ tadā utkarṣaḥ syāt  na tad yuktam anyatas asiddhasya vastunaḥ pada prayogāt eva pratipattau siddhe hi vastuni prayoge tasya yathāsiddham eva mahat tvam nirucyate śabdāt eva tad artha anvaya pratītau niraṅkuśa eva arthaḥ abhyupetavyaḥ evam ca bṛṃhateḥ arthaḥ paripūrṇaḥ  bhavati yadi sarvam asya sākṣāt eva saṃvid gocare vaśe ca varteta tad etad āha asti tāvat  brahma nitya śuddha mukta svabhāvam sarvajñam sarva śakti samanvitam brahma śabdasya hi vyutpādyamānasya nitya śuddhatva āt ayaḥ arthāḥ pratīyante bṛṃhateḥ dhātoḥ artha anugamāt iti nanu evam api vyutpatti anusaraṇena bhavati evam ātmake vastuni pratītiḥ na punar etāvatā tasya siddhiḥ pada mātrasya apramāṇa tvāt  satyam evam ata eva jijñāsā dharmasya iva loka ākhya pramāṇa ābhāsa siddhasya idam aparam brahma śabda arthasya siddha tve kāraṇam ucyate sādhyatva sidhi artham sarvasya ātma tvāt ca brahma astitva prasiddhiḥ iti tad eva darśayati sarvaḥ  hi ātma astitvam pratyeti na na aham asmi iti yadi na ātma astitva prasiddhiḥ syāt  sarvaḥ  lokaḥ  na aham asmi iti pratīyāt  ātmā ca brahma iti katham punar ātmā brahma vedānteṣu ātmani brahma śabda prayogāt  ātmānam eva ca lokaḥ aham iti vyapadiśati tad evam ahaṃpratyaya eva brahmaṇaḥ prasiddha tvāt  na aprasiddhi śaṅkā yadi tarhi loke brahma ātma tvena prasiddham asti tatas  jñātam eva iti ajijñāsya tvam punar āpannam iti viṣayam ākṣipati asiddham hi vastu sādhyamānam viṣayaḥ siddham tu na punar  sādhyate iti na śāstrasya viṣayaḥ na tad viśeṣam prati vipratipatteḥ iti viṣaya sambandhau samarthyete satyam aham iti ātmani pratyayaḥ ātmā ca brahma kintu tasmin  eva vipratipattayaḥ ayam asau ayam asau  iti tāḥ ca vastu tas  brahma padārtha viṣayā eva tad eka artha tvāt  brahma śabdasya tatas  sāmānyatas  prasiddham api viśeṣataḥ asiddheḥ asiddha kalpam eva iti bhavati asya viśeṣa siddhi hetoḥ viṣayaḥ sāmānyatas  siddha tvāt ca śakyate viśeṣataḥ pratipādayitum iti bhavati tasya śāstram sādhanam iti sambandhaḥ api samarthitaḥ vipratipattim darśayati deha mātram ityādi tad yathā gaḥ śabdasya vyakti ākṛti jāti kriyā guṇa sāsnā ādi aneka artha sannidhau prayujyamānasya kaiścid jātiḥ anyaiḥ vyaktiḥ ityādi abhidheyam pratipannam evam sa caitanya kārya kāraṇa saṅghāta sannidhau  ahaṃpratyayasya utpadyamānasya kaiścid  kiñcid ālambanam pratipannam tad āha deha mātram caitanya viśiṣṭam ātmā iti prākṛtā janā lokāyatikāḥ ca pratipannā iti tathā hi ‘manuṣyaḥ aham i ati ātmani manuṣyatva abhimānaḥ  ‘gacchāmī ati ca gantṛtva abhimānaḥ  deha viṣayatva upapadyate ‘deha mātram i ati sa śiraska piṇḍa abhiprāyam draṣṭavyam mātra śabdena na deha atiriktam svatantram caitanyam anya viśeṣaṇam vā kintu deha ākāra pariṇata bhūta catuṣṭaya antar bhūtam eva iti darśayati ātmā iti ahaṃpratyaya ālambanam iti arthaḥ prākṛtā iti śāstra upadeśa asaṃskṛta matayaḥ dṛṣṭa mātra avikalpita vyavahāriṇa iti arthaḥ lokāyatikā iti bhūta catuṣṭaya tattva vādinaḥ prasiddhāḥ evam indriyāṇi eva cetanāni ātmā iti apare indriyāṇām cakṣuḥ ādi manaḥ paryantānām ekaikasmin  asati api śarīre rūpa ādi jñānānām abhāvāt teṣām eva vyastānām cetana tvam ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tvam ca manyante krameṇa varagoṣṭhīvat itaretara guṇa bhāvam tathā ca indriya dharma sāmānādhikaraṇyam ahaṃpratyayasya dṛśyate ‘kāṇaḥ aham mūkaḥ aham i atyādi manaḥ eva cetanam ahaṃpratyayasya viṣayam anye manyante dṛśyate hi svapna indriya daśaka uparame api manasa eva ‘aham i ati sarva vyavahāra āspadatvam iti vadantaḥ vijñāna mātram kṣaṇikam iti eka iti mātra grahaṇena na aham iti ākāra ādi varṇa traya atiriktam kiñci d avabhāsate yad ahaṃpratyayasya viṣayaḥ kalpyeta tena vijñānam eva sva rasa bhaṅguram avirata udayam akhila loka yātrā nilayam anubhava bhagna pakṣa antaram aham iti utpadyata iti anye manyante śūnyam iti apara iti suṣupte vijñāna leśasya api abhāvāt akasmāt eva aham iti samudaya darśanāt akāraṇasya kādācid kasya parama artha vastutva abhāvāt asat avabhāsa eva ahaṅkāra iti apare saṅgirante asti deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ saṃsārī kartā bhoktā iti apara iti aham ullekha śūnyasya bhoktṛ tvasya adarśanāt  tasya ca pratyabhijñānāt  sthiratva siddheḥ sthirasya ca avadhi hetu anupalabdheḥ nitya tvam nirvikārasya ca bhoga asambhavāt vikārasya ca kriyā phala tvāt kriyā veśa ātmaka tvāt ca kartṛ tvasya evam ātmaka tvāt ca saṃsāri tvasya deha ādeḥ ca buddhi paryantasya bhoktṛ tvā anupapatteḥ tad vyatiriktaḥ saṃsārī kartā bhoktā ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya iti apare pratijānate katham punar tad vyatirikta tvam manyante tasya bhoktṛ tvā anupapatteḥ iti uktam katham tasya bhoktṛ tvā anupapattiḥ iti ucyate bhūta saṅghātaḥ tāvat  śarīram tatra vyastānām samastānām vā yugapad  krameṇa vā bhogaḥ parikalpyeta sarvathā api asambhavaḥ yadi tāvat  vyastānām yugapad  parikalpyeta tatas  sva artha prayukta tvāt  pravṛtteḥ aṅga aṅgibhāvaḥ  na avakalpeta na ca aṅga aṅgi bhāvam antareṇa saṅghāta upapadyate tasmāt na vyasteṣu yugapad  bhogaḥ asti tarhi krameṇa virodhāt vara goṣṭhīvat iti na etad evam yuktam tatra bhogyasya asādhāraṇa tvāt asādhāraṇa tvañca prati puruṣa niyamāt  iha punar viparītam bahūnām sannidhau sādhāraṇe ca bhogye pratiniyata bhoga vyavasthā hetu asambhavāt  astu tarhi samūhasya tila jvālāvat cetanā samanvaya upapatteḥ mā bhūt  pratyekam yugapad  krameṇa vā na etad evam bhogeṣu samūhā sambhavāt katham asambhavaḥ bhoktuḥ bhogam prati prādhānyāt  nanu bhoge api samūhaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ yathā strīpuṃsayoḥ na etad  sāram sandigdha tvāt  samūhasya uta tad vyatiriktasya iti tila jvālā āyāntu viparītam samūha kārye samūhinām guṇa bhāva upapatteḥ astu ekasya tarhi niyataḥ  bhogaḥ na tatra api kasya ekasya iti anavadhāraṇāt kim avadhāraṇena vinā api tena vivakṣita artha upapatteḥ yadi evam sameṣu keṣāñcit guṇa bhāva anupapatteḥ ayuktaḥ kārya ātmakeṣu evam kāraṇa ātmakeṣu api samānaḥ carcaḥ bhūta svābhāvya aviśeṣāt tathā ubhaya ātmake samūhe tasmāt  deha ādi vyatiriktam ahaṃpratyaya viṣayam manyante bhoktā eva kevalam na kartā iti eka iti pūrva uktasya eva deha ādi vyatiriktasya kartṛ tvam atad svabhāvam manvānā bhoktā eva kevalaḥ ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya iti eke prasthitāḥ karomi jānāmi bhuñje ca iti na sarvadā ahaṃpratyayena anuṣaṅgaḥ tena na ayam tad viṣayaḥ yadi syāt  na tad ullekha vikala udiyāt  nanu bhoktā api tarhi na asau tad ullekhā bhāvāt na etad evam aham iti cetanatva samullekhāt  tad artha tvāt sarvasya tad ātmakam eva bhoktṛ tvam iti bhoktā eva kevalam iti yuktam manyante asti tad vyatirikta īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva śaktiḥ iti kecid iti tasmāt api deha ādi vyatiriktāt ahaṃpratyaya viṣayāt anyaḥ sarvasya īśitā tatas ca īśitavyasya sarva ātmanā vettā niyamana śakti sampannaḥ ca śarīriṇām manasā api acintya rūpāt tanu bhuvana viracana kāryāt prekṣāvat kartṛka tvam antareṇa asambhāvyamānāt kulāla ādiḥ iva ghaṭa ādi kāryāt pratipannaḥ sa atiśayānām kāṣṭhā prāptiḥ pariṇāmānām upalabdhā sa atiśayañca jñānam atas  kvacid  kāṣṭhām prāptam sarva viṣayam iti sarva vid  sarvadā siddhaḥ īśvaraḥ pratipannaḥ  brahma śabda artha iti kecid  pratipedire nanu ‘aham iti sarvaḥ  loka ātmānam pratyeti ātmā ca brahme ati ahaṃpratyaya viṣayasya ātmanaḥ  brahma tvena tad vipratipattau brahma vipratipattim darśayitum prakrāntam tad  katham anahaṃpratyaya viṣaye anātmani īśvare brahmatva vipratipattiḥ pradarśyate ucyate brahmaṇi vipratipatti pradarśanasya prakrānta tvāt ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya vipratapattyā api praṇāḍyā brahma vipratipattiḥ eva nirdiśyate yatas  na ahaṃviṣaya vipratipatti pradarśanena kiñcid  kṛtyam asti tasmāt  sādhu etad  ātmā sa bhoktuḥ iti apara iti yaḥ ayam aham iti ullikhyamānaḥ cetanaḥ bhoktā sa brahma iti kaiścid pratipannaḥ tasya ahaṃpratyaya siddhaḥ  bhoktṛ tvā avabhāsaḥ sa mithyā eva anirvacanīyāna ādi vidyā vila sitaḥ paramārthataḥ tu yaḥ sarvajña īśvaraḥ ahaṃpratyaye anantarbhūtaḥ pramāṇa antara anavasitaḥ saḥ asya ātmā svarūpam evam asau bṛṃhati artha anvayāt  brahma śabda abhidhānīyatām labhate itarathā tad rūpa vikalasya na niraṅkuśam bṛhat tvam iti na brahma śabda abhidheyaḥ syāt  evam bahavaḥ  vipratipannā yukti vākya tad ābhāsa samāśrayāḥ santaḥ iti upasaṃharati evam uktena prakāreṇa kecid  kiñcid  brahma iti pratipannāḥ kim evam eva manoratha mātreṇa na iti āha yuktim pramāṇānām sva viṣaya niścaye anugrāhikām tarka śabda paryāyām vākyañca prativeda antam yathāvat  brahma svarūpa pratipādana parama ālocayantaḥ ‘a ātmā sa bhoktuḥ i ati yukti vākya abhyām antyam pakṣam niścitavantaḥ samyak darśinaḥ itare tu yuktaya iva avabhāsanta iti yukti ābhāsāḥ na paramārtha taḥ  yuktayaḥ tāḥ samāśritya vākyāni iva avabhāsante na tāni vākyāni atatparatvāt  tāni vākya ābhāsāni parigṛhya pakṣa antareṣu vipratipannāḥ yuktyā abhāsa tvam leśataḥ  darśitam eva deha ādi vyatirikta ātma pakṣam darśayadbhiḥ itareṣām yukti ābhāsa siddha tvam sva avasare darśayiṣyāmaḥ darśitam ca leśata uttara uttara pakṣa grahaṇa kāraṇa pradarśanena vākya ābhāsa tām tu tatra tatra adhikaraṇe siddha antayiṣyantaḥ pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ tatra avicārya yad  kiñcid  pratipadyamānaḥ  niḥśreyasāt  pratihanyeta anarthañceyāt iti tatra evam sthite mumukṣuḥ brahma jñānena param niḥśreyasam āptu kāmaḥ avicārya etad śāstram aśrutvā pravartamānaḥ antya pakṣāt arva ācīnam kañcid  pakṣam parigṛhṇīyāt  tadā mokṣasya samyak  jñāna phala tvāt tasya ca ātathā bhāvāt niḥśreyasāt pratihanyeta mokṣa phalam na prāpnuyāt  anarthañca pratipadyeta ‘andham tamaḥ praviśanti ye ke ca ātma hanaḥ  janāḥ iti śruteḥ anātma darśanena ātmanaḥ asat kalpatva āpādanam ātma hananam evaṃrūpasya ātma hananasya kṛta tvāt  anyathā ātmanaḥ  hanana asambhavāt  prāṇatyāgasya prakṛta anupayogāt iti tasmāt  brahma jijñāsā upanyāsa mukhena vedānta vākya mīmāṃsā tad avirodhi tarka upakaraṇā niḥśreyasa prayojanā prastūyata iti brahma jijñāsā upanyāsa vyājena jijñāsā padena antarṇītamī māṃsā vedānta vākyānām ārabhyate athavā brahma jñāne kartavya tayā upadiṣṭe tad jñānāya pravṛttebhyaḥ arthāt eva tad pratipādanam pratijñātam iti tad artham vedāntamīmāṃsa ārabhyate kimprayojanā kim upakaraṇā ca iti ucyate tad avirodhi tarka upakaraṇā niḥśreyasa prayojanā ca iti taiḥ vedāntaiḥ avirodhī tarkaḥ yuktiḥ upakaraṇam itikartavya tā sahakāri kāraṇam iti yāvat  athavā tarkaḥ anumānam vedāntaiḥ aviruddham tad artha pratīteḥ eva dṛḍhatva hetu tayā upakaraṇam asya iti arthaḥ iti paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ādi śrī śaṅkara bhagavat pāda antevāsi vara śrī padma pāda ācārya kṛtau pañcapādikāyām viṣaya prayojana ākṣepa parihāra varṇanam nāma turīya varṇakam samāptam yuktiḥ api lakṣaṇa nirṇaye arthāt  sūtritā eva janma utpattiḥ ādiḥ asya iti tad guṇa saṃvijñānaḥ  bahuvrīhiḥ iti pada  chedaḥ padārthaḥ pada vigraha iti etad  tritayam api vyākhyāna aṅgam sampādayati tad guṇa saṃvijñāne prayojanam āha janma sthiti bhaṅgam samāsārtha iti tṛtīya liṅga nirdeśāt saṃhati pradhānam samāsa arthaḥ nanu ādiḥ pūrva kāla koṭimataḥ bhavati tad abhāve prapañcasya kaḥ  nāma ādiḥ iti āśaṅkya āha janmanaḥ ca ādi tvam śruti nirdeśa apekṣam vastu vṛtta apekṣam ca iti yad anena sūtreṇa lakṣitam brahma tad svarūpa kathana param vākyam tatra ādau janma nirdiṣṭam iti tasya ādi tvam vastu svabhāva apekṣam api na hi vastu pralīya tiṣṭhati sthitvā vā jāyate na api janitvā eva pralīyate kṣaṇikatva nirākaraṇāt  atas  janitvā sthitvā pralīyate evam anādiḥ ayam prapañcaḥ ‘asya iti bhāṣyeṇa pada bhāgasya idamaḥ prakṛti mātrasya artha nirdeśaḥ tathā hi sarvatra sarva nāma prakrama ādi kāraṇa antara balena katipaya abhidheya param tad abhāve sva mahimnā pramāṇa viṣaya mātra abhidhāyakam tena āha pratyakṣa ādi sannidhāpitasya dharmiṇa idamā nirdeśa iti ṣaṣṭhī janma ādi dharma sambandha artha iti sarva eva iha sambandhaḥ sambhavati na tad viśeṣa ādaraṇīya iti kathayati yata iti kāraṇa nirdeśa iti prakṛtitva nibandhanā hi pañcamī na anya nibandhana iti darśayati asya jagataḥ ityādinā bhāṣyeṇa lakṣyasya brahmaṇaḥ svarūpa lakṣaṇam kathayitum upakramate dvividham hi lakṣaṇam upalakṣaṇam viśeṣa lakṣaṇam ca tatra idam lakṣaṇam prapañca dharma tvāt  pṛthak bhūtam eva kāraṇam upalakṣayati na viśeṣaṇa tvena atas  pṛthak  sva lakṣaṇa kathanam nāma rūpābhyām vyākṛtasya iti kārya prapañcam kecid  sva prakriyā anusāreṇa vibhajanti tad vyudāsāya prasiddha artha anuvāda śruti balena dvairāśyam kṛtvā āha nāma rūpābhyām iti ittham bhāve tṛtīyā vyākriyamāṇam hi vastu abhidheya rūpam sva nāma garbham vikalpa pūrvam eva vyākriyata iti sva saṃvedyam etad  aneka kartṛ bhoktṛ saṃyuktasya iti kartṛtva bhoktṛ tvam api nāma rūpa ātmaka tvāt prapañca anuyāyi iti darśayati pratiniyata deśa kāla nimitta kriyā phala āśrayasya iti pratikarma phala upabhoge niyataḥ  deśaḥ svarga phalasya meru pṛṣṭham grāma ādi phalasya bhū maṇḍalam kālaḥ api svarga phalasya deha pātāt ūrdhvam putra phalasya bāla bhāvāt  nimittam api uttarāyaṇa ādi maraṇasya manasā api acintya racanā rūpasya iti na hi arvāk darśī kvacid bahis loka sanniveśa prakāram adhyātmam ca pratiniyata artha kriyā samartha avayava śirā jāla sanniveśam nirūpayitum api samarthaḥ kim punar viracayitum janma sthiti bhaṅgam yatas  sarvajñāt sarva śakteḥ kāraṇāt  bhavati tad  brahma iti vākya śeṣa iti sa ākāṅkṣasya sūtra vākyasya ākāṅkṣita pada pūraṇam upalakṣita brahma svarūpam lakṣaṇam ca darśayati nanu anye api pariṇāma ādayaḥ  bhāva vikārāḥ santi te kim iti na saṅgṛhyante iti āśaṅkya āha anyeṣām api iti na kvacid vastunaḥ  hi avasthā viśeṣaḥ  vināśa rahitaḥ na api anirvṛtta janmanaḥ asthita svabhāvasya vināśaḥ atas triṣu eva antar bhāvāt na pṛthak upanyāsaḥ teṣām nanu ṣaṣ  bhāva vikārā iti nairuktāḥ teṣām grahaṇe antarbhāva ukti prayāsaḥ api parihṛtaḥ syāt iti āśaṅkya āha yāska paripaṭhitānām tu jāyate asti ityādīnām iti pṛthivī ap tejaḥsu jagat racanā rūpa sthiteṣu tad mayānām eva te sambhāvyante tatas tad grahaṇe teṣām eva brahma tvena lakṣitatva āśaṅkā syāt  na ca tad yuktam atas  sūtra arthavat tvāya śruti nirdiṣṭā eva utpatti ādayaḥ  gṛhyante tad artha nirṇaya artha tvāt sūtrāṇām atas  yad avaṣṭambhaḥ  viśvaḥ vivartate prapañcaḥ tad eva mūla kāraṇam brahma iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu śruti nirdiṣṭa grahaṇe sūtram artha śūnyam syāt  na hi imām pṛthivīm jāyamānām paśyāmaḥ na apaḥ  na tejaḥ katham siddhavat lakṣaṇatva una upādīyeta iti ucyate tejasaḥ tāvat araṇi nirmathana ādiṣu dṛśyate janma indhana apāye vināśaḥ apām api candrakānta ādiṣu janma krameṇa ca śoṣaḥ pṛthivyāḥ  api avayava saṃyoga vibhāga darśanāt tad nimittau janma vināśa  anumīyete dṛśyeta ca adya api avayava saṃyoga vibhāga kṛtau pṛthivī eka deśasya janma vināśau vāyu ākāśa kāla diśām api ‘yāvat vikāram tu vibhāgaḥ  lokavat i ati vakṣyamāṇena nyāyena sta eva janma vināśau na yathā ukta viśeṣaṇasya ityādinā bhāṣyeṇa yuktiḥ api brahma svarūpa nirṇaya āya anena eva sūtreṇa tantreṇa āvṛttyā vā janma ādyasya yatas  sambhavati iti sūtritā iti darśayati asya jagataḥ  nāma rūpābhyām vyākṛtasya ityādi abhihita viśeṣaṇa catuṣṭayasya yathā ukta viśeṣaṇam īśvaram muktvā iti sarvajñam sarva śaktim vihāya na anyatas  para parikalpitāt  pradhāna ādeḥ acetanāt  cetanāt api paricchinna jñāna kriyā śakteḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ  hiraṇyagarbhāt  utpatti ādi sambhāvayitum api śakyam acetanāt tāvat acetana tvāt eva anupapannam cetanāt api paricchinna jñāna kriyā śakti tvāt abhāvāt  punar na acetana tvāt eva kevalāt anupapattiḥ api tu nirupākhya tvāt atīta kalpa saṃskāra abhāvāt pūrva kalpa eka rūpaḥ  vartamānaḥ api kalpa iti pramāṇa abhāvāt  sarva eva vyavahāraḥ  yādṛcchika iti na kvacid  kaścid niyamaḥ abhaviṣyat  na ca svabhāvataḥ viśiṣṭa deśa kāla nimitta upādānāt iti svabhāvaḥ  nāmānya anapekṣaḥ tena apekṣā eva anupapannā kutaḥ niyama sambhavaḥ atas  yuktyā api vastu antarasya kāraṇatva sambhāvanā nirākaraṇena pāriśeṣyāt pūrva ukta viśeṣaṇa īśvara eva kāraṇam iti siddham etad eva anumānam iti yā iyam yuktiḥ abhihitā yathā ukta viśeṣaṇam īśvaram muktvā na anyatas  jagataḥ  janma ādi sambhavati iti etad eva svatantram anumānam īśvara siddhau sarvajñatva sarva śaktitva siddhau ca tasya pramāṇam kim veda vākyaiḥ iti īśvara kāraṇinaḥ kaṇāda prabhṛtayaḥ manyante janma ādi sūtra lakṣitāni api vākyāni ‘yataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante ityādīni para artha anumāna vākya samāni dṛśyanta iti vadantaḥ nanu iha api tad eva upanyastam iti yathā dhūma viśeṣasya agaru sambhava tvam tathā prapañca sanniveśa viśeṣasya sarvajñatva ādi guṇa kāraṇaka tvam iti na vedānta vākya kusuma grathana artha tvāt sūtrāṇām iti satyam tad eva upanyastam upakaraṇa tvena na tatra tātparyam tātparyantu veda vākya grathane tad eva prapañcayati vedānta vākyāni iti samanvaya sūtra pramukha upāttaiḥ śabda śakti anusāribhiḥ nyāyaiḥ vākyānām brahmaṇi tātparyā adhyavasāna nirvṛttā brahma avagatiḥ na anumāna ādi pramāṇa antara nirvṛttā satsu tu vedānta vākyeṣu tad avirodhi anumānam api pramāṇam bhavat na nivāryate śrutyā eva sahāya tvena tarkasya api abhyupeta tvāt tathā hi ‘śrotavyaḥ  mantavyaḥ iti śrutyā yathā śravaṇam brahma avagati hetuḥ anūdyate tathā mananasya api siddhavat anūdyamāna tvāt  tathā aparā śrutiḥ ‘paṇḍitaḥ  medhāvī atyādiḥ ‘ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  vede ati puruṣa buddhi sāhāyyam ātmanaḥ  darśayati yad ācāryeṇa śruti anusāriṇā sphaṭika ādi nidarśanena śiṣyebhyaḥ pratyaya dārḍhya āpādanam tadācāryavān puruṣaḥ  veda iti anūdyate na dharma jijñāsāyām iva ityādinā yukti sāhāyya apekṣaṇe kāraṇam āha śruti ādaya iti śrutiḥ pada antara nirapekṣaḥ śabdaḥ ādi śabdena liṅga vākya ādayaḥ śabda prakārā gṛhyante na ta eva brahmaṇi pramāṇam kintu anubhava ādayaḥ api tatra hetum āha anubhava avasāna tvāt  bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt ca brahma jñānasya iti siddhe vastuni sambhavati anubhavaḥ tad avasānā ākāṅkṣā nivṛttiḥ yatas  nanu dharma jijñāsāyām vinā api anubhavena śabda śakti anusaraṇa mātreṇa eva nirākāṅkṣam phala paryantam jñānam bhavati na tarka gandham api apekṣate tathā iha api syāt  pramāṇatva aviśeṣāt vedānta vākyānām iti āśaṅkya viśeṣam āha kartavye hi viṣaya ityādinā brahma jñānam api vastu tantram eva bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt iti antena bhāṣyeṇa katham kartavyam hi kartavya tvāt eva asiddha svabhāvam na anubhavitum śakyam iti na tad ākāṅkṣā iha tu siddhasya sākṣāt rūpeṇa viparyāsa gṛhītasya samyak jñānena sākṣātkaraṇam antareṇa na mithyājñāna udaya nivṛttiḥ dvi candra ādiṣu tathā darśanāt  na hi
