kartavya siddhārtha niṣṭhayoḥ pramāṇatva sāmyāt avabodhana prakāre api sāmyam yadi syāt  puruṣa icchā vaśa niṣpādyam api syāt  tatas  vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpa samuccaya utsarga apavāda bādha abhyuccaya vyavasthita vikalpa ādayaḥ api prasajyeran na vastuni yuktam etad  niḥsvabhāvatva prasaṅgāt  tathā ca ekasmin vastuni sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ  vā iti vikalpaḥ na vaikalpika dravya tyāgavat  samyak jñānam bhavati sthāṇuḥ eva iti niścitā eka artha tā parama arthe yatas  vastu svabhāva paratantram siddha vastu jñānam na jñāna paratantram vastu yadi syāt  śukti rajatam api tathā syāt  kartavya jñānam punar vaiparītye api samyak eva ‘yoṣā vāva gautama agniḥ i atyādiṣu darśanāt  tatra ivam sati brahma jñānam api vastu tantram eva bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt atas  yuktaḥ  yukteḥ anupraveśaḥ anubhava apekṣā ca na itaratra aparaḥ paricodayati nanu bhūta vastu viṣayatva ityādinā ayam abhiprāyaḥ bhūta tvāt  yukteḥ api ced anupraveśaḥ tathā sati kim veda vākyaiḥ vicāritaiḥ yathā āhuḥ īśvara kāraṇinaḥ tathā bhavatu pūrva sūtreṇa pratijñā nirdeśaḥ anena ca hetu abhidhānam iti uttaram āha na indriya ādi viṣaya tvena sambandha grahaṇāt ityādinā indriyāṇi prapañca mātram gṛhṇanti na tad kāraṇam yadi tad grahaṇam api syāt  na anumāna upanyāsena kṛtyam asti sāmānyatodṛṣṭam api na pramāṇam atīndriye brahmaṇi ata upasaṃharati tasmāt janma ādi sūtram na anumāna upanyāsa artham kim tarhi vedānta vākya pradarśana artham iti yuktim api tad upakaraṇām tad artha anubhava prayojanām sūcayati iti uktam nanu evam sati katham yuktiḥ abrahma viṣayā satī tad viṣayāṇām vākyānām upakaraṇam bhavati ucyate brahma pareṣu mṛd ādi dṛṣṭānteḥ yuktasya upanyasyante tāḥ ca vidhi pratiṣedha vākyayoḥ pravartakatva nivartakatva ākāṅkṣita stuti nindā artha vādavat  svarūpa vākyasya phala paryanta apekṣita sambhāvana artha vāda tām pratipadyamānāḥ tatra śruti sāhāyye vartanta iti ucyate kimpunaḥ tad  veda vākyam yad  sūtreṇa iha lila kṣayiṣitam iti sarvatra vedānta vākye brahma padasya aprasiddha tvāt na sva artham viśeṣya tvena viśeṣaṇa tvena vā vākya arthe samarpayitum alam iti ākṣipati yeṣām vedānta vākyānām yena sanniveśa krameṇa brahma pratipādane samanvayaḥ svādhyāya pade sthitaḥ tad lakṣaṇa artham sūtra dvayam iti tathā eva udāhaṇam āha bhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ iti atha śabda upātta nyāyena prathama sūtrasya udāharaṇam ‘yataḥ  vā imāni bhūtānī ati janma ādi sūtrasya katham pūrva uktena nyāyena pṛthivī ādīnām janma ādi darśanāt  tad kāraṇa ekatva nānā tvayoḥ anyatara avagame pramāṇa abhāvāt  buddhimat kāraṇa pūrva tā mātre pratipanne ‘yataḥ  vā imānī ati kāraṇasya eka vacana nirdeśāt tad artha mātrasya eva vidhitsita tvāt arthāt sarvajñam sarva śakti jagat kāraṇam iti kāraṇa viśeṣaḥ  vākyāt avagamyate punar tad vijijñāsasva iti anūdya tad  brahma iti tatra brahma śabda prayogāt  bṛhatī artha anvayena sarvatas anavacchinna svabhāvam jagat kāraṇam brahma padārtha  iti gamyate tasya ca nirṇaya vākyam ānandāt hi eva khalu iti prasiddha avadyotakena hi śabdena saṃyuktam ānanda avadyotakam upapadyate anānanda ātmake hi jagat kāraṇe brahma śabda prayogaḥ  na yujyate na hi tasya upekṣaṇīye viṣaye sva artha prakṣepeṇa vṛttiḥ samañjasā tasmāt  brahma pare vākye janma ādi dharma jātasya upalakṣaṇa tvāt  brahma saṃsparśa abhāvāt sarvajñam sarva śakti samanvitam parama ānandam brahma iti janma ādi sūtreṇa brahma svarūpam lakṣitam iti siddham iti paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ādi śrī śaṅkara bhagavat pāda antevāsi vara śrī padma pāda ācārya kṛtau pañcapādikāyām janma ādi adhikaraṇam nāma pañcama varṇakam samāptam atha saptamam varṇakam atha vā yathā ukta mṛgveda ādi ityādinā sūtrasya pramāṇa pratijñām artha antaram āha apekṣita tvāt  katham punar ekasya sūtrasya artha dvayam sūtra tvāt eva tathā ca paurāṇikāḥ ‘alpa akṣaram asat digdham sāravat viśvatomukham astobhamanavadyam ca sūtram sūtra vidaḥ  viduḥ iti viśvatomukham iti nānā artha tām āha atas alaṅkāra eva sūtrāṇām yad aneka artha tā nāma nanu pūrva sūtre śāstram udāha ratā brahma avagame śāstram pramāṇam pratijñātam eva satyam etad sūtra balena tad udāhṛtam anyathā sūtre śāstra upādāna abhāvāt anumāna āśaṅkāyām ‘yataḥ sarvajñāt sarva śakteḥ kāraṇāt jagataḥ  janma ādi bhavati tad  brahma iti vākya śeṣaḥ iti asya upaskārasya apramāṇatva prasaṅgaḥ pratiprapañcam pṛthak kāraṇa janma tāyā api sambhavāt  sarvajñatva sarva śaktitva asiddheḥ loke ca jagat kāraṇe brahma śabda prayoga adarśanāt  atas  ‘janmādyasya yatas ‘śāstra pramāṇa kam i ati etāvat idam sūtram sat asat digdham anumāna śaṅkā nivṛtteḥ pṛthak karaṇam prapañca antaḥpātinaḥ śāstrasya api hetu tvena sarvajña tvam su sampādam iti vyākhyāna antareṇa kathayitum iti paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ādi śrī śaṅkara bhagavat pāda antevāsi vara śrī padma pāda ācārya kṛtau pañcapādikāyām brahmaṇaḥ śāstra pramāṇaka tvam nāma saptamam varṇakam samāptam tad tu samanvayāt  tad  brahma sarvajñatva ādi guṇakam vedānta śāstrāt pratīyata iti pratijānīte hetum ca ācaṣṭe samanvayāt iti tatra tātparyeṇa vedānta vākyānām samanvayāt iti arthaḥ samyak anvayaḥ samanvayaḥ atha kā iyam samyakta anvayasya padānām paraspara anavacchinna arthānām ananyā kāṅkṣāṇām avyatirikta eka rasa prātipadikā artha mātra anvayaḥ ‘saḥ ayam i atyādi vākya stha padānām iva prakṛṣṭa prakāśa śabdayoḥ iva candra pada abhidheya artha kathanena tathā ca vyakti viśeṣaḥ kaścid candra prātipadikā abhidheyaḥ kenacid  pṛṣṭaḥ ‘asmin jyotiḥ maṇḍale kaḥ candraḥ nāma iti tasya prativacanam ‘prakṛṣṭa prakāśaḥ candraḥ iti tad evam prativacanam bhavati yadi yathā candra padena uktam tathā ābhyām api padābhyām ucyeta evam ca sati nīlotpalavat ayuta siddha paraspara avacchinna viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena api anvayaḥ durlabhaḥ kutas  pṛthak siddhaḥ kriyā kāraka lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ tathāvidhāni udāharati sat eva somya idam agra ityādīni nanu janma ādi sūtra udāharaṇeṣu eva prāmāṇyam darśanīyam kim uda āharaṇa antareṇa bāḍham asti atra abhiprāyaḥ  bhāṣya kārasya tatra brahmaṇaḥ  lakṣaṇam vaktavyam iti taṭa sthasya eva brahmaṇaḥ  nirūpakāṇi vākyāni udāhṛtāni iha tu ‘tattvam asī ati jīvasya brahma ātma tā avagati paryantāni vedānta vākyāni na taṭa stham eva jagat kāraṇam pratipādya paryavasyanti iti atas tathābhūtāni eva vākyāni udāhṛtāni ‘sat eva somya idam agra āsīdi ati evamādīni yad punar  siddhe vastuni pratyakṣa ādi sambhavāt tad abhāve mithyātva āśaṅkāyām aprāmāṇyam iti tad  rūpa ādi abhāvāt  na indriya gocara iti pratyuktam nanu indriya agocara tvāt eva pratyakṣa ādya viṣaya tvāt na śabda mātrasya tatra prāmāṇyam iti uktam ucyate yadi api śabda mātrasya pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya eva prayogaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ vyutpattā tu katham vyutpadyate iti vācyam śrotṛ vyavahāraḥ  hi mūlam bālānām vyutpatteḥ sa ca śrotuḥ jñāna antara animitta tā pariśuddhaḥ śabda sāmarthya avagama hetuḥ atas  na pratipattuḥ jñāna antara asiddha artha avabodhaka tvam sāmarthya avagama kāle avagatam tena anavagamya eva tad viṣayam jñānam sāmarthya avagamaḥ yathā avagamam ca vijñāna utpattiḥ yadā punar vyutpannaḥ sa svayam prayuyukṣate para pratipattaye tadā jñāna antara sannidhāpitam sva sākṣikam vivakṣan sāmarthya avagama kāle api tayoḥ sattām pratipadyate kevalam na jñāna utpattau tayoḥ upayogam tasmāt na śabdasya pramāṇa antara gṛhīta artha prakāśane sāmarthyam vyutpatti kāle avagatam kintu cakṣuḥ ādivat anya nirapekṣaḥ  yathā avagata sāmarthyaḥ ca śabdaḥ  vijñānam janayati tasmāt na prameyasya pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya tvam śabdasya vijñāna janana upayujyate api ca apauruṣeye śabde cakṣuṣi iva vijñāna utpattau  anapekṣe katham aprāmāṇyam āśaṅkyeta nanu uktam āśaṅkā kāraṇam sparśana gocara citra nimna unnata viṣayasya cākṣuṣasya pratyayasya tad saṃvāda abhāvāt apramāṇa tvam na tad sādhūktam aduṣṭa karaṇa tvāt asya tasya ca tad abhāvāt tathā hi śabdaḥ tāvat apauruṣeya tvāt aduṣṭaḥ prameyasya punar jñāna hetu tve na pramāṇam asti śabdasya eva tad eka niṣṭhatvena tad niyamāt  citrasya tu cākṣuṣa jñāne sāmagrī antaḥpātinaḥ śyāma ādi rekhā sanniveśa viśeṣaḥ  doṣaḥ tad abhāve timira abhāva iva samyak darśana utpatteḥ atas  pravartamānam api pramāṇam saṃvādakam eva iti na aprāmāṇyam āvahati na ca saṃvāda lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam api tu bodha lakṣaṇam iti pramāṇa vidān sthitiḥ atas  yathā eva vidhi vākyānām sva artha mātre prāmāṇyam evam sva rūpa vākyānām api anavagata artha pariccheda sāmānyāt  nanu vidhi vākyānām eva prāmāṇyam yuktam kriyā artha tvāt āmnāyasya na itaretara āśraya tvāt vidhi vākyānām eva hi prāmāṇye siddhe kriyā artha tvam āmnāyasya siddhyet  kriyā artha tve ca siddhe teṣām eva prāmāṇyam iti itaretara āśraya tvam syāt  na hi ekam api anyatas  siddham atas  yad avagamaya ti āmnāyaḥ tad arthaḥ saḥ tasmāt  yathākāryam avagamayan  tad arthaḥ evam aikātmyam api avagamayan  tad arthaḥ  bhavitum arhati pratīti kṛta tvāt prāmāṇyasya pratītiḥ tu kāryā aikātmyayoḥ tulyā pratyakṣa ādiṣu api etad eva pramāṇa vṛttam yad anavagatam avagamyate āha yuktam pratyakṣa ādīnām tāvat  prāmāṇyam apekṣa antara abhāvāt āmnāyasya tu adhyayana vidhinā upādāpitasya na punar  puruṣa artham aprāpya paryavasānam labhyate vidhāna anarthakya prasaṅgāt tasmāt aikātmya vākyānām sva artha mātra niṣṭhatā na yuktā ucyate puruṣaḥ  hi etāvat apekṣate iṣṭam me syāt aniṣṭam me mā bhūt iti na tu ittham anyathā vā iti na ca asya svayam īṣṭe dvividham ceṣṭam prepsati kiñcid prāpyam yathā grāma ādi kiñcid prāptam api yathā bhrāntyā hasta gatam eva vismṛta suvarṇa ādi aniṣṭam api dvividham parijihīrṣati kiñcid  parihāryam yathāgarta ādi kiñcid parihṛtam api bhrāntyā yathā rajju ādi sarpa ādi buddhi gṛhītam tatra prāpya parihāryayoḥ sādhana jñāna āyatta tvāt puruṣa arthasya vidhi pratiṣedhau  arthavantau itarayoḥ tāvat  bhrānti mātra vyavahita tvāt na tad apanayāt anyat  puruṣa artha tvena apekṣate tad apanayaḥ ca tattva jñānāt  bhavati na anyathā evam api labhyamānam puruṣa artham anumanyata eva puruṣaḥ sutarām ca abhinandati sa dhana āyattaḥ  hi āyāsāt labhyeta jñāna āyatte tu āyāsaḥ api parihriyate tena aneka anartha kaluṣitam iva ātmānam manyamānasya bhrāntasya sarva anartha śūnya ātma tattva pratipādanāt eva puruṣa artha siddheḥ aikātmya vākyānām sva artha mātra niṣṭhatve api na vidhyānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt  siddham brahmaṇaḥ śāstra pramāṇa tvam iti paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ādi śrī śaṅkara bhagavat pāda antevāsi vara śrī padma pāda ācārya kṛtau pañcapādikāyām vedāntānām brahmaṇi samanvayanirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭamam varṇakam samāptam atha navamam varṇakam atra apare pratyavatiṣṭhante yadi api śāstreṇa pramīyate brahma tathā api vidhi saṃsparśinā na tad rahitena kasmāt evam anyathā śabda prayoga anupapatteḥ puruṣa icchā samutthāpitaḥ  hi śabda prayogaḥ sā ceṣṭā aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra viṣayā na ca pāramparyeṇa api sukha duḥkhe vihāya iṣṭa aniṣṭe sambhavataḥ na ca vismṛta suvarṇa āropita sarpa raśanā pratipattau  iva tad anantaram śāstrāt api brahma ātma pratipattau sukha avāptiḥ duḥkha parihāraḥ ca dṛśyate pūrvavat  saṃsāritvā upalabdheḥ prati iti uttara kālam ca dhyāna upadeśāt tasmāt  santu nāma loke vidhi rahitāni api puruṣa artha paryantāni vākyāni vede tu na tad rahitānām tad paryanta tā tasmāt  yadi api jijñāsya vailakṣaṇyam dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ siddha sādhya viṣaya tvena tathā api ‘saḥ anveṣṭavyaḥ u ‘sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ u ityādi vidhiṣu kaḥ asau  ātmā iti ākāṅkṣāyām sarva eva brahma svarūpa paraḥ pada samanvayaḥ tad samarpaka tvena upayuktaḥ na svatantram eva brahma pratipādayitum alam atas  vidhīyamāna jñāna karma kāraka tvena eva brahma pratipādyata iti yaḥ punar  ‘tasmāt  pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā eva śāstra pramāṇakam brahma abhyupagantavyam i ati bhāṣye pūrva pakṣa upasaṃhāraḥ tatra pratipatti śabdaḥ sarva eva manaḥ vyāpāraḥ pramāṇa ātmaka itaraḥ  vā brahma saṃsparśi tvena vidheyaḥ kaiścid  kathañcid  kalpitaḥ tasya sarvasya saṅgraha arthaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ atra ucyate kim idam jñānam brahma karmakam vidhīyate na tāvat śabda janyam svādhyāya pāṭhāt eva tad siddheḥ atha śabda janyasya eva jñānasya abhyāsaḥ  vidhīyata iti na tasya prayojanam paśyāmaḥ nanu iṣṭa viṣayasya jñāna santānasya sukha santāna hetu tvam dṛśyate yadi evam tadvat eva vidhyānarthakyam atha punar  sākṣātkaraṇāya jñāna santāna vidhiḥ ucyate na etad yuktam na hi dṛṣṭa adhikāraḥ  vidhiḥ asambhāvita dṛṣṭa phalaḥ  bhavati na hi laiṅgikaḥ arthaḥ  liṅga janmanā eva jñānena sahasraśas api abhyasyamānena sākṣātkriyate mā bhūt  śābda jñānāt eva abhyasyamānāt sākṣāt bhāvaḥ tad janmanaḥ  jñāna antarāt bhaviṣyati na ittham bhāve pramāṇam asti astu tarhi śabdāt  pratipannasya yathāpratipatti dhyānam nāma manaḥ vyāpāraḥ  vidhīyata iti kimartham tasya vidhānam dhyeya sākṣātkārāya ced  na tasya sambhavaḥ na hi parokṣam dhyāyamānam sākṣāt bhāvam āpadyamānam dṛṣṭam nanu dṛṣṭam parokṣam api dhyāyamānam sākṣāt bhāvam āpannam kāma ādi upaplave mā evam na tad  dhyāyamānam apitva vidyā ātmakam anyathā bādhaḥ  na bhavet  nanu ‘draṣṭavyaḥ iti darśanam anūdya ‘nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti dhyānam darśana phalam vidhīyate uktam etad  na dṛṣṭa adhikāraḥ  vidhiḥ asambhāvita dṛṣṭa phalaḥ  bhavati iti na hi dhyānam dhyeya sākṣāt bhāva hetuḥ kvacid  dṛṣṭam atha api bhavatu nāma dhyānāt  dhyeya sākṣāt bhāvaḥ  dhyeyasya tathā tve kim pramāṇam śabdaḥ tāvat sākṣāt karaṇa upāya upāsana vidhāne paryavasitaḥ  na tad sadbhāve satyam tathā api tattvam sidhyati vakṣyamāṇena devatā vigrahavattva nyāyena viṣama upanyāsaḥ tatra hi na tathā tve sādhakam bādhakam vā iti pratīti śaraṇaiḥ tathā abhyupeyate na tathā iha sarvasya ātma tve pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt āropita rūpeṇa api dhyāna upapatteḥ pūrva ukteṣu api jñāna vidhi pakṣeṣu anayā eva diśā vastu tathātva siddhiḥ nirākāryā yad punar  kaiścid ucyate śābda jñānāt anyat eva jñāna antaram alaukikam vedānteṣu kartavya tvena vidhīyata iti tatra vadāmaḥ tad punar  kiṃsādhanam kiṅkarma ca iti vaktavyam na hi anavagata karma kārakam jñānam vidhātum śakyam avagate ca tasmin vidhāna ānarthakyam sādhanam api na vihitam tena vinā sa ākāṅkṣam vacanam anarthakam bhavet  ‘tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣantī atyādinā vacanena sādhanam veda anuvacana ādi vihitam eva iti ced  pramāṇa antarasya tarhi pramāṇam śabdaḥ  na ātma tattvasya na etad upapadyate kārya gamyam hi prāmāṇyam na vidhi gamyam tad uktam ‘guṇāt vā api abhidhānam syāt sambandhasya aśāstra hetutva ādi ati tad evam ayuktam etad  vidhi samanvaye śāstra pramāṇa tvam brahmaṇaḥ atha api ‘atha yad atas  paraḥ  divaḥ  jyotiḥ i ati prapañca atirikta brahma abhyupagame devatā vigrahavattva nyāya sambhavāt  mokṣa kāmasya brahma upāsanam vidhīyate tathā ca śrutiḥ ‘vidyayā tadā ārohantī ati na ca sādhya tve api antavat tvam śabda gamya tvāt anāvṛtteḥ ‘na ca punar āvartate u iti na hi eṣa tarka gamyaḥ yena tarkeṇa asya tattvam vyavasthāpyeta śabda gamyasya tu śabdāt eva tattva vyavasthā iti manvānasya uttaram āha bhāṣya kāraḥ na karma brahma vidyā phalayoḥ vailakṣaṇyāt iti vastu saṅgraha vākyam etad  asya eva prapañcaḥ atas  na kartavya śeṣa tvena brahma upadeśaḥ  yukta iti etad antam bhāṣyam asyāmam arthaḥ saṅkṣepataḥ śrutitaḥ  nyāyataḥ ca mokṣasya nitya siddhatva pratīteḥ na kriyā asādhyaḥ  mokṣa iti katham yadi sandhyā upāsanavat mānasam brahma karmakam upāsanam nāma dharmaḥ  mokṣa phalaḥ svarga ādi phala yāgavat vidhīyate tathā sati śarīravatā eva tad phalam bhoktavyam iti ‘a śarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ u iti aśarīra mokṣa anuvādaḥ  yogya priya apriya sparśana abhāva anuvādaḥ ca nirālambanau syātām na ca aśarīra tvam eva dharma kāryam svābhāvika tvāt tasya tena anuṣṭheya vilakṣaṇam mokṣa ākhyam aśarīra tvam svabhāva siddham nityam iti siddham tathā api kathañcid pariṇāmi nityam syāt  syāt api kadācid dharma kāryam idantu kūṭastha nityam brahma jijñāsya tvena prakrāntam yad svarūpa avagamaḥ  jīvasya mokṣaḥ abhipreyate tatra yadi hasta gata vismṛta suvarṇa ādivat  bhrānti mātra vyavahitam mokṣam pratyākhyāya brahma viṣaya dhyāna kriyātaḥ  devatā viṣaya yāga ādivat prīti viśeṣaḥ  bhogyaḥ  mokṣaḥ kalpyeta tatas teṣu eva tāratamya avasthiteṣu yāga phaleṣu ayam api tathābhūtaḥ syāt  tatas  ‘tad yathā iha karma citaḥ  lokaḥ kṣīyate evam eva amutra puṇya citaḥ  lokaḥ kṣīyate u iti liṅga darśana upabṛṃhita nyāya avagata anitya tvaḥ  mokṣaḥ prasajyeta na ca tathā abhyupagamaḥ  mokṣa vādinām atas  na kartavya śeṣa tvena brahma upadeśaḥ  yukta iti upasaṃhāraḥ yad punar  ‘na ca punar āvartate u iti śāstra avagatam nitya tvam na tarkeṇa apanetum yuktam iti tad ayuktam vartamāna apadeśa tvena tathā abhāve pramāṇa apekṣaṇāt  na ca kāryasya nitya tve pramāṇam asti paramāṇūnām pākajaḥ  guṇa u nitya tve na udāharaṇam prakriyā mātra siddha tvāt kim ca teṣām iha na punarāvṛttiḥ ‘imam mānavam āvartam na āvartante iti śrutiḥ iha imam iti viśeṣaṇāt asmin kalpe anāvṛttim darśayati na anavadhikām anāvṛttim api ca abhyupetya brahmaṇaḥ kriyā anupraveśam mokṣasya anityatva doṣa uktaḥ na tu kriyā anupraveśam kṣamate vedānta vākya gataḥ pada samanvayaḥ tathā ca ‘brahma veda brahmā eva bhavatī atyādyāḥ śrutayaḥ brahma vidyā anantaram mokṣam darśayanti aḥ  madhye kārya antaram vārayanti vedana brahma bhavanayoḥ eka kālatva nirdeśāt atas  na viditasya kriyāyām viniyogaḥ tathā ‘taddha etad paśyan  ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede iti brahma darśana sarva ātma bhāvayoḥ eka kālatva nirdeśāt  madhye kriyā antaram vārayati paśyan  iti śatṛ pratyayaḥ ‘lakṣaṇa hetvoḥ kriyāyāḥ iti kriyāyāḥ  hetu bhūtāt dhātoḥ śatṛ pratyaya smaraṇāt  kriyāyāḥ ca avyavahite hetumati hetu tvāt  yathā ‘tiṣṭhan gāyatī ati tiṣṭhatigāyatyoḥ madhye kriyā antara abhāvaḥ pratīyate tadvat  atra na sthiti kriyā sāmarthyāt eva gīti kriyā nirvṛttiḥ api tu prayatna antarāt śabdataḥ na tayoḥ madhye kriyā antara pratītiḥ iti etau  atā uda āharaṇam iha punar na sarva ātma bhāvasya brahma darśana atirekeṇa prayatna antara apekṣā vidyate kim ca ‘tasmai mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ pāram darśayatī atyādyāḥ śrutayaḥ tamasaḥ  mithyājñānasya mokṣa vyavadhāyinaḥ apanayana mātram darśayanti na mokṣam kriyā asādhyam itas ca etad evam anye api nyāya vidaḥ  mithyājñāna apāye tad anantaram duḥkha abhāvam nirvāṇam darśayanti mithyājñāna apāyaḥ ca brahma ātmā ekatva vijñānāt bhavati na kriyātaḥ katham gamyate ‘indraḥ  māyābhiḥ puru rūpa īyate iti mithyā eva bheda avabhāsaḥ tasya pratipakṣāt abheda avabhāsāt apanaya iti gamyate atha api sya at na ekatva vijñānam yathā avasthita vastu viṣayam yena mithyā rūpam bheda avabhāsam nivartayet  api tu sampad ā ādi rūpam vidhitaḥ puruṣa icchayā kartavyam iti sampad nāma alpam api vastu ālambanīkṛtya kenacid sāmānyena darśana mātrāt mahat vastu sampādanam tatas ca tad phala avāptiḥ phalasya eva vā sampādanam yathā manasaḥ  vṛtti anantatva sāmānyena ananta viśvadeva sampādanam kṛtvā ananta loka jayaḥ evam jīvasya cit rūpa sāmānyena brahma rūpa sampādanam kṛtvā brahma phalam avāpyata iti adhyāsa sva brahmaṇi mana āditya ādau brahma dṛṣṭyā upāsanam jīvasya api brahma dṛṣṭyā upāsanam sampādya ālambanam avidyamāna samam kṛtvā sampādyamānasya eva prādhānyena manasā anucintanam adhyāse tu ālambanasya eva prādhānyena anucintanam kriyā yogaḥ  vāyoḥ agni ādīnām samharaṇāt saṃvarga guṇa tvena upāsanam evam jīvasya sva gatena bṛṃhati artha yogena brahma iti upāsanam kārya antareṇa guṇa bhūtasya brahma dṛṣṭiḥ saṃskāra ājyasya iva avekṣaṇam atra uttaram sampad ā ādi rūpe hi ityādi tathā sati tad tvam asya ādi vākyānām nirupacarita brahma ātmā ekatva avagama paraḥ pada samanvayaḥ  vinā kāraṇena sva icchā mātreṇa sampad ā ādi paraḥ parikalpyeta tad avagama nimittam ca mithyājñāna apāya pūrvikā vismṛta hasta gata suvarṇa avāptivat brahma avāptiḥ phalam anubhava ārūḍham apahnūyeta ‘na iha nānā asti kiñcane ati ca bheda abhāva śrutiḥ uparuddhi eta tasmāt na sampad ā ādivat puruṣa vyāpāra tantrā brahma vidyā kintu pratyakṣa ādi janita jñānavat aparāmṛṣṭa hāna upādāna vastu sva rūpa mātra niṣṭhā iti abhyupagantavyam tatra ivam sati katham brahma pratipati uttara kālam karmakāraka tām nīyeta tad tad jñānam vā tad adhigama phala paryantam sat  vidhi viṣayaḥ  bhavet  atas  mithyā eva bheda avabhāsaḥ tasya pratipakṣāt abheda avabhāsāt apanayaḥ tasmāt  mithyājñāna nivṛtti mātram mokṣa iti śruti nyāyābhyām siddham nanu vidhi kriyā karma tāvat bhavati brahma tatas  kriyā sambandhe sambhāvite bhavati vidheḥ avasara iti āśaṅkya āha na ca vidhi kriyā karma tvena ityādi āha saḥ ayam śānti karmaṇi vetāla udayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ kriyā anupraveśam nirākartum jñāna kriyāyāḥ  api viṣaya tvam nirākurvatā tatas  eva śāstra yoni tvam api nirākṛtam eva tad āha aviṣaya tve brahmaṇaḥ śāstra yonitva anupapattiḥ iti ced iti atra uttaram na avidyā kalpita ityādi śāstram hi saḥ ayam ityādi laukika vākyavat  brahmaṇi pramāṇam tathā hi saḥ ayam iti deśa kāla bhedhā upādhi pravilayena abhedaḥ avagamyate tathā tvam padārthaḥ api ātmānam ahaṃrūpam manyamānaḥ tattvam asi vākyāt tad padārtha eka tām upagacchan saḥ ayam itivat aham ātmaka idam aṃśa upādhi kṛtavedya vedita vedanā ātmaka prapañcena arthāt pralīyamānena avacchidya vicchidyamāna anidamprakāśaḥ pramāṇa phalam darśitaḥ tad api avacchedaka vināśe tadā eva vijahat nirviśeṣa tām āpadyate tena pramāṇa ādi catuṣṭayasya yugapad pralaye api tad avaccheda anubhava phalam vākya nibandhanam atas  veda eka gocaraḥ  nirvāṇam iti veda vidaḥ pratipedire tathā ca evaṃvidhasya pramāṇa vyāpārasya prakāśaka amantra brāhmaṇa vādā bhāṣye darśitāḥ evam ca nitya mukta ātma svarūpa samarpaṇāt na mokṣasya anityatva doṣaḥ yasya tu utpādyaḥ  mokṣa ityādinā tasmāt  jñānam ekam mukttvā kriyāyāḥ  gandha mātrasya api anupraveśa iha na upapadyate iti antena bhāṣyeṇa avidyā nivartanena nitya mukta ātma svarūpa samarpaṇam mokṣam vihāya kriyā anupraveśam kalpayataḥ api na tasya tatra sambhava iti darśitam katham yadi tāvat utpādyaḥ  vikāryaḥ  vā mokṣaḥ tadā yadi api kriyā anupraveśaḥ  yuktaḥ tathā api mokṣasya dhruvam anitya tvam iti uktam ‘na karma brahma vidyā phalayoḥ vailakṣaṇī ādi atyādi bhāṣyeṇa atha anityatva parihārāya sthitasya eva api atvam ucyate tad api na ātma svarūpasya kriyā pūrva kāpyatva anupapatteḥ vyatireke api sarva gata tvena nitya prāpta tvad ākāśena iva na kriyā apekṣā prāptiḥ atha vikārāvartinaḥ api ‘atha yad atas  paraḥ  divaḥ  jyotiḥ dīpyate u iti śrūyamāṇasya prāptaye kriyā apekṣā iti na vikāra deśe api brahmaṇaḥ  vikāra saṃsparśa abhāvāt aviśeṣāt  atha vikārāvarti eva brahma na vikāra deśe asti tena tad prāptaye kriyā apekṣā iti sā tarhi tad prāptiḥ ātmanaḥ tādātmya āpattiḥ uta svena eva rūpeṇa tatra avasthānam yadi pūrva kalpaḥ tadā svarūpa nāśaḥ atha dvitīyaḥ saṃyogasya viprayoga avasāna tvāt punarāvṛttiḥ na ca apunarāvṛtti śrutiḥ vartamāna apadeśinī tathā abhāve pramāṇa antaram apekṣamāṇā svayam pramāṇībhavati saṃskārya tvam api na sambhavati guṇa doṣayoḥ ādheya apaneyayoḥ tatra asambhavāt  atha vidyamānasya abhivyaktiḥ ādarśasya iva nigharṣaṇena tad ca na ātmanaḥ kriyā rahita tvāt  anya āśrayāyāḥ tu na viṣayaḥ pratyagrūpa tvāt  nanu īśvara abhidhyānāt mala apagamaḥ  bhaviṣyati dīpa prabhayā iva ghaṭa avaguṇṭhanena tamaḥ apanayaḥ ucyate kim asau malaḥ parama arthaḥ san uta avidyā ātmakaḥ yadi parama arthaḥ san na tarhi sva āśraya vikāram antareṇa apasārayitum śakyaḥ na hi vikāra ātmanaḥ sambhavati avikāritva śruteḥ atha avidyā ātmakaḥ na tarhi avidyāvat gatena samyak jñānena vinā tasya apanayaḥ loke tathā dṛṣṭa tvāt  anyathā ca adṛṣṭa tvāt  na ca snāna ādi kriyayā iva saṃskāryatva sambhavaḥ ahaṅkartuḥ idam aṃśasya eva tatra saṃskārya tvāt  tasmāt na saṃskāryaḥ api mokṣaḥ iti upasaṃharati atha api tu anyat api kriyā phalam asti tad dvāreṇa mokṣasya kriyā anupraveśaḥ syāt iti āśaṅkya āha atas anyat mokṣam prati ityādi na hi dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam vā kriyā phalam utpatti ādi catuṣṭaya atiriktam śakyam kenacid  darśayitum tasmāt jñānasya eva mokṣaḥ  gocaraḥ na kriyāyāḥ nanu jñānasya api na gocaraḥ  brahma iti uktam ‘na ca vidikriyā karma tvena kārya anupraveśaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ iti vadatā satyam karma tvam jñānam prati niṣiddham na punar anupayoga eva ekāntatas  jñānasya abhihitaḥ tathā ca tatra eva upayoga prakāraḥ  darśitaḥ avidyā parikalpita bheda nivṛtti paratvāt ityādinā bhāṣyeṇa mā tarhi vocaḥ kriyāyāḥ  gandha mātrasya api anupraveśa iha na upapadyata iti nanu jñānam mānasī kriyā na vailakṣaṇyāt iti uttaram katham vailakṣaṇyam ajanya phala tvāt  uktam ajanya phala tvam ahaṅkāra ṭīkāyām idam aparam vailakṣaṇyam jñānam na codanā janyam vastu janyam hi tad  vastu ca jñānāt prāk eva svarūpe vyavasthitam atas tad tantram jñānam na tad  jñānena anyathā kartum śakyam atha api syāt  bhavet pratyakṣam vastu janyam anumāna ādiṣu katham tatra api liṅga ādi paratantram na codanāyāḥ tatra anupraveśaḥ kim ca na codanā janyam jñānam ekāntatas  vastu paricchedakam yoṣa ādiṣu agni ādi dṛṣṭi vidhāna darśanāt atas  vastu viṣayasya jñānasya kriyā tve api na codanā janya tvam na vā puruṣa tantra tvam api tu pramāṇa vastu paratantra tvam evam samyak jñānatva upapatteḥ agnau  iva agni jñānasya evam sati brahma ātmā ekatva vijñānasya api yathā bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt na codanā janya tvam atas  na vidheḥ atra avakāśaḥ atas  śrūyamāṇā api vidhayaḥ kevala pramāṇa vastu paratantre jñāne akiñcitkara tvāt  kuṇṭhībhavanti atas artha vāda tayā ātma jñānaḥ tāvaka tvena tad unmukhīkaraṇāt sāmarthya siddha bahis mukha tā nirodhāt ca vidhi kārya leśasya vidyamāna tvāt vidhaya iva lakṣyante tathā ca śravaṇam nāma ātma avagataye vedānta vākya vicāraḥ śārīraka śravaṇam ca mananam vastu niṣṭha vākya apekṣita dundubhi ādi dṛṣṭānta janma sthiti laya vācā ārambhaṇatva ādi yukta artha vāda anusandhānam vākya artha avirodhi anumāna anusandhānam ca nididhi āsanam mananā upabṛṃhita vākya artha viṣaye sthirībhāvaḥ vidheyasya upāsana aparyāyasya niṣphala tvāt  darśanam atas  vākya arthe sthairyāt nirasta samasta prapañca avabhāsa vijñāna ghana eka tā anubhavaḥ kaḥ punar atra artha vādaḥ idam atra prastutam kriyā kāraka phala ātmakāt saṃsārāt viraktāyai maitreyyai mumukṣave mokṣa sādhanam ātma jñānam pratipipāt ayiṣan ‘na vā are patyuḥ kāmāya patiḥ priyaḥ  bhavatī ati pati ādeḥ īpsita tvam pratiṣidhya ātmana īpsitatama tvam āha nanu na eva ātmana īpsitatama tvam ucyate kintu pati ādīnām eva ātma artha tayā īpsita tvam ucyate ‘a ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya patiḥ priyaḥ  bhavatī ati mā evam na hi tasmin  aniṣṭe tad artham iṣṭam bhavati tasmāt anena upāyena ātmana eva īpsita tvam uktam īpsitaḥ ced  ‘draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ iti eṣaḥ artha vādaḥ etad ca sarvam prathama sūtreṇa eva sūtritam vivṛtam ca bhāṣye api ca na eva ayam vidhau kṛtyaḥ kim tarhi ‘arhe kṛtya tṛcaḥ ce ati arhe kṛtyaḥ etena u ‘a ātmā iti eva upāsīta ‘a ātmānam eva lokam upāsīte ati evamādīni vidhi  chāyāni vākyāni vyākhyātāni veditavyāni atas  hāna upādāna śūnya ātmā avagamāt eva kṛtakṛtya tā pratīyate śruti smṛti vādānām ca tathā prasthita tvāt  tasmāt na pratipatti vidhi viṣaya tayā brahmaṇaḥ samarpaṇam iti upasaṃharati tasya ayam arthaḥ na pramāṇa ātmakena itareṇa vā jñāna vyāpāreṇa vidhīyamāna tvena kalpitena saṃsparśaḥ  brahmaṇa iti yad api kecid āhuḥ ityādi asya ayam arthaḥ yadi sva rūpa mātra niṣṭhaḥ api veda bhāgaḥ asti tatas  idam pūrva uktam pratiṣṭhām labhate anyathā kriyā anupraveśa atiriktam aveda artha  eva syāt iti asya uttaram tad na aupaniṣadasya puruṣasya ananya śeṣa tvāt iti vastu saṅgraha vākyam asya eva prapañcaḥ yaḥ asau  upaniṣatsu eva adhigata ityādiḥ asya ayam arthaḥ yaḥ ayam ahaṃpratyaya viṣayāt kriyā sambandhyātmanaḥ atiriktaḥ sama ekaḥ sarva bhūteṣu ahaṅkartuḥ api sākṣi bhūtaḥ na sa kenacid pramāṇena siddhaḥ yena kriyā aśeṣa tām nīyeta na hi pramāṇa antara asiddhaḥ kriyā sambandhi tayā upadeṣṭum śakyaḥ na ca sa na pratīyata iti yuktam vaktum tad pratipādaka upaniṣad pada samanvayasya darśita tvāt  ata eva aupaniṣadatva viśeṣaṇam ananya viṣaya tvāt  tad ca vedāntānām tad paratve avakalpate na eṣa pratīyamānaḥ api śukti rajatavat mithyā iti śakyam vaktum bādhā bhāvāt  itas ca na śakyate mithyā iti viditum tasmin  aupaniṣade puruṣe ‘sa eṣaḥ ‘nā iti na iti ātma śabda prayogāt  ātmanaḥ ca anirākārya tvāt  ya eva nirākartā tasya eva ātmatva prasaṅgāt  na ca tasya kadācid abhāvaḥ sambhavati abhāva hetūnām aviṣaya tvāt na ca nirhetukaḥ  vināśaḥ citeḥ eka rūpa avabhāsena kṣaṇa bhaṅga nirākaraṇāt  atas avaccheda traya śūnye tasmin svayam prakāśa māne sarvasya puruṣa avadhiḥ vināśaḥ sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ tad evam asaṃsārya ātmani pramāṇa antara agocare vedānta vākya samanvayāt pratīyamāne katham tad paraḥ  veda bhāgaḥ  na bhavet  katham vā pratīyamānaḥ  nirākriyeta nanu ‘āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt ānarthakyamatad arthānāmi atyakriyā arthānām padānām artha śūnya tvam śāstra tātparyavida āhuḥ tasmāt pravṛtti nivṛtti vyatirikta artha vādinām nirālambana tvāt  tatas  vastu avagamaḥ sāmānyatodṛṣṭa nibandhanaḥ  bhramaḥ tena pravṛtti nivṛtti anupayogi vastu na śabdāt avagamyate ata eva tad mithyā iti śakyate vaktum pramāṇa antarasya api tad viṣayasya asambhavāt  katham punar  pravṛtti nivṛtti anupayogi vastu na śabdāt avagamyate śabdasya tatra sāmarthya agrahaṇāt  na ca agṛhīta sāmarthya eva śabdaḥ cakṣuḥ ādivat vijñānam janayati sāmarthya grahaṇam ca jñāna kārya unneyam jñānam ca viśiṣṭa artha viṣayam tad viṣaya pravṛttyā avagamyate tad abhāve kutas  sāmarthya kalpanā syāt  aklṛpta sāmarthyaḥ ca śabdaḥ akriyā śeṣe arthe katham vijñānam janayet  ucyate na eva sūtrakāra bhāṣya kārayoḥ abhiprāyaḥ  laukikaḥ  vā nyāyaḥ samyak avagataḥ  bhavatā paśyatu bhavān devadatta   ‘gām abhyāja ‘śuklām daṇḍene ati pravartaka abhyājeti padā ati rekiṇām deva datta ādi bhūta artha vādinām apravartakānām api pravartakāt eva vākyāt bhūta vastu viṣayam api sāmarthyam pratīyate na vā iti pratīyate ced  niṣprayojana tvam ānarthakyam na nirālambana tvam tad āha bhāṣya kāraḥ api ca āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt ityādinā bhāṣyeṇa prayojanam ca anantaram pāramparyeṇa vā sukha avāptiḥ duḥkha parihāraḥ  vā syāt  atas tad artha kriyā anupayogi artha vācinām ‘saḥ arodīdi atyādi padānām bhavatu ānarthakyam brahma ātma tvā avagati samanvitānām tu parama puruṣa artha phalānām katham niṣprayojana tvam syāt etad  yadi api pravartakāt eva vākyāt bhūta artha viṣayam api sāmarthyam pratīyate tathā api na apratipanna bhūta artha avagateḥ sambhavaḥ kriyā artha tayā eva saṃsarga avagamāt  na hi gaḥ padāt tad arthaḥ sāsnādimad piṇḍa dharma tvena avagataḥ  vyutpatti kāle punar  prayoga antareṣu apratiṣṭhitaḥ kesara ādimad piṇḍa dharma tvena vā pratīyate viṣama upanyāsaḥ gopadasya abhidheya sambandhena nānāvidha sāmarthyam upalabdham atas  yukta eka rūpā eva pratītiḥ śabda antara artha anvaye punar  prativibhakti pratipadārtha antaram ca prayoga bhedāt anyathā anyathā ca sambandha grahaṇa kāla ā iva avāpa udvāpa nibandhanaḥ samanvayaḥ  dṛśyate tena dravya guṇa kriyā abhidhāyibhiḥ padaiḥ sambandha yogyatā abhidhāyi vibhakti saṃyuktaiḥ prayoga aidamparya vaśāt niyataḥ sambandhaḥ  vyutpatti kāle nirūpitaḥ tathā ca ‘vaṣaṭkartuḥ prathama bhakṣaḥ ‘tasmāt pūṣā prapiṣṭa bhāgaḥ iti evamādau kriyā śūnyānām samanvayaḥ  dṛśyate yaḥ tu kartavya iti kriyā sambandhaḥ sa samanvaya nimittaḥ  na tad nimittaḥ samanvayaḥ yad tu tad bhūtānām kriyā arthena samāmnāya iti sūtrayāmāsa jaiminiḥ tad api siddheṣu rūpa ādiṣu artheṣu vartamānānām sāmānādhikaraṇya ādi artha tvena samāmnāyaḥ samuccāraṇam iti yatas  darśitaḥ samanvayaḥ  viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvena api kriyā arthena iti tu dharma jijñāsā upakramāt prakṛta upayogi tayā sūcitam tathā ca bhāṣya kāraḥ api ‘dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam i atyartha sadbhāva mātre kathanīye karma avabodhanam iti prakṛta upayogi tvena eva uktavān tad etad āha bhāṣya kāraḥ yad api śāstra tātparya vidām anukramaṇam ityādi bhāṣyeṇa ata eva pūrveṇa tantreṇa āgata artha tvāt śārīraka ārambhaḥ tatra hi vedasya vivakṣita artha tvam svatas prāmāṇyam svarūpe ca vijñāna utpattau śabdasya sāmarthyam iti etad sarvam avagatam kriyā arthena samāmnāya iti tu dharma jijñāsā pratijña anusāreṇa sūtritam iha punar  ‘tattu samanvaya ādi ati viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyāt kam api gauṇam api sāmānādhikaraṇyam vihāya ekasmin niraṃśe ‘tattvam asī ati samanvayaḥ  mukhyaḥ pradarśitaḥ tathā ca bhagavān pāṇi niravyatirikte prātipadikā artha mātre prathamām smarati nāstikriyā kartari eva atirikte arthe tena ca kātyāyanasya ‘astiḥ bhavantī paraḥ iti matam na anumanyate dṛśyate ca ‘phalitā amī drumāḥ ‘rājñaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ iti asti kriyā śūnyaḥ samanvayaḥ na atra api ye phalita adrumāḥ te santi yaḥ  rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ saḥ asti iti vivakṣitam api tvete drumāḥ phalitāḥ ayam puruṣaḥ  rājña iti sambandha mātra avasitam vākyam evam sāmānyatas  siddhasya jagat kāraṇasya sarvajñatva ādi svabhāva tve tvam padārthasya ca brahma ātma tāyām samanvayaḥ  vedānta vākyānām siddhaḥ na tatra asti kriyāyāḥ  vastu svarūpa antar vartinyā api anupraveśaḥ  dūrata eva bāhyāyāḥ kiñca ‘brāhmaṇaḥ  na hantavyaḥ iti pratiṣedha vākya samanvaye na kriyā kriyā arthaḥ  vā avagamyate kintu kriyā nivṛttiḥ eva niyamena pratīyate vrata śabda samanvayāt tu prajāpati vrata ādiṣu ‘nekṣeta udyantam ādityam i atyādiṣu anīkṣaṇam mānasī saṅkalpa kriyā pratīyate anīkṣaṇam kuryāt  na īkṣe aham iti saṅkalpayet iti na nañaḥ samanvaya mātrāt tasya samanvīyamāna artha abhāva kara tvāt na ca svabhāva prāpta hanti artha anurāgeṇa ityādi bhāṣyasya ayam arthaḥ svabhāvata eva rāga ādi nimittāt śāstram antareṇa eva hanana kriyā prāptā yadi nañānurajyate viśeṣyate tadā bhavati ahananam iti tatas ca āhananam kuryāt iti vākya arthaḥ syāt  na ‘hananam na kuryādi ati hanana kriyā nivṛtti audāsīnyam atas  na hanyām iti mānasī saṅkalpa kriyā pūrva abhihitā syāt  na ca etad yuktam nañaḥ sambandhi upamarda rūpa tvāt anīkṣaṇe tu vrata śabda balāt tathā samanvayaḥ na nañaḥ sāmarthyāt iti uktam nanu nañarthe niyogaḥ pratiṣedheṣu tena yāga ādi anuṣṭhānāt iva nañartha anuṣṭhānāt niyogaḥ sādhyaḥ kim ucyate kriyā nivṛtti audāsīnyam pratīyata iti vārtam etad  nañarthaḥ  hi nāma na kriyā na api sādhanam api tu yena saṃsṛjyate tasya abhāvaḥ  na tad siddhi hetuḥ evam pratiṣedhasya vidheḥ anya tvam sidhyati anyathā vidhiḥ eva sarvam syāt  tasmāt  saṃsṛjyamāna abhāva mātre pratiṣedha vākyam paryavasyati tatra na vidhi gandhaḥ api vidyate tad ca saṃsṛjyamānam vidhi ni mantraṇā mantraṇa adhīṣṭa sampraśna abhyanujñānānām abhāvāt pratipādya dharmaḥ pratiṣidhyamāna kriyā phalam prārthanā pratiṣedha vākye liṅā ādi arthaḥ tena tad abhāvaḥ pratiṣedha arthaḥ sa ca prāc abhāvaḥ svabhāva siddhaḥ tasmāt saṃskāra udbodha nimitta sannidhau  api tad pratibandhe prayatna āstheyaḥ sa ca yadi api sādhyaḥ tathā api anvaya vyatireka gamyaḥ  na śabda arthaḥ tad pratipādaka pada abhāvāt ca eka vākye saṃsṛṣṭa padārtha vyatirekeṇa anyatra vākya arthatva abhāvāt ca atas  yaḥ ca arthāt arthaḥ  na sa codanā arthaḥ vākyantu kriyā śūnyam eva avasitam na sādhyam kiñcittena viṣayīkṛtam audāsīnya mātrau  asita tvāt tasya atha punar nañartha viṣayaḥ  niyoga eva pratiṣedhe api vākya artha iti abhiniveśaḥ bhavatu tathā api pratiṣidhyamāna kriyā nivṛttyā sa sidhyati kriyā upādāne ca tad phala prārthanā eva hetuḥ iti tad kāraṇa pratibandhe prayatna āsthānāt niyoga siddhiḥ tad ca anvaya vyatirekauvaseyam iti pūrva uktān mārgān na viśiṣyate tad evam vṛddha vyavahāra anusāreṇa eva samanvaya anusaraṇe sati tad gamyam brahma na dharmavat codana agamyam darśitāni ca vedānta vākyāni kāraṇa sāmānye siddhe tad viśeṣa avagamāya samanvitāni ‘yataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante ityādīni tad tvam asi ityādīni ca yad  punaruktam pratipanna brahma ātma bhāvasya api pūrvavat saṃsāritva darśanāt na rajju svarūpa kathanavat arthavat tvam asya samanvayasya tatas  na tanmātre tasya paryavasānam iti atra uttaram na avagata brahma ātma bhāvasya ityādi asya ayam arthaḥ na karma nimittaḥ tāvat śarīra sambandhaḥ itaretara āśraya doṣāt kriyā ādi rahita tvāt ca caitanyasya anādi tve api andha paramparāvat pratiṣṭhita tvāt  tad nimitta tve ca putra ādi śarīreṣu iva gauṇatva prasaṅgāt  tathā anubhava abhāvāt prasiddha gauṇatva prakāra asambhavāt putra ādi śarīreṇa iva sva śarīreṇa api pramātṛtva abhāva prasaṅgāt  pāriśeṣyāt avidyā nimittaḥ śarīra sambandhaḥ tasyām ca nivṛttāyām tad sambandha nivṛttau katham pūrvavattva nimittaḥ sukha duḥkha anubhavaḥ tathā ca śruti smṛti vādā brahma vidaḥ sarva saṃsāra pravṛtti abhāvam darśayanta udāhṛtā bhāṣye tasmāt na brahma ātma abhimāninaḥ pūrvavat saṃsāri tvam tad abhimāna virodhāt vaiṣayikaḥ tu sākṣāt anubhava abhimānaḥ saṃsāra viṣaya ārabdha karma śeṣa nimittaḥ timira nimitta dvi candravat manana nididhi āsanayoḥ na brahma avagati uttara kālīnatā kintu śravaṇavat avagati upāyatayā pūrva kālatā eva iti uktam adevam siddhasya vastunaḥ sva rūpa sattā mātreṇa apratipannasya pramāṇa viṣaya tayā prameya tvāt vidhīyamāna kriyā karma tve tu kāraka tvasya pramāṇa antara siddhi apekṣa tvāt tatas  siddhi anupapatteḥ vākya bheda prasaṅgāt pratyakṣa ādi virodhe devatā adhikaraṇa nyāya asiddheḥ vākya antara siddhasya karma kāraka tve caturvidhasya api karma kāryasya tatra asambhavāt  tad karmaka upāsanāt devatā karma yāga ādivat svarga upamaḥ  mokṣaḥ phalam kalpyeta tasya tadvat eva anityatva prasaṅgāt  ‘brahma veda brahmā eva bhavatī ati ādibhyaḥ  brahma vedana mokṣa phalayoḥ nirantaratva pratipādakebhyaḥ  vākyebhyaḥ arthāt antarāle kriyā anupraveśa nirākaraṇāt ‘tarati śokam ātma vidi ati ādi śrutibhyaḥ  mokṣa pratibandha nivṛtti mātrasya eva ātma jñāna phalasya darśita tvāt  sādhya antara abhāve kriyā anupapatteḥ brahma ātmā avagamasya ca mukhya aikya adhikaraṇasya sampad ā ādivat vikalpanā anupapatteḥ pramāṇa janyāyāḥ  api vidikriyāyaḥ karmatva niṣedhāt vidhīyamāna upāsti kriyā viṣaya tvasya dūra nirasta tvāt  vidikriyā viṣaya tve api samāropita nivartana mukhena nitya siddha caitanyasya brahma sva rūpa tā samarpaṇāt  vākya viṣayatva upapatteḥ sati api vā vidhi kriyā karma tve tasya ca vidhi anāyatta tvāt vidhi  chāyānām saṃstāvaka tvena āhārya tvāt saṃsāra nivṛtteḥ ca jñāna phalasya dṛṣṭa tvāt  atas  vidhi niḥ apekṣam svatantram eva brahma śāstra pramāṇakam vedānta vākya samanvayāt iti siddham evam ca sati padānām paraspara samanvaya janita vijñāna atirekeṇa cakṣuḥ ādivat pravartaka tvasya abhāvāt  tad viṣayaḥ śāstra ārambhaḥ pṛthak upapadyate anyathā atrā api bodhakatva atirekeṇa pravartaka tvam api ced  ‘atha atas  dharma jijñāse ati eva ārabdha tvāt na pṛthak ārabhyeta atha api abahis sādhana tvāt tatas  pariśeṣitam iti tathā api atha atas  pariśiṣṭa dharma jijñāsā iti pratijñā syāt  pravartaka viśeṣa jijñāsanāt  tad evam brahma avagamāt  prāk eva vidhi vidheya pramāṇa prameya vyavahāraḥ paratas tu pramātuḥ vidhi viṣayasya ca abhāvāt na tad sadbhāva iti apicāhuḥ iti prasiddham etad  brahma vidām iti pūrva uktam nyāyam saṅkṣepataḥ ślokaiḥ saṅgṛhṇāti gauṇa mithyā ātmana iti gauṇaḥ ahaṃmānaḥ  mamatvena sambandhāt putra dāra ādau atas  sa gauṇa ātmā mithyā dehāt ārabhya ahaṅka rtuḥ idam aṃśa paryantaḥ ahaṃmānaḥ  na ātmani ātma abhimānāt  atas  sa mithyā ātmā tasya ubhayasya api ātmanaḥ  mukhya parama artha brahma ātmā avagamena tad ādhāra putra deha ādi bādhanāt asattvam tad nimittam śāstrī iyam niyojya tvam śārīram ca bhoktṛ tvam nimitta abhāvāt na kathañcid udbhavet iti arthaḥ tad etad draḍhayan  āha anveṣṭa vyātmā iti ‘saḥ anveṣṭavyaḥ ityādi upakrameṇa upadiṣṭa apāstā aśeṣa saṃsāra rūpa brahma ātmā avagamāt prāk eva pramātṛtva abhimānaḥ pratyakciteḥ yadā punar tad rūpam vismṛta suvarṇavat avāptam tadā sa eva pramātṛtva abhimataḥ  nirasta saṃsāra doṣaḥ sampannaḥ kutas tasya kartṛtva bhoktṛ tve bhavataḥ yadi ayam aham ullekha pramukha pramātṛtva ādi vyavahāraḥ kalpitaḥ katham idānīm asya prāmāṇyam iti āśaṅkya āha deha ātma pratyaya iti yathā dehe viśiṣṭa jātīye tad vyatiriktasya ahaṅkartuḥ ahaṃmāna sambandhaḥ kalpitaḥ api sva nibandhane lokaśāstra vyavahāre yathā avagati tattva hetuḥ tathā ayam kalpitaḥ api alaukika ātma svarūpa pratipatteḥ prāk  pramāṇam niścita pratyaya utpādanāt bādha anupalabdheḥ ca iti iti paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ādi śrī śaṅkara bhagavat pāda antevāsi vara śrī padma pāda ācārya kṛtau pañcapādikāyām vedāntānām brahmaṇi samanvayanirūpaṇam nāma navamam varṇakam samāptam
